};

function byId(id) { try { return document.getElementById(id); } catch(e) { return null; } }
function safeHTML(el, html) { if (!el) return; try { el.innerHTML = html; } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); } }
function safeText(el, text) { if (!el) return; try { el.innerText = text; } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); } }

function showLoader(title) {
    title = title || 'جاري التحميل...';
    try { Swal.fire({ title: title, allowOutsideClick: false, didOpen: function() { Swal.showLoading(); } }); } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); }
}
function hideLoader() { try { Swal.close(); } catch(e) {} }
function showToast(message, type) {
    type = type || 'success';
    try { Swal.fire({ title: message, icon: type, timer: 2000, showConfirmButton: false }); } catch(e) { alert(message); }
}
// ============================================================
// دالة توليد Base64 لنص QR Code الفاتورة (متوافقة مع ZATCA)
// ============================================================
function generateQRInvoiceBase64(sellerName, vatNumber, invoiceDate, totalAmount, vatAmount) {
    var text = '';
    text += (sellerName || '') + '\n';
    text += (vatNumber || '') + '\n';
    text += (invoiceDate || '') + '\n';
    text += (totalAmount || '') + '\n';
    text += (vatAmount || '');
    var utf8Bytes = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {
        var charCode = text.charCodeAt(i);
        if (charCode < 0x80) {
            utf8Bytes.push(charCode);
        } else if (charCode < 0x800) {
            utf8Bytes.push(0xc0 | (charCode >> 6));
            utf8Bytes.push(0x80 | (charCode & 0x3f));
        } else if (charCode < 0xd800 || charCode >= 0xe000) {
            utf8Bytes.push(0xe0 | (charCode >> 12));
            utf8Bytes.push(0x80 | ((charCode >> 6) & 0x3f));
            utf8Bytes.push(0x80 | (charCode & 0x3f));
        } else {
            i++;
            charCode = 0x10000 + (((charCode & 0x3ff) << 10) | (text.charCodeAt(i) & 0x3ff));
            utf8Bytes.push(0xf0 | (charCode >> 18));
            utf8Bytes.push(0x80 | ((charCode >> 12) & 0x3f));
            utf8Bytes.push(0x80 | ((charCode >> 6) & 0x3f));
            utf8Bytes.push(0x80 | (charCode & 0x3f));
        }
    }
    var binary = '';
    for (var j = 0; j < utf8Bytes.length; j++) {
        binary += String.fromCharCode(utf8Bytes[j]);
    }
    return btoa(binary);
}

var RW_Server = {
    exists: function() { return (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run); },
    call: function(functionName, args) {
        args = args || [];
        var self = this;
        return new Promise(function(resolve) {
            if (!self.exists()) { RW_LOG.warn('Apps Script غير متاح'); resolve({ status: 'offline', data: null }); return; }
            try {
                var runner = google.script.run;
                runner = runner.withSuccessHandler(function(res) { resolve(res || { status: 'success' }); });
                runner = runner.withFailureHandler(function(err) { RW_LOG.error(err); resolve({ status: 'error', msg: (err && err.message) ? err.message : 'Server Error' }); });
                if (typeof runner[functionName] === 'function') { runner[functionName].apply(null, args); }
                else { resolve({ status: 'missing_function' }); }
            } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); resolve({ status: 'exception', msg: e.message }); }
        });
    }
};

var RW_Data = {
    loadInitialData: function() {
        var self = this;
        return RW_Server.call('getInitialData', [RW_STATE.app.currentUser ? RW_STATE.app.currentUser.email : '']).then(function(res) {
            if (res && res.status === 'success') {
                RW_STATE.data.items = res.items || [];
                RW_STATE.data.customers = res.customers || [];
                RW_STATE.data.suppliers = res.suppliers || [];
                RW_STATE.data.orders = res.orders || [];
                RW_STATE.data.runsheets = res.runsheets || [];
                RW_STATE.data.employees = res.employees || [];
                RW_STATE.data.branches = res.branches || [];
                // ✅ الأسطر الثلاثة الجديدة فقط:
                RW_STATE.data._treasury = res.treasury || [];
                RW_STATE.data._accountsTree = res.accountsTree || [];
                RW_STATE.data._accountsFlat = res.accountsFlat || [];
                RW_STATE.data._loadedAll = true;
            } else { self.loadFallbackData(); }
        }).catch(function(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); self.loadFallbackData(); });
    },
    loadFallbackData: function() {
        RW_LOG.warn('تشغيل البيانات الوهمية');
        RW_STATE.data.items = [{ code: 'ITM001', name: 'منتج تجريبي', cat: 'عام', unit: 'قطعة', stock: 50, sPrice: 100 }];
        RW_STATE.data.customers = [];
        RW_STATE.data.suppliers = [];
        RW_STATE.data.orders = [];
        RW_STATE.data.runsheets = [];
    },
    refresh: function() {
        var self = this;
        return this.loadInitialData().then(function() {
            try { if (RW_STATE.app.currentView === 'items') RW_Items.render(); if (RW_STATE.app.currentView === 'dashboard') RW_Dashboard.render(); } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); }
        });
    }
};

var RW_Auth = {
    login: function(username, password) {
        if (!username || !password) { showToast('يرجى إدخال اسم المستخدم وكلمة المرور', 'error'); return; }
        showLoader();
        var self = this;
        RW_Server.call('handleLogin', [username, password]).then(function(res) {
            hideLoader();
            if (res && res.status !== 'success' && res.status !== 'offline' && res.status !== 'missing_function') { showToast((res && res.msg) ? res.msg : 'فشل تسجيل الدخول', 'error'); return; }
            RW_STATE.app.authenticated = true;
            RW_STATE.app.currentUser = (res && res.user) ? res.user : { name: username, role: 'مدير النظام', email: username };
            RW_STATE.permissions = (res && res.user && res.user.permissions) ? res.user.permissions : [];
            if (res && res.company) {
                RW_STATE.app.company = res.company;
                safeText(byId('rw-sidebar-company-name'), res.company.name || 'الروائع ERP');
                var logoImg = byId('rw-sidebar-brand-logo');
                if (logoImg && res.company.logo) {
                    logoImg.src = res.company.logo;
                    logoImg.style.objectFit = 'contain';
                    logoImg.style.backgroundColor = '#f8fafc';
                }
            }
            self.enterSystem();
        }).catch(function(e) { hideLoader(); RW_LOG.error(e); self.forceEnterFallback(); });
    },
    enterSystem: function() {
    try {
        byId('rw-login-page').style.display = 'none';
        byId('rw-main-shell').style.display = 'flex';
        
        var user = RW_STATE.app.currentUser;
        var userName = user ? (user.name || user.email) : 'مستخدم';
        var userRole = user ? (user.role || '') : '';
        var displayText = userName + (userRole ? ' (' + userRole + ')' : '');
        
        // تحديث القائمة الجانبية (إن وُجدت)
        safeText(byId('rw-sidebar-user-name'), userName);
        safeText(byId('rw-sidebar-user-role'), userRole);
        
        // تحديث العنصر الجديد في الهيدر
        safeText(byId('rw-header-user-display'), displayText);
        
        RW_Data.loadInitialData().then(function() {
            RW_Navigation.buildSidebar();
            RW_Navigation.navigate('dashboard');
        });
    } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); this.forceEnterFallback(); }
},
    forceEnterFallback: function() {
        try {
            hideLoader();
            byId('rw-login-page').style.display = 'none';
            byId('rw-main-shell').style.display = 'flex';
            RW_Data.loadFallbackData();
            RW_Navigation.buildSidebar();
            RW_Navigation.navigate('dashboard');
            showToast('تم تشغيل النظام في الوضع الآمن', 'warning');
        } catch(e) { document.body.innerHTML = '<div style="min-height:100vh;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;font-family:Cairo;background:#f3f6fb;"><h1>RAWAEA ERP</h1><p>حدث خطأ أثناء تشغيل النظام</p><button onclick="location.reload()">إعادة التحميل</button></div>'; }
    },
    logout: function() {
        try {
            RW_STATE.app.authenticated = false;
            byId('rw-main-shell').style.display = 'none';
            byId('rw-login-page').style.display = 'flex';
            var u = byId('rw-username'); if (u) u.value = '';
            var p = byId('rw-password'); if (p) p.value = '';
        } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); }
    }
};

_buildMenuHTML: function(items) {
    var html = '<ul style="list-style:none;padding:0;margin:0;">';
    items.forEach(function(item) {
        if (item.submenu) {
            html += '<li style="margin-bottom:4px;">';
            html += '<div class="rw-sidebar-link" style="justify-content:space-between;" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); var sub = this.nextElementSibling; if(sub) sub.style.display = sub.style.display === \'none\' ? \'block\' : \'none\';">';
            html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:16px;">';
            html += '<div class="rw-sidebar-link-icon"><i class="fa-solid ' + (item.icon || 'fa-folder') + '"></i></div>';
            html += '<div class="rw-sidebar-link-text">' + item.label + '</div>';
            html += '</div>';
            html += '<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-down" style="font-size:11px;color:#94a3b8;"></i>';
            html += '</div>';
            html += '<div style="display:none;padding-right:16px;" class="rw-sidebar-submenu">' + RW_Navigation._buildMenuHTML(item.submenu) + '</div>';
            html += '</li>';
        } else if (item.action) {
            html += '<li style="margin-bottom:4px;">';
            html += '<button class="rw-sidebar-link" onclick="RW_Navigation._handleAction(\'' + item.action + '\', \'' + (item.arg || '') + '\')">';
            html += '<div class="rw-sidebar-link-icon"><i class="fa-solid ' + (item.icon || 'fa-cog') + '"></i></div>';
            html += '<div class="rw-sidebar-link-text">' + item.label + '</div>';
            html += '</button>';
            html += '</li>';
        } else {
            var view = item.view || '';
            html += '<li style="margin-bottom:4px;">';
            html += '<button class="rw-sidebar-link" data-view="' + view + '">';
            html += '<div class="rw-sidebar-link-icon"><i class="fa-solid ' + (item.icon || 'fa-file') + '"></i></div>';
            html += '<div class="rw-sidebar-link-text">' + item.label + '</div>';
            html += '</button>';
            html += '</li>';
        }
    });
    html += '</ul>';
    return html;
},

_handleAction: function(action, arg) {
    try {
        if (action === 'showFinanceTab') {
            // تعيين التبويب الفرعي الافتراضي
            var targetTab = arg || 'treasury';
            
            // التحقق من أن RW_Finance موجود وجاهز
            if (typeof RW_Finance !== 'undefined' && typeof RW_Finance.renderSubTab === 'function') {
                // فتح التبويب المطلوب مباشرة
                RW_Finance.renderSubTab(targetTab);
                // تحديث عنوان الهيدر ليتوافق مع التبويب المالي
                var financeTabs = {
                    'treasury': 'الخزائن والبنوك',
                    'accounts': 'دليل الحسابات',
                    'journal': 'قيود يومية',
                    'receipts': 'سندات القبض',
                    'payments': 'سندات الصرف',
                    'transfers': 'التحويلات',
                    'reports': 'التقارير المالية'
                };
                var headerTitle = financeTabs[targetTab] || 'الحسابات والمالية';
                safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), headerTitle);
                safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'إدارة الحسابات والمالية');
                // تحديث حالة العرض الحالية
                RW_STATE.app.currentView = 'finance';
            } else {
                if (typeof showToast === 'function') {
                    showToast('وحدة المالية غير محملة بشكل صحيح', 'error');
                }
            }
            return;
        }
        // التوجيه للتبويبات الأخرى
        if (typeof RW_Views !== 'undefined' && RW_Views.render) {
            RW_Views.render(action);
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.error('Navigation error:', e);
    }
},

    buildSidebar: function() {
        try {
            var nav = byId('rw-sidebar-nav');
            if (!nav) return;

            var perms = RW_STATE.permissions || [];
            var hasFullAccess = (perms.indexOf('*') !== -1);

            function isAllowed(item) {
                if (hasFullAccess) return true;
                if (item.perm === 'owner') { return RW_STATE.app.currentUser && RW_STATE.app.currentUser.isOwner === true; }
                if (item.perm) return perms.indexOf(item.perm) !== -1;
                if (item.view) return perms.indexOf(item.view) !== -1;
                return true;
            }

            function filterMenu(items) {
                var filtered = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                    var item = items[i];
                    if (!isAllowed(item)) continue;
                    if (item.submenu) {
                        var filteredSub = filterMenu(item.submenu);
                        if (filteredSub.length === 0) continue;
                        var newItem = {}; for (var k in item) newItem[k] = item[k];
                        newItem.submenu = filteredSub;
                        filtered.push(newItem);
                    } else { filtered.push(item); }
                }
                return filtered;
            }

            var filteredTree = filterMenu(this.menuTree);
            var menuHTML = this._buildMenuHTML(filteredTree);
            safeHTML(nav, menuHTML);

            nav.querySelectorAll('.rw-sidebar-link[data-view]').forEach(function(btn) {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    var view = btn.dataset.view;
                    if (view) { RW_Navigation.navigate(view); }
                });
            });
        } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error('فشل بناء القائمة الجانبية', e); }
    },

    toggleSidebar: function() {
        var sidebar = byId('rw-sidebar');
        var mainContent = byId('rw-main-content');
        if (!sidebar || !mainContent) return;
        var collapsed = sidebar.classList.toggle('collapsed');
        if (collapsed) { mainContent.classList.add('expanded'); } else { mainContent.classList.remove('expanded'); }
        RW_STATE.ui.sidebarCollapsed = collapsed;
        try { localStorage.setItem('rw_sidebar_collapsed', collapsed ? '1' : '0'); } catch(e) {}
    },

    navigate: function(view) {
        try {
            RW_STATE.app.currentView = view;
            document.querySelectorAll('.rw-sidebar-link').forEach(function(el) { el.classList.remove('active'); });
            var activeBtn = document.querySelector('.rw-sidebar-link[data-view="' + view + '"]');
            if (activeBtn) activeBtn.classList.add('active');
            RW_Views.render(view);
        } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); showToast('حدث خطأ أثناء فتح الصفحة', 'error'); }
    }
};
window.RW_Navigation = RW_Navigation;

var RW_Views = {
    render: function(view) {
        try {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;
            switch (view) {
                case 'dashboard': RW_Dashboard.render(); break;
                case 'items':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الأصناف');
                    if (RW_STATE.data.items && RW_STATE.data.items.length > 0) { RW_Items.render(); }
                    else { showLoader('جاري تحميل الأصناف...'); google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) { hideLoader(); RW_STATE.data.items = data || []; RW_Items.render(); }).withFailureHandler(function() { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل تحميل الأصناف', 'error'); }).loadItemsData(1, 100); }
                    break;
                case 'customers':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'العملاء');
                    if (RW_STATE.data.customers && RW_STATE.data.customers.length > 0) { if (window.RW_Customers && window.RW_Customers.render) window.RW_Customers.render(); }
                    else { showLoader('جاري تحميل العملاء...'); google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) { hideLoader(); RW_STATE.data.customers = data || []; if (window.RW_Customers && window.RW_Customers.render) window.RW_Customers.render(); }).withFailureHandler(function() { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل تحميل العملاء', 'error'); }).loadCustomersData(1, 100); }
                    break;
                case 'branches':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'المخازن والفروع');
                    if (RW_STATE.data.branches && RW_STATE.data.branches.length > 0) { if (window.RW_Branches && window.RW_Branches.render) window.RW_Branches.render(); }
                    else { showLoader('جاري تحميل الفروع...'); google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) { hideLoader(); RW_STATE.data.branches = data || []; if (window.RW_Branches && window.RW_Branches.render) window.RW_Branches.render(); }).withFailureHandler(function() { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل تحميل الفروع', 'error'); }).loadBranchesData(1, 100); }
                    break;
                case 'suppliers':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الموردين');
                    if (RW_STATE.data.suppliers && RW_STATE.data.suppliers.length > 0) { if (window.RW_Suppliers && window.RW_Suppliers.render) window.RW_Suppliers.render(); }
                    else { showLoader('جاري تحميل الموردين...'); google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) { hideLoader(); RW_STATE.data.suppliers = data || []; if (window.RW_Suppliers && window.RW_Suppliers.render) window.RW_Suppliers.render(); }).withFailureHandler(function() { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل تحميل الموردين', 'error'); }).loadSuppliersData(1, 100); }
                    break;
                case 'users': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'المستخدمين والصلاحيات'); RW_Users.render(); break;
                case 'roles': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إدارة أدوار الموظفين'); RW_Roles.render(); break;
                case 'settings': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إعدادات النظام'); RW_Settings.render(); break;
                case 'reports':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التقارير الذكية');
                    if (window.RW_Reports && window.RW_Reports.renderDashboard) { RW_Reports.renderDashboard(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">التقارير الذكية</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'reports-dashboard':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'لوحة القيادة');
                    if (window.RW_Reports && window.RW_Reports.renderDashboard) { RW_Reports.renderDashboard(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">لوحة القيادة</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'reports-detailed':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التقارير التفصيلية');
                    if (window.RW_Reports && window.RW_Reports.renderDetailedReports) { RW_Reports.renderDetailedReports(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">التقارير التفصيلية</h2><div style="padding:20px">قيد التطوير</div></div>'); }
                    break;                case 'license': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إدارة الترخيص'); RW_OwnerLicense.render(); break;
                case 'orders':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'أوردرات المبيعات');
                    if (window.RW_Orders && window.RW_Orders.render) { RW_Orders.render(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">أوردرات المبيعات</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'runsheets':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الرانشيتات');
                    if (window.RW_Runsheets && window.RW_Runsheets.render) { RW_Runsheets.render(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">الرانشيتات</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'pos':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'نقطة البيع');
                    if (window.RW_POS && window.RW_POS.render) { RW_POS.render(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">نقطة البيع</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'online-store':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'المتجر الإلكتروني');
                    if (window.RW_OnlineStore && window.RW_OnlineStore.render) { RW_OnlineStore.render(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">المتجر الإلكتروني</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'purchases':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'أوردرات الشراء');
                    if (window.RW_Purchases && window.RW_Purchases.renderOrders) { window.RW_Purchases.renderOrders(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">أوردرات الشراء</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'purchase-pos':
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'نقطة شراء');
                    if (window.RW_Purchases && window.RW_Purchases.renderPOS) { window.RW_Purchases.renderPOS(); }
                    else { safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">نقطة شراء</h2><div style="padding:20px">جاري تحميل الوحدة...</div></div>'); }
                    break;
                case 'picking': 
                    safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التحضير'); 
                    RW_Warehouse.loadPicking(); 
                    break;
                case 'loading': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التحميل'); RW_Warehouse.loadLoading(); break;
                case 'delivery': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التوصيل'); RW_Warehouse.loadDelivery(); break;
                case 'return': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'المرتجعات'); RW_Warehouse.loadReturn(); break;
                case 'unloading': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التفريغ'); RW_Warehouse.loadUnloading(); break;
                case 'vouchers': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الأذونات المخزنية'); RW_Warehouse.loadVouchers(); break;
                case 'transfer': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'تحويل مخزني'); RW_Warehouse.loadVoucherForm('Transfer'); break;
                case 'direct-sale': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'صرف سيارة بيع مباشر'); RW_Warehouse.loadVoucherForm('DirectSale'); break;
                case 'direct-return': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'استلام مرتجع سيارة'); RW_Warehouse.loadVoucherForm('DirectReturn'); break;
                case 'supplier-return': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'مرتجع لمورد'); RW_Warehouse.loadVoucherForm('SupplierReturn'); break;
                case 'receiving': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الاستلام'); RW_Warehouse.loadReceiving(); break;
                case 'receiving': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الاستلام'); RW_Warehouse.loadReceiving(); break;
                case 'vehicle-count': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'جرد سيارة'); RW_Warehouse.loadVehicleCount(); break;
                case 'branch-count': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'جرد فرع'); RW_Warehouse.loadBranchCount(); break;
                case 'general-count': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'جرد عام'); RW_Warehouse.loadGeneralCount(); break;
                case 'settlement': safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إغلاق اليومية'); RW_Warehouse.loadSettlement(); break;
                case 'finance':
                    if (typeof RW_Finance !== 'undefined') { RW_Finance.render(); }
                    else { showToast('وحدة المالية غير محملة', 'error'); }
                    break;
                default: safeHTML(container, '<div class="rw-card"><h2 class="rw-card-title">' + view + '</h2><div style="padding:20px">الصفحة قيد التطوير</div></div>');
            }
        } catch(e) {
            console.error("🔥 RW_Views.render FATAL ERROR - View:", view);
            console.error("Message:", e.message);
            console.error("Stack:", e.stack);
            safeHTML(byId('rw-page-container'), '<div class="rw-card"><h2>خطأ في الصفحة</h2><pre>' + e.message + '\n' + (e.stack || '') + '</pre></div>');
        }
    }
};
var RW_Dashboard = {
    render: function() {
        try {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;
            var html = '<div class="rw-kpi-grid">' +
                '<div class="rw-kpi-card"><div class="rw-kpi-title">إجمالي المبيعات (شهرياً)</div><div class="rw-kpi-value" id="stat-sales">...</div></div>' +
                '<div class="rw-kpi-card"><div class="rw-kpi-title">قيمة المخزون</div><div class="rw-kpi-value" id="stat-stock">...</div></div>' +
                '<div class="rw-kpi-card"><div class="rw-kpi-title">أصناف نشطة / راكدة</div><div class="rw-kpi-value" id="stat-active-dormant">...</div></div>' +
                '<div class="rw-kpi-card"><div class="rw-kpi-title">أصناف منخفضة</div><div class="rw-kpi-value" id="stat-low-stock">...</div></div>' +
                '</div>' +
                '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6" id="quick-alerts"></div>' +
                '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">' +
                '<div class="rw-card"><div class="rw-card-title">أعلى 10 مبيعاً</div><div id="top-selling-table"></div></div>' +
                '<div class="rw-card"><div class="rw-card-title">أصناف راكدة</div><div id="dormant-items-table"></div></div>' +
                '</div>';
            safeHTML(container, html);
            if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(analytics) {
                    if (analytics && analytics.status === 'success') {
                        var stats = analytics.monthlyStats || {};
                        safeText(byId('stat-sales'), Number(stats.totalRevenue || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP');
                        safeText(byId('stat-stock'), Number(stats.totalStockValue || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP');
                        safeText(byId('stat-active-dormant'), (stats.activeItems || 0) + ' / ' + (stats.dormantCount || 0));
                        safeText(byId('stat-low-stock'), stats.lowStockCount || 0);
                    }
                }).getDashboardAnalytics();
            }
        } catch(e) { RW_LOG.error(e); }
    }
};

function sanitizeForAppsScript(obj) {
  if (obj === null || obj === undefined) return null;
  if (typeof obj !== 'object') return obj;
  if (obj instanceof Date) return obj.toISOString();
  if (obj.nodeType || typeof obj === 'function') return undefined;
  var cleanObj = Array.isArray(obj) ? [] : {};
  for (var key in obj) {
    if (!obj.hasOwnProperty(key)) continue;
    var val = obj[key];
    if (typeof val === 'undefined') { cleanObj[key] = null; }
    else if (typeof val === 'function') { continue; }
    else if (typeof val === 'object' && val !== null) { cleanObj[key] = sanitizeForAppsScript(val); }
    else { cleanObj[key] = val; }
  }
  return cleanObj;
}

window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE = [];
window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false;

function enqueueSync(job) { window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.push(job); processSyncQueue(); }

function processSyncQueue() {
  if (window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING) return;
  if (!window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.length) return;
  window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = true;
  var job = window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE[0];

  // --- الأصناف ---
  if (job.type === 'saveItem') {
    try {
      var safePayload = sanitizeForAppsScript(job.payload);
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
          window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();
          if (job.onSuccess) job.onSuccess(res);
          processSyncQueue();
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
          console.error("Apps Script Error:", err);
          window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();
          if (job.onFailure) job.onFailure(err);
          processSyncQueue();
        })
        .saveItem(safePayload);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("فشل تجهيز البيانات:", e);
      window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();
      if (job.onFailure) job.onFailure({ message: "بيانات غير صالحة للإرسال" });
      processSyncQueue();
    }

  } else if (job.type === 'deleteItem') {
    google.script.run
      .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
        window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();
        if (job.onSuccess) job.onSuccess(res);
        processSyncQueue();
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
        window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();
        if (job.onFailure) job.onFailure(err);
        processSyncQueue();
      })
      .deleteItem(job.payload);

  // --- الفروع ---
  } else if (job.type === 'saveBranch') {
    try {
      var safePayload = sanitizeForAppsScript(job.payload);
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
          window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();
          if (job.onSuccess) job.onSuccess(res);
          processSyncQueue();
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
          console.error("Branch Save Error:", err);
          window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();
          if (job.onFailure) job.onFailure(err);
          processSyncQueue();
        })
        .saveBranch(safePayload.branchId || null, safePayload.branchData);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("Queue saveBranch crash:", e);
      window.RW_SYNC_RUNNING = false; window.RW_SYNC_QUEUE.shift();

  // --- العملاء ---
  } else if (job.type === 'saveCustomer') {
    try {

      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {

  }
}
// ============================================================
// RW_Items – تبويب الأصناف (كامل)
// ============================================================
var RW_Items = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var sortField = 'code';
    var sortAsc = true;
    var categoriesList = [];


    function render() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الأصناف');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'عرض وإدارة جميع أصناف المخزون');
        safeHTML(container, buildMainHTML());
        bindMainEvents();
        
        // ✅ قراءة من الذاكرة أولاً (Bootstrap Data Pattern)
        if (RW_STATE.data._loadedAll && RW_STATE.data.items && RW_STATE.data.items.length > 0) {
            renderTable(RW_STATE.data.items);
            loadCategories();
        } else {
            // Fallback: تحميل من الخادم
            showLoader('جاري تحميل الأصناف...');
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    hideLoader();
                    RW_STATE.data.items = data || [];
                    renderTable(RW_STATE.data.items);
                    loadCategories();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function() {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل تحميل الأصناف', 'error');
                    renderTable([]);
                    loadCategories();
                })
                .loadItemsData(1, 500);
        }
    }

    function buildMainHTML() {
        var h = '<div class="flex flex-col" style="height:100%;">';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-wrap gap-3 mb-4">';
        h += '<input type="text" id="items-search" placeholder="🔍 بحث بالاسم، الكود، الباركود..." class="flex-1 min-w-[250px] p-3 bg-white rounded-xl border">';
        h += '<button id="btn-category" class="bg-slate-700 text-white px-5 py-3 rounded-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-layer-group ml-1"></i> تصنيف</button>';
        h += '<button id="btn-add-item" class="bg-blue-600 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-plus ml-1"></i> صنف جديد</button>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '<div class="flex-1 bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-y-auto" id="items-table-wrapper"></div>';
        h += '</div>';
        return h;
    }

    function bindMainEvents() {
        var s = byId('items-search');
        if (s) s.addEventListener('input', filterTable);
        var b = byId('btn-category');
        if (b) b.addEventListener('click', showCategoryModal);
        var a = byId('btn-add-item');
        if (a) a.addEventListener('click', function() { openItemModal(null); });
    }

    function loadCategories() {
    if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                categoriesList = [];
                if (res && Array.isArray(res)) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < res.length; i++) {
                        var nm = res[i].name || res[i].category_name || '';
                        if (nm) categoriesList.push(nm);
                    }
                }
                renderTable(RW_STATE.data.items || []);
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                RW_LOG.error('فشل تحميل التصنيفات: ' + err.message);
                categoriesList = ['عام', 'عصائر', 'حلويات'];
                renderTable(RW_STATE.data.items || []);
            })
            .getCategories();
    } else {
        categoriesList = ['عام', 'عصائر', 'حلويات'];
        renderTable(RW_STATE.data.items || []);
    }
}
    function renderTable(data) {
    var w = byId('items-table-wrapper');
    if (!w) return;
    if (!data || !data.length) {
        safeHTML(w, '<div class="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-gray-400 text-lg">لا توجد أصناف</div>');
        return;
    }
    var sorted = data.slice().sort(function(a, b) {
        var va = a[sortField] || '', vb = b[sortField] || '';
        if (sortField === 'stock' || sortField === 'sPrice' || sortField === 'maxQty') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
        else { va = String(va).toLowerCase(); vb = String(vb).toLowerCase(); }
        if (va < vb) return sortAsc ? -1 : 1;
        if (va > vb) return sortAsc ? 1 : -1;
        return 0;
    });
    var cols = [
        { field: 'name', label: 'المنتج' },
        { field: 'cat', label: 'التصنيف' },
        { field: 'unit', label: 'الوحدة' },
        { field: 'stock', label: 'المخزون' },
        { field: 'sPrice', label: 'السعر' },
        { field: 'maxQty', label: 'الأقصى' }
    ];
    var html = '';
    html += '<div class="flex-1 overflow-y-auto overflow-x-hidden h-full">';
    html += '<table class="w-full text-sm text-right border-collapse">';
    html += '<thead class="sticky top-0 bg-gray-50 z-10 shadow-[0_1px_2px_rgba(0,0,0,0.1)]"><tr>';
    for (var i = 0; i < cols.length; i++) {
        var col = cols[i];
        var icon = (sortField === col.field) ? (sortAsc ? 'fa-sort-up' : 'fa-sort-down') : 'fa-sort';
        html += '<th class="cursor-pointer p-4 font-bold text-gray-700 border-b" onclick="RW_Items._sortTable(\'' + col.field + '\')">' + col.label + ' <i class="fa-solid ' + icon + ' text-gray-400"></i></th>';
    }
    html += '</tr></thead><tbody class="divide-y divide-gray-100">';
    for (var j = 0; j < sorted.length; j++) {
        var item = sorted[j];
        var catDisplay = item.cat || '-';
        var img = item.image || 'https://via.placeholder.com/60';
        var stockWarn = (Number(item.stock) || 0) <= (Number(item.reorder) || 5) ? 'color:#ef4444;font-weight:bold;' : '';
        html += '<tr class="hover:bg-blue-50/50 transition-colors cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Items._openItemModal(\'' + (item.code || '') + '\')">';
        html += '<td class="p-4"><div class="flex items-center gap-3"><img src="' + img + '" class="w-12 h-12 rounded-lg object-cover border shadow-sm cursor-pointer" onclick="event.stopPropagation();RW_Items._viewImage(\'' + img + '\')"><span class="font-medium text-gray-900">' + (item.name || '') + '</span></div></td>';
        html += '<td class="p-4 text-gray-500">' + catDisplay + '</td>';
        html += '<td class="p-4 text-gray-500">' + (item.unit || '-') + '</td>';
        html += '<td class="p-4 font-bold" style="' + stockWarn + '">' + (item.stock || 0) + '</td>';
        html += '<td class="p-4 font-bold text-blue-600">' + Number(item.sPrice || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
        html += '<td class="p-4 text-gray-700">' + (item.maxQty || 'غير محدد') + '</td>';
        html += '</tr>';
    }
    html += '</tbody></table></div>';
    safeHTML(w, html);
}

    function filterTable() {
        var q = (byId('items-search') ? byId('items-search').value : '').toLowerCase();
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
        var filtered = items.filter(function(item) {
            return String(item.name || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1 ||
                String(item.code || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1 ||
                String(item.barcode || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1 ||
                String(item.cat || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1;
        });
        renderTable(filtered);
    }

    function _sortTable(field) {
        if (sortField === field) sortAsc = !sortAsc;
        else { sortField = field; sortAsc = true; }
        renderTable(RW_STATE.data.items || []);
    }

    function openItemModal(itemCode) {
    if (categoriesList.length === 0) {
        showLoader('جاري تحميل التصنيفات...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    categoriesList = [];
                    if (res && Array.isArray(res)) {
                        for (var i = 0; i < res.length; i++) {
                            var nm = res[i].name || res[i].category_name || '';
                            if (nm) categoriesList.push(nm);
                        }
                    }
                    hideLoader();
                    openItemModalAfterCategories(itemCode);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function() {
                    hideLoader();
                    openItemModalAfterCategories(itemCode);
                })
                .getCategories();
        } else {
            hideLoader();
            openItemModalAfterCategories(itemCode);
        }
        return;
    }
    openItemModalAfterCategories(itemCode);
}

    function openItemModalAfterCategories(itemCode) {
        var item = null;
        if (itemCode) {
            var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
            for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                if (items[i].code === itemCode) { item = items[i]; break; }
            }
        }
        var isEdit = !!item;
        var html = buildModalHTML(item, isEdit);
        Swal.fire({
            html: html,
            width: '1000px',
            showConfirmButton: false,
            showCancelButton: false,
            customClass: { popup: '!bg-transparent !shadow-none !p-0' },
            didOpen: function() { bindModalEvents(item, isEdit); }
        });
    }

    function buildModalHTML(item, isEdit) {
        item = item || {};
        var catOpts = '<option value="">اختر التصنيف</option>';
        for (var i = 0; i < categoriesList.length; i++) {
            var cn = categoriesList[i];
            var sel = (item.cat === cn) ? 'selected' : '';
            catOpts += '<option value="' + cn + '" ' + sel + '>' + cn + '</option>';
        }
        var title = isEdit ? 'تعديل الصنف' : 'إضافة صنف جديد';
        var h = '';
        h += '<div class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 z-50" dir="rtl">';
        h += '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-4xl overflow-hidden">';
        h += '<div class="bg-blue-600 px-6 py-4 flex justify-between text-white"><h3 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-box-open ml-2"></i>' + title + '</h3><button class="text-white/80 hover:text-white" onclick="Swal.close()"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark text-xl"></i></button></div>';
        h += '<form class="p-6 space-y-6" style="max-height:70vh;overflow-y:auto;">';
        h += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col items-center bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-xl border"><label class="text-sm font-bold w-full text-right">صورة المنتج</label><div class="w-48 h-48 rounded-xl border-2 border-dashed bg-white relative group mt-2"><img id="item-img-preview" src="' + (item.image || 'https://via.placeholder.com/200') + '" class="w-full h-full object-cover cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Items._viewImage(this.src)"><div class="absolute inset-0 bg-black/40 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer" onclick="document.getElementById(\'item-image-file\').click()"><span class="text-white text-sm">تغيير الصورة</span></div></div><input type="file" id="item-image-file" accept="image/*" class="mt-3 text-xs file:py-2 file:px-4 file:rounded-lg file:bg-blue-50 file:text-blue-700"></div>';
        h += '<div class="md:col-span-2 grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
        h += '<input type="hidden" id="item-code-hidden" value="' + (item.code || '') + '">';
        h += '<input type="hidden" id="item-existing-image" value="' + (item.image || '') + '">';
        h += fieldHTML('الباركود', 'item-barcode', item.barcode);
        h += fieldHTML('اسم المنتج *', 'item-name', item.name, 'required');
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold">التصنيف</label><select id="item-cat" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">' + catOpts + '</select></div>';
        h += fieldHTML('الوحدة الأساسية', 'item-unit', item.unit || 'حبة');
        h += fieldHTML('سعر البيع', 'item-price', item.sPrice || 0, 'number');
        h += fieldHTML('السعر القديم', 'item-oprice', item.oPrice || 0, 'number');
        h += fieldHTML('المخزون الافتتاحي', 'item-stock', item.stock || 0, 'number');
        h += fieldHTML('حد إعادة الطلب', 'item-reorder', item.reorder || 5, 'number');
        h += fieldHTML('الحد الأقصى', 'item-maxqty', item.maxQty || 0, 'number');
        h += fieldHTML('الوحدة البديلة', 'item-altunit', item.altUnit || '');
        h += fieldHTML('عدد الوحدات البديلة', 'item-altqty', item.altUnitQty || 0, 'number');
        h += '</div>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '<div class="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2"><input type="checkbox" id="item-show-in-store" ' + (item.show_in_store !== false ? 'checked' : '') + '><label class="text-sm font-bold">الظهور في المتجر الإلكتروني</label></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold">الوصف</label><textarea id="item-desc" rows="2" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">' + (item.desc || '') + '</textarea></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t">';
        if (isEdit) h += '<button type="button" id="btn-delete-item" class="px-5 py-2.5 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold mr-auto"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash ml-1"></i> حذف</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" class="px-5 py-2.5 border border-gray-300 rounded-xl font-bold" onclick="Swal.close()">إلغاء</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" id="btn-save-item" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold">حفظ</button>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '</form>';
        h += '</div></div>';
        return h;
    }

    function fieldHTML(label, id, value, type, extra) {
        type = type || 'text';
        extra = extra || '';
        return '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">' + label + '</label><input id="' + id + '" value="' + (value || '') + '" type="' + type + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm" ' + extra + '></div>';
    }

    function bindModalEvents(item, isEdit) {
        var fi = document.getElementById('item-image-file');
        if (fi) fi.addEventListener('change', function() {
            var p = document.getElementById('item-img-preview');
            if (!p || !this.files || !this.files[0]) return;
            var file = this.files[0];
            compressImage(file).then(function(compressed) {
                p.src = compressed;
                window._itemCompressedImage = compressed;
            });
        });
        var sb = document.getElementById('btn-save-item');
        if (sb) sb.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var data = gatherFormData();
            if (!data.name) { showToast('اسم المنتج مطلوب', 'error'); return; }
            Swal.close();
            saveItem(data);
        });
        if (isEdit) {
            var db = document.getElementById('btn-delete-item');
            if (db) db.addEventListener('click', function() {
                Swal.close();
                confirmDelete(item.code, item.name);
            });
        }
    }

    function gatherFormData() {
        var get = function(id, fb) { var e = document.getElementById(id); return e ? e.value : (fb || ''); };
        
        // معالجة show_in_store بدون ?.
        var showInStoreEl = document.getElementById('item-show-in-store');
        var showInStore = true; // القيمة الافتراضية
        if (showInStoreEl) {
            showInStore = showInStoreEl.checked !== false;
        }
        
        return {
            id: get('item-code-hidden'),
            item_code: get('item-code-hidden'),
            barcode: get('item-barcode'),
            name: get('item-name').trim(),
            category: get('item-cat'),
            unit: get('item-unit', 'حبة'),
            alt_unit: get('item-altunit'),
            alt_unit_qty: parseFloat(get('item-altqty', '0')) || 0,
            sales_price: parseFloat(get('item-price', '0')) || 0,
            old_price: parseFloat(get('item-oprice', '0')) || 0,
            cost_price: 0,
            weight_kg: 0,
            volume_m3: 0,
            reorder_point: parseFloat(get('item-reorder', '5')) || 5,
            max_qty: parseFloat(get('item-maxqty', '0')) || 0,
            description: get('item-desc'),
            image_url: get('item-existing-image'),
            is_active: true,
            show_in_store: showInStore
        };
    }

    function saveItem(data) {
    var cleanData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data));
    if (!cleanData.item_code) cleanData.item_code = 'ITM-' + Date.now();

    var doServerSave = function(imageUrl) {
        if (imageUrl) cleanData.image_url = imageUrl;
        enqueueSync({
            type: 'saveItem',
            payload: cleanData,
            onSuccess: function(res) {
                if (res && res.success) {
                    // تحديث محلي بعد نجاح الخادم
                    var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
                    var idx = -1;
                    for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) { if (items[i].code === cleanData.item_code) { idx = i; break; } }
                    if (idx >= 0) {
                        for (var k in cleanData) { if (cleanData.hasOwnProperty(k)) items[idx][k] = cleanData[k]; }
                        items[idx].cat = cleanData.category;
                    } else {
                        var newItem = {
                            code: cleanData.item_code,
                            name: cleanData.name,
                            barcode: cleanData.barcode,
                            cat: cleanData.category,
                            unit: cleanData.unit,
                            sPrice: cleanData.sales_price,
                            oPrice: cleanData.old_price,
                            stock: 0,
                            reorder: cleanData.reorder_point,
                            maxQty: cleanData.max_qty,
                            altUnit: cleanData.alt_unit,
                            altUnitQty: cleanData.alt_unit_qty,
                            weight: cleanData.weight_kg,
                            vol: cleanData.volume_m3,
                            desc: cleanData.description,
                            image: cleanData.image_url
                        };
                        items.unshift(newItem);
                    }
                    renderTable(items);
                    showToast('✅ تم الحفظ على الخادم', 'success');
                } else {
                    showToast('⚠️ الخادم: ' + (res ? res.message : 'فشل'), 'error');
                }
            },
            onFailure: function(err) {
                showToast('❌ فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
            }
        });
    };

    // معالجة الصورة (إن وجدت) ورفعها أولاً
    if (window._itemCompressedImage) {
        var compImg = window._itemCompressedImage;
        window._itemCompressedImage = null;
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(uploadRes) {
                if (uploadRes && uploadRes.url) {
                    doServerSave(uploadRes.url);
                } else {
                    doServerSave('');
                }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function() {
                doServerSave('');
            })
            .uploadImage(compImg, 'img_' + Date.now() + '.jpg');
    } else {
        doServerSave('');
    }
}

function confirmDelete(code, name) {
    Swal.fire({
        title: 'تأكيد الحذف',
        text: 'حذف "' + name + '"؟',
        icon: 'warning',
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonColor: '#ef4444',
        confirmButtonText: 'حذف',
        cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
    }).then(function(res) {
        if (!res.isConfirmed) return;
        showLoader('جاري الحذف...');
        var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ item_code: code });
        enqueueSync({
            type: 'deleteItem',
            payload: cleanPayload.item_code,
            onSuccess: function(r) {
                hideLoader();
                if (r && r.success) {
                    var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
                    var newItems = [];
                    for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) { if (items[i].code !== code) newItems.push(items[i]); }
                    RW_STATE.data.items = newItems;
                    renderTable(newItems);
                    showToast('✅ ' + (r.message || 'تم الحذف'), 'success');
                } else {
                    showToast('❌ ' + (r.message || 'فشل الحذف'), 'error');
                }
            },
            onFailure: function(err) {
                hideLoader();
                showToast('❌ فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
            }
        });
    });
}

    function showCategoryModal() {
        var listHTML = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < categoriesList.length; i++) {
            var cn = categoriesList[i];
            listHTML += '<div class="flex justify-between items-center py-2 px-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg mb-1"><span>' + cn + '</span><button class="text-red-500" onclick="RW_Items._deleteCategoryConfirm(\'' + cn + '\')"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></div>';
        }
        if (!listHTML) listHTML = '<div class="text-gray-400 py-4">لا توجد تصنيفات</div>';
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'إدارة التصنيفات',
            html: '<div class="text-right"><div class="max-h-60 overflow-y-auto mb-4">' + listHTML + '</div><div class="flex gap-2"><input id="new-cat-name" class="swal2-input flex-1" placeholder="اسم جديد"><button id="btn-add-cat" class="bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg">إضافة</button></div></div>',
            showCancelButton: true,
            cancelButtonText: 'إغلاق',
            showConfirmButton: false,
            didOpen: function() {
                var btn = document.getElementById('btn-add-cat');
                if (btn) btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    var nm = document.getElementById('new-cat-name').value.trim();
                    if (!nm) { showToast('أدخل اسماً', 'error'); return; }
                    Swal.close();
                    addCategory(nm);
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function addCategory(name) {
    google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
            if (res && res.status === 'success') {
                showToast('✅ ' + (res.msg || 'تمت الإضافة'), 'success');
                loadCategories();
            } else {
                showToast('❌ ' + ((res && res.msg) ? res.msg : 'فشل الحفظ'), 'error');
            }
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(err) { showToast('❌ فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
        .saveNewCategory(name);
}

function _deleteCategoryConfirm(catName) {
    Swal.fire({
        title: 'حذف التصنيف',
        text: 'حذف "' + catName + '"؟',
        icon: 'warning',
        showCancelButton: true,
        confirmButtonColor: '#ef4444',
        confirmButtonText: 'حذف',
        cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
    }).then(function(res) {
        if (!res.isConfirmed) return;
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                if (res && res.status === 'success') {
                    showToast('✅ ' + (res.msg || 'تم الحذف'), 'success');
                    loadCategories();
                } else {
                    showToast('❌ ' + ((res && res.msg) ? res.msg : 'فشل الحذف'), 'error');
                }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) { showToast('❌ فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
            .deleteCategory(catName);
    });
}

    function compressImage(file) {
        return new Promise(function(resolve) {
            var reader = new FileReader(); reader.readAsDataURL(file);
            reader.onload = function(e) {
                var img = new Image(); img.src = e.target.result;
                img.onload = function() {
                    var c = document.createElement('canvas');
                    c.width = Math.min(img.width, 800);
                    c.height = img.height * (c.width / img.width);
                    c.getContext('2d').drawImage(img, 0, 0, c.width, c.height);
                    resolve(c.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.7));
                };
            };
        });
    }

    function _viewImage(url) {
        Swal.fire({ imageUrl: url, showCloseButton: true, showConfirmButton: false, width: '800px', customClass: { popup: '!bg-transparent !shadow-none !p-0' } });
    }

    return {
        render: render,
        _sortTable: _sortTable,
        _viewImage: _viewImage,
        _openItemModal: openItemModal,
        _deleteCategoryConfirm: _deleteCategoryConfirm
    };
})();
window.RW_Items = RW_Items;
// ============================================================
// RW_Branches – تبويب الفروع (كود تلقائي غير قابل للتعديل)
// ============================================================
var RW_Branches = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var branchesData = [];
    var filterText = '';

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _generateBranchCode() {
        var maxNum = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < branchesData.length; i++) {
            var match = branchesData[i].branch_code && branchesData[i].branch_code.match(/BR-(\d+)/);
            if (match) {
                var num = parseInt(match[1], 10);
                if (num > maxNum) maxNum = num;
            }
        }
        return 'BR-' + (maxNum + 1);
    }

    function _renderTable() {
        var tbody = byId('branches-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;

        var filtered = branchesData.filter(function(branch) {
            if (!filterText) return true;
            var search = filterText.toLowerCase();
            return (branch.branch_code && branch.branch_code.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (branch.name && branch.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (branch.location && branch.location.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (branch.manager && branch.manager.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (branch.phone && branch.phone.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1);
        });

        if (filtered.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد فروع متطابقة</td></tr>');
            return;
        }

        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < filtered.length; i++) {
            var b = filtered[i];
            var isActive = (b.is_active === true || b.is_active === 1);
            var statusText = isActive ? 'نشط' : 'غير نشط';
            var statusClass = isActive ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-red-100 text-red-700';
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Branches._editBranch(\'' + _escapeHtml(b.branch_code) + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(b.branch_code || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(b.name || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(b.location || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(b.manager || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(b.phone || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ' + statusClass + '">' + statusText + '</span></td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _loadBranches() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    RW_STATE.data.branches = data || [];
                    branchesData = RW_STATE.data.branches;
                    _renderTable();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('branches-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">خطأ في التحميل</td></tr>');
                })
                .getBranches();
        } else {
            branchesData = [];
            _renderTable();
        }
    }

    function _editBranch(branchCode) {
        var branch = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < branchesData.length; i++) {
            if (branchesData[i].branch_code === branchCode) {
                branch = branchesData[i];
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!branch) {
            showToast('الفرع غير موجود', 'error');
            return;
        }
        _openModal(branch);
    }

    function _confirmDelete(branchCode) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف',
            text: 'هل أنت متأكد من حذف هذا الفرع؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            cancelButtonColor: '#3085d6',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، احذف',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ branch_code: branchCode });
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'deleteBranch',
                    payload: cleanPayload.branch_code,
                    onSuccess: function(res) {
                        if (res && res.success) {
                            showToast('تم حذف الفرع بنجاح', 'success');
                            _loadBranches();
                        } else {
                            showToast(res && res.message ? res.message : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الحذف', 'error');
                        }
                    },
                    onFailure: function(err) {
                        showToast('فشل الحذف: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function _buildModalHTML(branchData, generatedCode) {
        var isEdit = !!branchData;
        var title = isEdit ? 'تعديل الفرع' : 'إضافة فرع جديد';
        var codeValue = isEdit ? _escapeHtml(branchData.branch_code || '') : (generatedCode || '');
        var h = '';
        h += '<div class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 z-50" dir="rtl">';
        h += '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-2xl overflow-hidden">';
        h += '<div class="bg-indigo-600 px-6 py-4 flex justify-between text-white"><h3 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fas fa-store ml-2"></i>' + title + '</h3><button class="text-white/80 hover:text-white" onclick="Swal.close()"><i class="fas fa-xmark text-xl"></i></button></div>';
        h += '<form class="p-6 space-y-6" style="max-height:70vh;overflow-y:auto;">';
        h += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">كود الفرع</label><input id="branch-code" value="' + codeValue + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-100 border rounded-lg text-sm" readonly></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">اسم الفرع *</label><input id="branch-name" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(branchData.name || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الموقع / العنوان</label><input id="branch-location" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(branchData.location || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">المدير المسؤول</label><input id="branch-manager" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(branchData.manager || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">رقم الهاتف</label><input id="branch-phone" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(branchData.phone || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الحالة</label><select id="branch-status" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">';
        h += '<option value="active" ' + (!isEdit || (branchData.is_active === true || branchData.is_active === 1) ? 'selected' : '') + '>نشط</option>';
        h += '<option value="inactive" ' + (isEdit && (branchData.is_active === false || branchData.is_active === 0) ? 'selected' : '') + '>غير نشط</option>';
        h += '</select></div>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t border-gray-100">';
        if (isEdit) h += '<button type="button" id="btn-delete-branch" class="px-5 py-2.5 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold mr-auto"><i class="fas fa-trash-alt ml-1"></i> حذف</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" class="px-5 py-2.5 border border-gray-300 rounded-xl font-bold text-gray-700 bg-white hover:bg-gray-50" onclick="Swal.close()">إلغاء</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" id="btn-save-branch" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white rounded-xl font-bold shadow-md">حفظ</button>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '</form>';
        h += '</div></div>';
        return h;
    }

    function _openModal(branchData) {
        var isEdit = !!branchData;
        var generatedCode = isEdit ? null : _generateBranchCode();
        Swal.fire({
            html: _buildModalHTML(branchData, generatedCode),
            width: '800px',
            showConfirmButton: false,
            showCancelButton: false,
            customClass: { popup: '!bg-transparent !shadow-none !p-0' },
            didOpen: function() {
                var saveBtn = document.getElementById('btn-save-branch');
                if (saveBtn) {
                    saveBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        var codeInput = document.getElementById('branch-code');
                        var code = codeInput ? codeInput.value.trim() : '';
                        var name = document.getElementById('branch-name') ? document.getElementById('branch-name').value.trim() : '';
                        if (!name) { showToast('اسم الفرع مطلوب', 'error'); return; }
                        if (!code) { showToast('كود الفرع غير متاح', 'error'); return; }
                        var statusVal = document.getElementById('branch-status') ? document.getElementById('branch-status').value : 'active';
                        var branchObj = {
                            branch_code: code,
                            name: name,
                            location: document.getElementById('branch-location') ? document.getElementById('branch-location').value.trim() : '',
                            manager: document.getElementById('branch-manager') ? document.getElementById('branch-manager').value.trim() : '',
                            phone: document.getElementById('branch-phone') ? document.getElementById('branch-phone').value.trim() : '',
                            is_active: (statusVal === 'active')
                        };
                        Swal.close();
                        if (isEdit) {
                            var branchId = branchData.branch_code;
                            var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ branchId: branchId, branchData: branchObj });
                            enqueueSync({
                                type: 'saveBranch',
                                payload: cleanPayload,
                                onSuccess: function(res) {
                                    if (res && res.success) {
                                        showToast('تم تحديث الفرع بنجاح', 'success');
                                        _loadBranches();
                                    } else {
                                        showToast(res && res.message ? res.message : 'حدث خطأ أثناء التحديث', 'error');
                                    }
                                },
                                onFailure: function(err) { showToast('فشل تحديث الفرع: ' + err.message, 'error'); }
                            });
                        } else {
                            var cleanPayloadNew = sanitizeForAppsScript({ branchData: branchObj });
                            enqueueSync({
                                type: 'saveBranch',
                                payload: cleanPayloadNew,
                                onSuccess: function(res) {
                                    if (res && res.success) {
                                        showToast('تم إضافة الفرع بنجاح', 'success');
                                        _loadBranches();
                                    } else {
                                        showToast(res && res.message ? res.message : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الإضافة', 'error');
                                    }
                                },
                                onFailure: function(err) { showToast('فشل إضافة الفرع: ' + err.message, 'error'); }
                            });
                        }
                    });
                }
                if (isEdit) {
                    var deleteBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-branch');
                    if (deleteBtn) {
                        deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                            Swal.close();
                            _confirmDelete(branchData.branch_code);
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    return {
        _editBranch: _editBranch,
                render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;
            var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-6 gap-3"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fas fa-store ml-2"></i> الفروع والمخازن</h2><button id="add-branch-btn" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow transition"><i class="fas fa-plus ml-1"></i> إضافة فرع</button></div><div class="mb-4"><div class="relative"><i class="fas fa-search absolute right-3 top-3 text-gray-400"></i><input type="text" id="branch-search" placeholder="بحث بالكود أو الاسم أو الموقع..." class="w-full pr-10 p-2 border rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-400"></div></div><div class="overflow-x-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow"><table class="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الكود</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الاسم</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الموقع</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">المدير</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الهاتف</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الحالة</th></tr></thead><tbody id="branches-table-body"><tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>';
            safeHTML(container, html);
            var addBtn = byId('add-branch-btn');
            if (addBtn) { addBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { _openModal(null); }); }
            var searchInput = byId('branch-search');
            if (searchInput) { searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() { filterText = this.value; _renderTable(); }); }
            
            // تحميل البيانات من الخادم مباشرة ونسيان أي بيانات قديمة
            if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                        RW_STATE.data.branches = data || [];
                        branchesData = RW_STATE.data.branches;
                        _renderTable();
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        var tbody = byId('branches-table-body');
                        if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">خطأ في التحميل</td></tr>');
                    })
                    .getBranches();
            } else {
                branchesData = [];
                _renderTable();
            }
        }
    };
})();
window.RW_Branches = RW_Branches;
// ============================================================
// RW_Customers – تبويب العملاء (متوافق مع طابور المزامنة)
// ============================================================
var RW_Customers = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var customersData = [];
    var filterText = '';
    var sortField = 'code';
    var sortAsc = true;

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _generateCustomerCode() {
        var maxNum = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < customersData.length; i++) {
            var match = customersData[i].code && customersData[i].code.match(/CUST-(\d+)/);
            if (match) {
                var num = parseInt(match[1], 10);
                if (num > maxNum) maxNum = num;
            }
        }
        return 'CUST-' + (maxNum + 1);
    }

    function _renderTable() {
        var tbody = byId('customers-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;

        var filtered = customersData.filter(function(customer) {
            if (!filterText) return true;
            var search = filterText.toLowerCase();
            return (customer.code && customer.code.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (customer.name && customer.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (customer.phone && customer.phone.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (customer.area && customer.area.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (customer.contact && customer.contact.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1);
        });

        var sorted = filtered.slice().sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[sortField] || '', vb = b[sortField] || '';
            if (sortField === 'debt') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            else { va = String(va).toLowerCase(); vb = String(vb).toLowerCase(); }
            if (va < vb) return sortAsc ? -1 : 1;
            if (va > vb) return sortAsc ? 1 : -1;
            return 0;
        });

        if (sorted.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد عملاء متطابقة</td></tr>');
            return;
        }

        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < sorted.length; i++) {
            var c = sorted[i];
            var debtClass = Number(c.debt) > 0 ? 'text-red-500 font-bold' : 'text-green-600 font-bold';
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Customers._editCustomer(\'' + _escapeHtml(c.code) + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-mono">' + _escapeHtml(c.code || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(c.name || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(c.phone || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(c.area || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(c.contact || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(c.visitDay || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center ' + debtClass + '">' + Number(c.debt || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _loadCustomers() {
    if (RW_STATE.data.customers && RW_STATE.data.customers.length > 0) {
        customersData = RW_STATE.data.customers;
        _renderTable();
    } else {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    RW_STATE.data.customers = data || [];
                    customersData = RW_STATE.data.customers;
                    _renderTable();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('customers-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">خطأ في التحميل</td></tr>');
                })
                .getCustomersList();
        } else {
            customersData = [];
            _renderTable();
        }
    }
}

    function _editCustomer(customerCode) {
        var customer = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < customersData.length; i++) {
            if (customersData[i].code === customerCode) {
                customer = customersData[i];
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!customer) {
            showToast('العميل غير موجود', 'error');
            return;
        }
        _openModal(customer);
    }

    function _confirmDelete(customerCode) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف',
            text: 'هل أنت متأكد من حذف هذا العميل؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            cancelButtonColor: '#3085d6',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، احذف',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ customer_code: customerCode });
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'deleteCustomer',
                    payload: cleanPayload.customer_code,
                    onSuccess: function(res) {
                        if (res && res.success) {
                            showToast('تم حذف العميل بنجاح', 'success');
                            _loadCustomers();
                        } else {
                            showToast(res && res.message ? res.message : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الحذف', 'error');
                        }
                    },
                    onFailure: function(err) {
                        showToast('فشل الحذف: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function _buildModalHTML(customerData, generatedCode) {
        var isEdit = !!customerData;
        var title = isEdit ? 'تعديل العميل' : 'إضافة عميل جديد';
        var codeValue = isEdit ? _escapeHtml(customerData.code || '') : (generatedCode || '');
        var h = '';
