        h += '<div class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 z-50" dir="rtl">';
        h += '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-4xl overflow-hidden">';
        h += '<div class="bg-emerald-600 px-6 py-4 flex justify-between text-white"><h3 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fas fa-user-tie ml-2"></i>' + title + '</h3><button class="text-white/80 hover:text-white" onclick="Swal.close()"><i class="fas fa-xmark text-xl"></i></button></div>';
        h += '<form class="p-6 space-y-6" style="max-height:70vh;overflow-y:auto;">';
        h += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">كود العميل</label><input id="customer-code" value="' + codeValue + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-100 border rounded-lg text-sm" readonly></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">اسم العميل *</label><input id="customer-name" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(customerData.name || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">رقم الهاتف</label><input id="customer-phone" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(customerData.phone || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">المنطقة</label><input id="customer-area" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(customerData.area || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">العنوان التفصيلي</label><input id="customer-location" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(customerData.location || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">نوع العميل</label><select id="customer-type" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">';
        h += '<option value="عادي" ' + (!isEdit || customerData.type === 'عادي' ? 'selected' : '') + '>عادي</option>';
        h += '<option value="جملة" ' + (isEdit && customerData.type === 'جملة' ? 'selected' : '') + '>جملة</option>';
        h += '<option value="VIP" ' + (isEdit && customerData.type === 'VIP' ? 'selected' : '') + '>VIP</option>';
        h += '</select></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">طريقة الدفع</label><select id="customer-payment" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">';
        h += '<option value="نقدي" ' + (!isEdit || customerData.payment === 'نقدي' ? 'selected' : '') + '>نقدي</option>';
        h += '<option value="أجل" ' + (isEdit && customerData.payment === 'أجل' ? 'selected' : '') + '>أجل</option>';
        h += '</select></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الرصيد الحالي (EGP)</label><input id="customer-debt" value="' + (isEdit ? (customerData.debt || 0) : '0') + '" type="number" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">يوم الزيارة</label><select id="customer-visit" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">';
        h += '<option value="" ' + (!isEdit || !customerData.visitDay ? 'selected' : '') + '>اختر</option>';
        var days = ['السبت', 'الأحد', 'الإثنين', 'الثلاثاء', 'الأربعاء', 'الخميس'];
        for (var d = 0; d < days.length; d++) {
            h += '<option value="' + days[d] + '" ' + (isEdit && customerData.visitDay === days[d] ? 'selected' : '') + '>' + days[d] + '</option>';
        }
        h += '</select></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">مسؤول التواصل</label><input id="customer-contact" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(customerData.contact || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="md:col-span-2 flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">ملاحظات</label><textarea id="customer-notes" rows="2" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm">' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(customerData.notes || '') : '') + '</textarea></div>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t border-gray-100">';
        if (isEdit) h += '<button type="button" id="btn-delete-customer" class="px-5 py-2.5 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold mr-auto"><i class="fas fa-trash-alt ml-1"></i> حذف</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" class="px-5 py-2.5 border border-gray-300 rounded-xl font-bold text-gray-700 bg-white hover:bg-gray-50" onclick="Swal.close()">إلغاء</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" id="btn-save-customer" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-700 text-white rounded-xl font-bold shadow-md">حفظ</button>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '</form>';
        h += '</div></div>';
        return h;
    }

    function _openModal(customerData) {
        var isEdit = !!customerData;
        var generatedCode = isEdit ? null : _generateCustomerCode();
        Swal.fire({
            html: _buildModalHTML(customerData, generatedCode),
            width: '900px',
            showConfirmButton: false,
            showCancelButton: false,
            customClass: { popup: '!bg-transparent !shadow-none !p-0' },
            didOpen: function() {
                var saveBtn = document.getElementById('btn-save-customer');
                if (saveBtn) {
                    saveBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        var code = document.getElementById('customer-code') ? document.getElementById('customer-code').value.trim() : '';
                        var name = document.getElementById('customer-name') ? document.getElementById('customer-name').value.trim() : '';
                        if (!name) { showToast('اسم العميل مطلوب', 'error'); return; }
                        if (!code) { showToast('كود العميل غير متاح', 'error'); return; }
                        var customerObj = {
                            id: code,
                            code: code,
                            name: name,
                            phone: document.getElementById('customer-phone') ? document.getElementById('customer-phone').value.trim() : '',
                            area: document.getElementById('customer-area') ? document.getElementById('customer-area').value.trim() : '',
                            location: document.getElementById('customer-location') ? document.getElementById('customer-location').value.trim() : '',
                            type: document.getElementById('customer-type') ? document.getElementById('customer-type').value : 'عادي',
                            payment: document.getElementById('customer-payment') ? document.getElementById('customer-payment').value : 'نقدي',
                            debt: parseFloat(document.getElementById('customer-debt') ? document.getElementById('customer-debt').value : '0') || 0,
                            visitDay: document.getElementById('customer-visit') ? document.getElementById('customer-visit').value : '',
                            contact: document.getElementById('customer-contact') ? document.getElementById('customer-contact').value.trim() : '',
                            notes: document.getElementById('customer-notes') ? document.getElementById('customer-notes').value.trim() : ''
                        };
                        Swal.close();
                        var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ customerId: isEdit ? customerData.code : null, customerData: customerObj });
                        enqueueSync({
                            type: 'saveCustomer',
                            payload: cleanPayload,
                            onSuccess: function(res) {
                                if (res && res.success) {
                                    showToast(isEdit ? 'تم تحديث العميل بنجاح' : 'تم إضافة العميل بنجاح', 'success');
                                    _loadCustomers();
                                } else {
                                    showToast(res && res.message ? res.message : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الحفظ', 'error');
                                }
                            },
                            onFailure: function(err) { showToast('فشل الحفظ: ' + err.message, 'error'); }
                        });
                    });
                }
                if (isEdit) {
                    var deleteBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-customer');
                    if (deleteBtn) {
                        deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                            Swal.close();
                            _confirmDelete(customerData.code);
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    return {
        _editCustomer: _editCustomer,
        render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;
            var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-6 gap-3"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fas fa-user-tie ml-2"></i> العملاء</h2><button id="add-customer-btn" class="bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-700 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow transition"><i class="fas fa-plus ml-1"></i> عميل جديد</button></div><div class="mb-4"><div class="relative"><i class="fas fa-search absolute right-3 top-3 text-gray-400"></i><input type="text" id="customer-search" placeholder="بحث بالاسم أو الكود أو الهاتف أو المنطقة..." class="w-full pr-10 p-2 border rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-emerald-400"></div></div><div class="overflow-x-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow"><table class="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Customers._sortTable(\'code\')">الكود</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Customers._sortTable(\'name\')">الاسم</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الهاتف</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Customers._sortTable(\'area\')">المنطقة</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">مسؤول التواصل</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Customers._sortTable(\'visitDay\')">يوم الزيارة</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Customers._sortTable(\'debt\')">الرصيد</th></tr></thead><tbody id="customers-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>';
            safeHTML(container, html);
            var addBtn = byId('add-customer-btn');
            if (addBtn) { addBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { _openModal(null); }); }
            var searchInput = byId('customer-search');
            if (searchInput) { searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() { filterText = this.value; _renderTable(); }); }
            _loadCustomers();
        },
        _sortTable: function(field) {
            if (sortField === field) sortAsc = !sortAsc;
            else { sortField = field; sortAsc = true; }
            _renderTable();
        }
    };
})();
window.RW_Customers = RW_Customers;
// ============================================================
// RW_Suppliers – تبويب الموردين (متوافق مع طابور المزامنة)
// ============================================================
var RW_Suppliers = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var suppliersData = [];
    var filterText = '';
    var sortField = 'code';
    var sortAsc = true;

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _generateSupplierCode() {
        var maxNum = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < suppliersData.length; i++) {
            var match = suppliersData[i].code && suppliersData[i].code.match(/SUPP-(\d+)/);
            if (match) {
                var num = parseInt(match[1], 10);
                if (num > maxNum) maxNum = num;
            }
        }
        return 'SUPP-' + (maxNum + 1);
    }

    function _renderTable() {
        var tbody = byId('suppliers-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;

        var filtered = suppliersData.filter(function(supplier) {
            if (!filterText) return true;
            var search = filterText.toLowerCase();
            return (supplier.code && supplier.code.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (supplier.name && supplier.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (supplier.phone && supplier.phone.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (supplier.area && supplier.area.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1) ||
                   (supplier.contact && supplier.contact.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1);
        });

        var sorted = filtered.slice().sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[sortField] || '', vb = b[sortField] || '';
            if (sortField === 'balance') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            else { va = String(va).toLowerCase(); vb = String(vb).toLowerCase(); }
            if (va < vb) return sortAsc ? -1 : 1;
            if (va > vb) return sortAsc ? 1 : -1;
            return 0;
        });

        if (sorted.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد موردين متطابقة</td></tr>');
            return;
        }

        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < sorted.length; i++) {
            var s = sorted[i];
            var balanceClass = Number(s.balance) > 0 ? 'text-red-500 font-bold' : 'text-green-600 font-bold';
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Suppliers._editSupplier(\'' + _escapeHtml(s.code) + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-mono">' + _escapeHtml(s.code || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(s.name || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(s.phone || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(s.area || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(s.contact || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center ' + balanceClass + '">' + Number(s.balance || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _loadSuppliers(forceReload) {
    if (!forceReload && RW_STATE.data.suppliers && RW_STATE.data.suppliers.length > 0) {
        suppliersData = RW_STATE.data.suppliers;
        _renderTable();
    } else {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    RW_STATE.data.suppliers = data || [];
                    suppliersData = RW_STATE.data.suppliers;
                    _renderTable();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('suppliers-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">خطأ في التحميل</td></tr>');
                })
                .getSuppliersList();
        } else {
            suppliersData = [];
            _renderTable();
        }
    }
}

    function _editSupplier(supplierCode) {
        var supplier = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < suppliersData.length; i++) {
            if (suppliersData[i].code === supplierCode) {
                supplier = suppliersData[i];
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!supplier) {
            showToast('المورد غير موجود', 'error');
            return;
        }
        _openModal(supplier);
    }

    function _confirmDelete(supplierCode) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف',
            text: 'هل أنت متأكد من حذف هذا المورد؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            cancelButtonColor: '#3085d6',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، احذف',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ supplier_code: supplierCode });
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'deleteSupplier',
                    payload: cleanPayload.supplier_code,
                    onSuccess: function(res) {
                        if (res && res.success) {
                            showToast('تم حذف المورد بنجاح', 'success');
                            _loadSuppliers(true)();
                        } else {
                            showToast(res && res.message ? res.message : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الحذف', 'error');
                        }
                    },
                    onFailure: function(err) {
                        showToast('فشل الحذف: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function _buildModalHTML(supplierData, generatedCode) {
        var isEdit = !!supplierData;
        var title = isEdit ? 'تعديل المورد' : 'إضافة مورد جديد';
        var codeValue = isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.code || '') : (generatedCode || '');
        var h = '';
        h += '<div class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 z-50" dir="rtl">';
        h += '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-4xl overflow-hidden">';
        h += '<div class="bg-orange-600 px-6 py-4 flex justify-between text-white"><h3 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fas fa-truck ml-2"></i>' + title + '</h3><button class="text-white/80 hover:text-white" onclick="Swal.close()"><i class="fas fa-xmark text-xl"></i></button></div>';
        h += '<form class="p-6 space-y-6" style="max-height:70vh;overflow-y:auto;">';
        h += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">كود المورد</label><input id="supplier-code" value="' + codeValue + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-100 border rounded-lg text-sm" readonly></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">اسم المورد *</label><input id="supplier-name" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.name || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">رقم الهاتف</label><input id="supplier-phone" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.phone || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">المنطقة</label><input id="supplier-area" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.area || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">العنوان التفصيلي</label><input id="supplier-address" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.address || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">نوع المورد</label><select id="supplier-type" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">';
        h += '<option value="مورد عام" ' + (!isEdit || supplierData.type === 'مورد عام' ? 'selected' : '') + '>مورد عام</option>';
        h += '<option value="مصنع" ' + (isEdit && supplierData.type === 'مصنع' ? 'selected' : '') + '>مصنع</option>';
        h += '<option value="مورد خارجي" ' + (isEdit && supplierData.type === 'مورد خارجي' ? 'selected' : '') + '>مورد خارجي</option>';
        h += '</select></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">طريقة الدفع</label><select id="supplier-payment" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">';
        h += '<option value="نقدي" ' + (!isEdit || supplierData.payment === 'نقدي' ? 'selected' : '') + '>نقدي</option>';
        h += '<option value="أجل" ' + (isEdit && supplierData.payment === 'أجل' ? 'selected' : '') + '>أجل</option>';
        h += '</select></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الرصيد الحالي (EGP)</label><input id="supplier-balance" value="' + (isEdit ? (supplierData.balance || 0) : '0') + '" type="number" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">جهة الاتصال</label><input id="supplier-contact" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.contact || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">مسؤول المشتريات</label><input id="supplier-rep" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.rep || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm"></div>';
        h += '<div class="md:col-span-2 flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">ملاحظات</label><textarea id="supplier-notes" rows="2" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm">' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(supplierData.notes || '') : '') + '</textarea></div>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t border-gray-100">';
        if (isEdit) h += '<button type="button" id="btn-delete-supplier" class="px-5 py-2.5 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold mr-auto"><i class="fas fa-trash-alt ml-1"></i> حذف</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" class="px-5 py-2.5 border border-gray-300 rounded-xl font-bold text-gray-700 bg-white hover:bg-gray-50" onclick="Swal.close()">إلغاء</button>';
        h += '<button type="button" id="btn-save-supplier" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-orange-600 hover:bg-orange-700 text-white rounded-xl font-bold shadow-md">حفظ</button>';
        h += '</div>';
        h += '</form>';
        h += '</div></div>';
        return h;
    }

    function _openModal(supplierData) {
        var isEdit = !!supplierData;
        var generatedCode = isEdit ? null : _generateSupplierCode();
        Swal.fire({
            html: _buildModalHTML(supplierData, generatedCode),
            width: '900px',
            showConfirmButton: false,
            showCancelButton: false,
            customClass: { popup: '!bg-transparent !shadow-none !p-0' },
            didOpen: function() {
                var saveBtn = document.getElementById('btn-save-supplier');
                if (saveBtn) {
                    saveBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        var code = document.getElementById('supplier-code') ? document.getElementById('supplier-code').value.trim() : '';
                        var name = document.getElementById('supplier-name') ? document.getElementById('supplier-name').value.trim() : '';
                        if (!name) { showToast('اسم المورد مطلوب', 'error'); return; }
                        if (!code) { showToast('كود المورد غير متاح', 'error'); return; }
                        var supplierObj = {
                            id: code,
                            code: code,
                            name: name,
                            phone: document.getElementById('supplier-phone') ? document.getElementById('supplier-phone').value.trim() : '',
                            area: document.getElementById('supplier-area') ? document.getElementById('supplier-area').value.trim() : '',
                            address: document.getElementById('supplier-address') ? document.getElementById('supplier-address').value.trim() : '',
                            type: document.getElementById('supplier-type') ? document.getElementById('supplier-type').value : 'مورد عام',
                            payment: document.getElementById('supplier-payment') ? document.getElementById('supplier-payment').value : 'نقدي',
                            balance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('supplier-balance') ? document.getElementById('supplier-balance').value : '0') || 0,
                            contact: document.getElementById('supplier-contact') ? document.getElementById('supplier-contact').value.trim() : '',
                            rep: document.getElementById('supplier-rep') ? document.getElementById('supplier-rep').value.trim() : '',
                            notes: document.getElementById('supplier-notes') ? document.getElementById('supplier-notes').value.trim() : ''
                        };
                        Swal.close();
                        var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ supplierId: isEdit ? supplierData.code : null, supplierData: supplierObj });
                        enqueueSync({
                            type: 'saveSupplier',
                            payload: cleanPayload,
                            onSuccess: function(res) {
                                if (res && res.success) {
                                    showToast(isEdit ? 'تم تحديث المورد بنجاح' : 'تم إضافة المورد بنجاح', 'success');
                                    _loadSuppliers(true)();
                                } else {
                                    showToast(res && res.message ? res.message : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الحفظ', 'error');
                                }
                            },
                            onFailure: function(err) { showToast('فشل الحفظ: ' + err.message, 'error'); }
                        });
                    });
                }
                if (isEdit) {
                    var deleteBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-supplier');
                    if (deleteBtn) {
                        deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                            Swal.close();
                            _confirmDelete(supplierData.code);
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    return {
        _editSupplier: _editSupplier,
        render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;
            var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-6 gap-3"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fas fa-truck ml-2"></i> الموردين</h2><button id="add-supplier-btn" class="bg-orange-600 hover:bg-orange-700 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow transition"><i class="fas fa-plus ml-1"></i> مورد جديد</button></div><div class="mb-4"><div class="relative"><i class="fas fa-search absolute right-3 top-3 text-gray-400"></i><input type="text" id="supplier-search" placeholder="بحث بالاسم أو الكود أو الهاتف أو المنطقة..." class="w-full pr-10 p-2 border rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-orange-400"></div></div><div class="overflow-x-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow"><table class="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Suppliers._sortTable(\'code\')">الكود</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Suppliers._sortTable(\'name\')">الاسم</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الهاتف</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Suppliers._sortTable(\'area\')">المنطقة</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">جهة الاتصال</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Suppliers._sortTable(\'balance\')">الرصيد</th></tr></thead><tbody id="suppliers-table-body"><tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>';
            safeHTML(container, html);
            var addBtn = byId('add-supplier-btn');
            if (addBtn) { addBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { _openModal(null); }); }
            var searchInput = byId('supplier-search');
            if (searchInput) { searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() { filterText = this.value; _renderTable(); }); }
            _loadSuppliers();
        },
        _sortTable: function(field) {
            if (sortField === field) sortAsc = !sortAsc;
            else { sortField = field; sortAsc = true; }
            _renderTable();
        }
    };
})();
window.RW_Suppliers = RW_Suppliers;
// ============================================================
// RW_Purchases – تبويب المشتريات (محسّن مع Lazy Loading)
// ============================================================
var RW_Purchases = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var purchaseOrdersData = [];
    var purchaseCart = [];

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) { if (m === '&') return '&amp;'; if (m === '<') return '&lt;'; if (m === '>') return '&gt;'; return m; });
    }

    // تحميل الأصناف والموردين تلقائياً عند فتح التبويب لأول مرة
    function _ensureDataAndRender(renderFunc) {
        var itemsLoaded = (RW_STATE.data.items && RW_STATE.data.items.length > 0);
        var suppliersLoaded = (RW_STATE.data.suppliers && RW_STATE.data.suppliers.length > 0);
        if (itemsLoaded && suppliersLoaded) { renderFunc(); return; }
        showLoader('جاري تحميل البيانات الأساسية...');
        var pending = 0;
        function done() { pending--; if (pending <= 0) { hideLoader(); renderFunc(); } }
        if (!itemsLoaded) { pending++; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) { RW_STATE.data.items = data || []; done(); }).withFailureHandler(function() { done(); }).loadItemsData(1, 500); }
        if (!suppliersLoaded) { pending++; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) { RW_STATE.data.suppliers = data || []; done(); }).withFailureHandler(function() { done(); }).loadSuppliersData(1, 100); }
        if (pending === 0) { hideLoader(); renderFunc(); }
    }

    function _loadSuppliersForSelect(selectId) {
        var select = byId(selectId); if (!select) return;
        var suppliers = RW_STATE.data.suppliers || [];
        var html = '<option value="">-- اختر مورداً --</option>';
        for (var i = 0; i < suppliers.length; i++) { var s = suppliers[i]; html += '<option value="' + _escapeHtml(s.code || '') + '">' + _escapeHtml(s.name || '') + '</option>'; }
        safeHTML(select, html);
    }

    function _renderPurchaseCart() {
        var tbody = byId('purchase-items-body'); if (!tbody) return;
        var total = 0;
        if (purchaseCart.length === 0) { safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="5" class="p-8 text-center text-gray-400">لا توجد أصناف</td></tr>'); safeText(byId('purchase-items-count'), '0'); safeText(byId('purchase-total'), '0.00'); return; }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < purchaseCart.length; i++) {
            var item = purchaseCart[i]; var lineTotal = item.price * item.qty; total += lineTotal;
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50"><td class="p-3"><div class="font-bold text-gray-800">' + _escapeHtml(item.name) + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-400">' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '</div></td><td class="p-3 text-center font-bold text-emerald-600">' + Number(item.price).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td><td class="p-3 text-center"><input type="number" value="' + item.qty + '" onchange="RW_Purchases._updateCartQty(' + i + ', this.value)" class="w-16 p-1.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded text-center font-bold" min="1"></td><td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(lineTotal).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td><td class="p-3 text-center"><button onclick="RW_Purchases._removeFromCart(' + i + ')" class="text-red-500 hover:text-red-700"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash-can"></i></button></td></tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html); safeText(byId('purchase-items-count'), String(purchaseCart.length)); safeText(byId('purchase-total'), Number(total).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 }));
    }

    function _updateCartQty(idx, val) { var q = parseInt(val, 10); if (isNaN(q) || q <= 0) { purchaseCart.splice(idx, 1); } else { purchaseCart[idx].qty = q; } _renderPurchaseCart(); }
    function _removeFromCart(idx) { purchaseCart.splice(idx, 1); _renderPurchaseCart(); }

    function _clearCart() {
        var hasItems = false;
        for (var k in cart) {
            if (cart.hasOwnProperty(k)) {
                hasItems = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!hasItems) {
            showToast('السلة فارغة بالفعل', 'info');
            return;
        }
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد مسح السلة',
            text: 'سيتم حذف جميع الأصناف من السلة. هل أنت متأكد؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، امسح',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                cart = {};
                _renderProductCards();
                showToast('تم مسح السلة', 'success');
            }
        });
    }

    function _savePurchaseOrder() {
        var supplierSelect = byId('purchase-supplier'); var supplierId = supplierSelect ? supplierSelect.value : '';
        if (!supplierId) { showToast('اختر مورداً', 'warning'); return; }
        if (purchaseCart.length === 0) { showToast('أضف أصنافاً', 'warning'); return; }
        var total = 0; for (var i = 0; i < purchaseCart.length; i++) { total += purchaseCart[i].price * purchaseCart[i].qty; }
        var suppliers = RW_STATE.data.suppliers || []; var supplierName = '';
        for (var s = 0; s < suppliers.length; s++) { if (suppliers[s].code === supplierId) { supplierName = suppliers[s].name || ''; break; } }
        var orderHeader = { supplierId: supplierId, supplierName: supplierName, total: total };
        var itemsList = []; for (var j = 0; j < purchaseCart.length; j++) { var it = purchaseCart[j]; itemsList.push({ code: it.code, name: it.name, unit: it.unit, qty: it.qty, price: it.price }); }
        showLoader('جاري حفظ أمر الشراء...');
        var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ orderHeader: orderHeader, itemsList: itemsList });
        enqueueSync({ type: 'savePurchaseOrder', payload: cleanPayload, onSuccess: function(res) { hideLoader(); if (res && res.status === 'success') { showToast('تم حفظ أمر الشراء: ' + (res.poID || ''), 'success'); purchaseCart = []; _renderPurchaseCart(); var supplierSel = byId('purchase-supplier'); if (supplierSel) supplierSel.value = ''; } else { showToast(res && res.msg ? res.msg : 'فشل الحفظ', 'error'); } }, onFailure: function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + (err.message || ''), 'error'); } });
    }

    function _renderPurchaseOrders() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) { google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) { purchaseOrdersData = data || []; _renderOrdersTable(purchaseOrdersData); }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { var wrapper = byId('po-table-wrapper'); if (wrapper) safeHTML(wrapper, '<div class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">خطأ في التحميل</div>'); }).getPurchaseOrders(); }
        else { purchaseOrdersData = []; _renderOrdersTable(purchaseOrdersData); }
    }

    function _getStatusBadge(status) {
        if (status === 'Draft') return '<span class="bg-gray-200 text-gray-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold">مسودة</span>';
        if (status === 'Received') return '<span class="bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold">مستلم</span>';
        if (status === 'Partially Received') return '<span class="bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold">مستلم جزئياً</span>';
        return '<span class="bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(status || '') + '</span>';
    }

    function _renderOrdersTable(data) {
        var wrapper = byId('po-table-wrapper'); if (!wrapper) return;
        if (!data || data.length === 0) { safeHTML(wrapper, '<div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-400">لا توجد أوامر شراء</div>'); return; }
        var html = '<table class="w-full text-right"><thead class="bg-gray-100 sticky top-0"><tr><th class="p-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">رقم الأمر</th><th class="p-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">التاريخ</th><th class="p-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">المورد</th><th class="p-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase text-center">القيمة</th><th class="p-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase text-center">الحالة</th><th class="p-3 text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase text-center">تفاصيل</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) { var o = data[i]; html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Purchases._showOrderDetails(\'' + _escapeHtml(o.poId || '') + '\')"><td class="p-3 font-bold text-emerald-700">' + _escapeHtml(o.poId || '') + '</td><td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(o.date || '') + '</td><td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(o.supplierName || '') + '</td><td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(o.total || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td><td class="p-3 text-center">' + _getStatusBadge(o.status) + '</td><td class="p-3 text-center"><i class="fa-solid fa-eye text-blue-600"></i></td></tr>'; }
        html += '</tbody></table>'; safeHTML(wrapper, html);
    }

    function _showOrderDetails(poId) {
        showLoader('جاري تحميل التفاصيل...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) { google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(details) { hideLoader(); _displayOrderDetailsModal(poId, details); }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل تحميل التفاصيل: ' + (err.message || ''), 'error'); }).getPurchaseOrderDetails(poId); }
        else { hideLoader(); showToast('الخادم غير متاح', 'error'); }
    }

    function _displayOrderDetailsModal(poId, details) {
        if (!details || details.length === 0) { showToast('لا توجد تفاصيل لهذا الأمر', 'info'); return; }
        var html = '<div class="text-right"><table class="w-full border text-sm"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-2 border">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">السعر</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الإجمالي</th></tr></thead><tbody>'; var total = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < details.length; i++) { var d = details[i]; var lineTotal = (Number(d.qty) || 0) * (Number(d.price) || 0); total += lineTotal; html += '<tr><td class="p-2 border font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(d.name || '') + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + d.qty + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + Number(d.price || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td><td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + Number(lineTotal).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td></tr>'; }
        html += '</tbody></table><div class="mt-3 text-left font-bold text-lg text-emerald-700">الإجمالي: ' + Number(total).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div></div>';
        var buttonsHtml = '<div class="mt-4 flex flex-col gap-2"><button id="btn-receive-po" class="w-full bg-emerald-600 text-white py-3 rounded-xl font-bold shadow-lg"><i class="fa-solid fa-truck-loading ml-2"></i> استلام البضاعة</button><button class="w-full py-2 bg-gray-100 rounded-lg font-bold" onclick="Swal.close()">إغلاق</button></div>';
        Swal.fire({ title: 'تفاصيل أمر الشراء: ' + _escapeHtml(poId), html: html + buttonsHtml, width: '800px', showConfirmButton: false, didOpen: function() { var btn = document.getElementById('btn-receive-po'); if (btn) btn.addEventListener('click', function() { Swal.close(); _openReceivingModal(poId); }); } });
    }

    function _openReceivingModal(poId) {
        showLoader('جاري جلب بيانات الاستلام...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) { google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(items) { hideLoader(); _buildReceivingModal(poId, items); }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل جلب بيانات الاستلام: ' + (err.message || ''), 'error'); }).getPurchaseOrderForReceiving(poId); }
        else { hideLoader(); showToast('الخادم غير متاح', 'error'); }
    }

    function _buildReceivingModal(poId, items) {
        if (!items || items.length === 0) { showToast('لا توجد أصناف للاستلام', 'info'); return; }
        var html = '<div class="text-right" dir="rtl"><div class="max-h-[450px] overflow-y-auto"><table class="w-full border" style="border-spacing:0 8px;"><thead><tr class="text-gray-400 text-xs uppercase"><th class="pb-2 pr-4 text-right">الصنف</th><th class="pb-2 text-center">المطلوب</th><th class="pb-2 text-center">المستلم سابقاً</th><th class="pb-2 text-center">الكمية المستلمة الآن</th><th class="pb-2 text-center">سعر الشراء</th><th class="pb-2 text-center">الإجمالي</th></tr></thead><tbody id="receiving-tbody">';
        for (var idx = 0; idx < items.length; idx++) { var it = items[idx]; var orderedQty = Number(it.orderedQty) || 0; var receivedSoFar = Number(it.receivedSoFar) || 0; var remaining = Math.max(0, orderedQty - receivedSoFar); var price = Number(it.price) || 0; html += '<tr class="bg-white shadow-sm rounded-xl"><td class="p-3"><div class="font-bold text-sm">' + _escapeHtml(it.name || '') + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-400">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemCode || '') + '</div></td><td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + orderedQty + '</td><td class="p-3 text-center text-blue-600 font-bold">' + receivedSoFar + '</td><td class="p-3 text-center"><input type="number" id="rec_qty_' + idx + '" value="' + remaining + '" class="w-20 p-2 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-center font-bold" min="0" max="' + remaining + '" oninput="RW_Purchases._calcRecLine(' + idx + ', ' + orderedQty + ', ' + price + ')"></td><td class="p-3 text-center"><input type="number" id="rec_price_' + idx + '" value="' + price + '" class="w-20 p-2 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-center font-bold" oninput="RW_Purchases._calcRecLine(' + idx + ', ' + orderedQty + ', this.value)"></td><td class="p-3 text-center font-bold"><span id="rec_total_' + idx + '">' + Number(remaining * price).toLocaleString() + '</span> EGP</td></tr>'; }
        html += '</tbody></table></div><div class="mt-4"><label class="text-sm font-bold block mb-1">ملاحظات</label><textarea id="receiving-notes" class="w-full p-3 bg-gray-50 border rounded-xl text-sm" rows="2" placeholder="ملاحظات الاستلام..."></textarea></div></div>';
        Swal.fire({ title: 'استلام بضاعة: ' + _escapeHtml(poId), html: html, width: '950px', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'اعتماد الاستلام', confirmButtonColor: '#10b981', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء', preConfirm: function() { return _collectReceivingData(items); } }).then(function(result) { _handleReceivingSubmit(poId, result, items); });
    }

    function _collectReceivingData(items) {
        var results = [];
        for (var j = 0; j < items.length; j++) { var qtyInput = document.getElementById('rec_qty_' + j); var priceInput = document.getElementById('rec_price_' + j); var receivedQty = parseFloat(qtyInput ? qtyInput.value : '0') || 0; var receivedPrice = parseFloat(priceInput ? priceInput.value : '0') || 0; if (receivedQty > 0) { results.push({ itemCode: items[j].itemCode || '', itemName: items[j].name || '', unit: items[j].unit || 'حبة', receivedQty: receivedQty, receivedPrice: receivedPrice, orderedQty: items[j].orderedQty || 0 }); } }
        var notesInput = document.getElementById('receiving-notes'); return { items: results, notes: notesInput ? notesInput.value : '' };
    }

    function _handleReceivingSubmit(poId, result, items) {
        if (!result.isConfirmed || !result.value || result.value.items.length === 0) return;
        showLoader('جاري حفظ الاستلام...'); var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ poId: poId, itemsReceived: result.value.items, notes: result.value.notes });
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(res) { hideLoader(); if (res && res.status === 'success') { showToast('تم استلام البضاعة بنجاح', 'success'); _renderPurchaseOrders(); } else { showToast(res && res.msg ? res.msg : 'فشل الاستلام', 'error'); } }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + (err.message || ''), 'error'); }).executeFinalStoreEntry(poId, result.value.items, result.value.notes);
    }

    function _calcRecLine(idx, orderedQty, price) { var qtyInput = document.getElementById('rec_qty_' + idx); var priceInput = document.getElementById('rec_price_' + idx); var totalSpan = document.getElementById('rec_total_' + idx); if (!totalSpan) return; var qty = parseFloat(qtyInput ? qtyInput.value : '0') || 0; var prc = parseFloat(priceInput ? priceInput.value : '0') || 0; totalSpan.textContent = Number(qty * prc).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 }); }

    return {
        renderPOS: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container'); if (!container) return;
            safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'نقطة شراء'); safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'إنشاء أمر شراء جديد');
            _ensureDataAndRender(function() {
                var html = '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6"><div class="lg:col-span-1 space-y-4"><div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700 block mb-2">اختيار المورد</label><select id="purchase-supplier" class="w-full p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg font-semibold"><option value="">-- اختر مورداً --</option></select></div><div class="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700 block mb-2">البحث عن صنف</label><div class="relative"><input type="text" id="purchase-item-search" oninput="RW_Purchases._smartSearch(this.value)" autocomplete="off" placeholder="ابحث بالباركود أو الاسم..." class="w-full p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"><div id="purchase-dropdown-results" class="absolute z-50 left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-white shadow-xl rounded-xl max-h-60 overflow-y-auto hidden border"></div></div></div></div><div class="lg:col-span-3 bg-white rounded-xl shadow-md overflow-hidden flex flex-col min-h-[500px]"><div class="bg-emerald-700 text-white p-4 flex justify-between items-center"><h2 class="font-bold text-lg">أمر شراء جديد</h2><div><span class="text-xs opacity-75">عدد الأصناف</span><div id="purchase-items-count" class="text-xl font-bold">0</div></div></div><div class="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4"><table class="w-full text-right"><thead><tr class="text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase"><th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">السعر</th><th class="p-2 text-center w-24">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الإجمالي</th><th class="p-2"></th></tr></thead><tbody id="purchase-items-body"><tr><td colspan="5" class="p-8 text-center text-gray-400">لا توجد أصناف</td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="p-4 bg-gray-50 border-t flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center gap-4"><div><span class="text-gray-500 font-bold ml-2">إجمالي الأمر:</span><span id="purchase-total" class="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-800">0.00</span><span class="text-sm text-gray-400 mr-2">EGP</span></div><div class="flex gap-2"><button onclick="RW_Purchases._clearCart()" class="px-4 py-2 bg-red-500 text-white rounded-lg font-bold text-sm">مسح الكل</button><button onclick="RW_Purchases._savePurchaseOrder()" class="px-6 py-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white rounded-lg font-bold shadow">حفظ أمر الشراء</button></div></div></div></div>';
                safeHTML(container, html); _loadSuppliersForSelect('purchase-supplier'); _renderPurchaseCart();
            });
        },
        renderOrders: function() { var container = byId('rw-page-container'); if (!container) return; safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'أوردرات الشراء'); safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'قائمة أوامر الشراء واستلام البضاعة'); var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-3 mb-4"><h2 class="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fa-solid fa-truck-fast ml-2"></i> أوامر الشراء</h2><button onclick="RW_Navigation.navigate(\'purchase-pos\')" class="bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-700 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-bold shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-plus ml-1"></i> أمر شراء جديد</button></div><div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm overflow-x-auto" id="po-table-wrapper"><div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-400">جاري التحميل...</div></div></div>'; safeHTML(container, html); _renderPurchaseOrders(); },
        _smartSearch: function(query) { var div = byId('purchase-dropdown-results'); if (!div) return; if (!query || query.trim().length < 1) { div.classList.add('hidden'); return; } var q = query.toLowerCase(); var items = RW_STATE.data.items || []; var filtered = items.filter(function(i) { return (String(i.name || '') + String(i.barcode || '') + String(i.code || '')).toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1; }); if (filtered.length > 0) { var html = ''; for (var idx = 0; idx < Math.min(filtered.length, 20); idx++) { var item = filtered[idx]; html += '<div onclick="RW_Purchases._addToCart(\'' + _escapeHtml(item.code || '') + '\')" class="p-3 hover:bg-emerald-50 cursor-pointer flex justify-between border-b"><div><div class="font-bold text-sm">' + _escapeHtml(item.name || '') + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-400">' + _escapeHtml(item.code || '') + '</div></div><div class="text-emerald-600 font-bold">' + (Number(item.sPrice || 0).toLocaleString()) + ' EGP</div></div>'; } safeHTML(div, html); div.classList.remove('hidden'); } else { safeHTML(div, '<div class="p-3 text-center text-gray-400">لا توجد نتائج</div>'); div.classList.remove('hidden'); } },
        _addToCart: function(itemCode) { var items = RW_STATE.data.items || []; var item = null; for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) { if (items[i].code === itemCode) { item = items[i]; break; } } if (!item) return; var existing = null; for (var j = 0; j < purchaseCart.length; j++) { if (purchaseCart[j].code === itemCode) { existing = purchaseCart[j]; break; } } if (existing) { existing.qty++; } else { purchaseCart.push({ code: item.code, name: item.name, price: Number(item.sPrice) || 0, unit: item.unit || 'حبة', qty: 1 }); } var searchInput = byId('purchase-item-search'); if (searchInput) searchInput.value = ''; var dropdown = byId('purchase-dropdown-results'); if (dropdown) dropdown.classList.add('hidden'); _renderPurchaseCart(); },
        _updateCartQty: _updateCartQty, _removeFromCart: _removeFromCart, _clearCart: _clearCart, _savePurchaseOrder: _savePurchaseOrder, _showOrderDetails: _showOrderDetails, _calcRecLine: _calcRecLine
    };
})();
window.RW_Purchases = RW_Purchases;
// ============================================================
// RW_Users – تبويب إدارة المستخدمين والصلاحيات (معدل)
// ============================================================
var RW_Users = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var employeesData = [];
    var filterText = '';
    var rolesList = [];
    var branchesList = [];

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;'; if (m === '<') return '&lt;'; if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _loadEmployees() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    employeesData = data || [];
                    _renderTable();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    console.error('Failed to load employees:', err);
                    var tbody = byId('users-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">خطأ في تحميل بيانات الموظفين</td></tr>');
                })
                .getEmployeesList();
        } else {
            employeesData = [];
            _renderTable();
        }
    }

    function _renderTable() {
        var tbody = byId('users-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;

        var filtered = employeesData.filter(function(emp) {
            if (!filterText) return true;
            var s = filterText.toLowerCase();
            return (emp.name && emp.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(s) !== -1) ||
                   (emp.email && emp.email.toLowerCase().indexOf(s) !== -1) ||
                   (emp.role && emp.role.toLowerCase().indexOf(s) !== -1) ||
                   (emp.phone && emp.phone.toLowerCase().indexOf(s) !== -1);
        });

        if (filtered.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا يوجد موظفون</td></tr>');
            return;
        }

        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < filtered.length; i++) {
            var emp = filtered[i];
            var statusClass = emp.status === 'Active' ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-red-100 text-red-700';
            var statusText = emp.status === 'Active' ? 'نشط' : 'غير نشط';
            
            var permsDisplay = '';
            if (emp.permissions && emp.permissions.length > 0) {
                if (typeof emp.permissions === 'string') {
                    permsDisplay = emp.permissions;
                } else {
                    permsDisplay = emp.permissions.join(', ');
                }
            } else {
                permsDisplay = '-';
            }
            
            var allowedBranchesText = Array.isArray(emp.allowed_branch_ids) ? emp.allowed_branch_ids.join(', ') : (emp.allowedBranches || '');

            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Users._editEmployee(\'' + _escapeHtml(emp.email) + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(emp.name || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(emp.email || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(emp.role || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ' + statusClass + '">' + statusText + '</span></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(emp.phone || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center text-xs">' + _escapeHtml(allowedBranchesText) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center text-xs">' + _escapeHtml(permsDisplay) + '</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _loadRolesAndBranches(callback) {
        var loaded = 0;
        function checkDone() {
            loaded++;
            if (loaded === 2 && callback) callback();
        }
        
        // تحميل الأدوار
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                if (data && data.roles) rolesList = data.roles;
                else if (data && Array.isArray(data)) rolesList = data;
                checkDone();
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                console.error('Failed to load roles:', err);
                checkDone();
            })
            .seedDefaultRoles();
        
        // تحميل الفروع
        if (RW_STATE.data.branches && RW_STATE.data.branches.length > 0) {
            branchesList = RW_STATE.data.branches;
            checkDone();
        } else {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    RW_STATE.data.branches = data || [];
                    branchesList = RW_STATE.data.branches;
                    checkDone();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    console.error('Failed to load branches:', err);
                    checkDone();
                })
                .getBranches();
        }
    }

    function _openModal(empData) {
        var isEdit = !!empData;
        var title = isEdit ? 'تعديل موظف' : 'إضافة موظف جديد';

        _loadRolesAndBranches(function() {
            var branchMultiOptions = '';
            for (var b = 0; b < branchesList.length; b++) {
                var br = branchesList[b];
                var code = br.branch_code || br.id || '';
                var name = br.name || br.branch_name || '';
                branchMultiOptions += '<option value="' + code + '">' + name + ' (' + code + ')</option>';
            }

            var roleOptions = '';
            for (var r = 0; r < rolesList.length; r++) {
                var role = rolesList[r];
                var selected = (isEdit && empData.role_id === role.id) ? ' selected' : '';
                roleOptions += '<option value="' + role.id + '"' + selected + '>' + role.role_name + '</option>';
            }

            var html = '<div class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 z-50" dir="rtl">';
            html += '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-4xl overflow-hidden">';
            html += '<div class="bg-indigo-600 px-6 py-4 flex justify-between text-white"><h3 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fas fa-user-cog ml-2"></i>' + title + '</h3><button class="text-white/80 hover:text-white" onclick="Swal.close()"><i class="fas fa-xmark text-xl"></i></button></div>';
            html += '<form class="p-6 space-y-6" style="max-height:70vh;overflow-y:auto;">';
            html += '<input type="hidden" id="emp-original-email" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(empData.email || '') : '') + '">';
            html += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الاسم الكامل *</label><input id="emp-name" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(empData.name || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">البريد الإلكتروني *</label><input id="emp-email" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(empData.email || '') : '') + '" type="email" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">رقم الهاتف</label><input id="emp-phone" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(empData.phone || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">كلمة المرور *</label><input id="emp-password" type="password" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg" placeholder="' + (isEdit ? 'اترك فارغاً للإبقاء' : '') + '"></div>';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الدور الوظيفي *</label><select id="emp-role-id" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"><option value="">-- اختر دوراً --</option>' + roleOptions + '</select></div>';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الحالة</label><select id="emp-status" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"><option value="Active"' + (!isEdit || empData.status === 'Active' ? ' selected' : '') + '>نشط</option><option value="Inactive"' + (isEdit && empData.status === 'Inactive' ? ' selected' : '') + '>غير نشط</option></select></div>';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">تاريخ انتهاء الصلاحية</label><input id="emp-expiry" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(empData.expiry_date || empData.expiryDate || '') : '') + '" type="date" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
            
            // --- قسم الفروع المسموحة (Tags + Checkboxes + بحث) ---
            html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الفروع المسموحة</label>';
            html += '<div class="relative">';
            html += '<input type="text" id="emp-branch-search" placeholder="ابحث عن فرع..." autocomplete="off" class="w-full p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg text-sm">';
            html += '<div id="emp-branch-dropdown" class="absolute z-50 left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-white shadow-xl rounded-xl max-h-48 overflow-y-auto hidden border">';
            // قائمة Checkboxes ستُملأ ديناميكياً
            html += '<label class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer"><input type="checkbox" value="*" onchange="RW_Users._toggleBranch(\'*\', this.checked)"> جميع الفروع (★)</label>';
            for (var b = 0; b < branchesList.length; b++) {
                var br = branchesList[b];
                var code = br.branch_code || br.id || '';
                var name = br.name || br.branch_name || '';
                html += '<label class="flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer"><input type="checkbox" value="' + code + '" onchange="RW_Users._toggleBranch(\'' + code + '\', this.checked)"> ' + name + ' (' + code + ')</label>';
            }
            html += '</div>';
            html += '</div>';
            html += '<div id="emp-selected-branches" class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2"></div>';
            html += '<input type="hidden" id="emp-allowed-branches" value="' + (isEdit ? (Array.isArray(empData.allowed_branch_ids) ? empData.allowed_branch_ids.join(',') : (empData.allowedBranches || '')) : '') + '">';
            html += '<p class="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">ابحث عن الفروع وحددها. يمكنك إزالة أي فرع بالضغط على ×.</p></div>';
            // --- نهاية قسم الفروع ---
            html += '</div>';
            html += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t border-gray-100">';
            if (isEdit) html += '<button type="button" id="btn-delete-employee" class="px-5 py-2.5 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold mr-auto"><i class="fas fa-trash-alt ml-1"></i> حذف</button>';
            html += '<button type="button" class="px-5 py-2.5 border border-gray-300 rounded-xl font-bold text-gray-700 bg-white hover:bg-gray-50" onclick="Swal.close()">إلغاء</button>';
            html += '<button type="button" id="btn-save-employee" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white rounded-xl font-bold shadow-md">حفظ</button>';
            html += '</div>';
            html += '</form>';
            html += '</div></div>';

            Swal.fire({
                html: html, width: '900px', showConfirmButton: false, showCancelButton: false,
                customClass: { popup: '!bg-transparent !shadow-none !p-0' },
                didOpen: function() {
                    // تعيين القيم الحالية للفروع المسموحة (للتعديل)
                    if (isEdit) {
                        var currentAllowed = empData.allowedBranches || (Array.isArray(empData.allowed_branch_ids) ? empData.allowed_branch_ids.join(',') : '');
                        var sel = document.getElementById('emp-allowed-branches');
                        if (sel && currentAllowed) {
                            var vals = currentAllowed.split(',').map(function(s) { return s.trim(); });
                            for (var o = 0; o < sel.options.length; o++) {
                                if (vals.indexOf(sel.options[o].value) !== -1) {
                                    sel.options[o].selected = true;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    var saveBtn = document.getElementById('btn-save-employee');
                    if (saveBtn) {
                        saveBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                            var name = document.getElementById('emp-name') ? document.getElementById('emp-name').value.trim() : '';
                            var email = document.getElementById('emp-email') ? document.getElementById('emp-email').value.trim() : '';
                            var password = document.getElementById('emp-password') ? document.getElementById('emp-password').value : '';
                            var roleId = document.getElementById('emp-role-id') ? document.getElementById('emp-role-id').value : '';
                            var status = document.getElementById('emp-status') ? document.getElementById('emp-status').value : 'Active';
                            var phone = document.getElementById('emp-phone') ? document.getElementById('emp-phone').value.trim() : '';
                            var expiry = document.getElementById('emp-expiry') ? document.getElementById('emp-expiry').value : '';
                            
                            var allowedSelect = document.getElementById('emp-allowed-branches');
                            var allowedBranches = '*';
                            if (allowedSelect) {
                                var selectedOpts = [];
                                for (var o = 0; o < allowedSelect.options.length; o++) {
                                    if (allowedSelect.options[o].selected) {
                                        selectedOpts.push(allowedSelect.options[o].value);
                                    }
                                }
                                if (selectedOpts.length > 0) {
                                    // إذا تم اختيار "جميع الفروع" (*)، نجعلها هي القيمة
                                    if (selectedOpts.indexOf('*') !== -1) {
                                        allowedBranches = '*';
                                    } else {
                                        allowedBranches = selectedOpts.join(',');
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            if (!name || !email) {
                                showToast('الاسم والبريد الإلكتروني مطلوبان', 'error');
                                return;
                            }
                            if (!isEdit && !password) {
                                showToast('يجب تعيين كلمة مرور للموظف الجديد', 'error');
                                return;
                            }

                            var currentCompanyId = (RW_STATE.app.currentUser && RW_STATE.app.currentUser.companyId) ? RW_STATE.app.currentUser.companyId : '';

                            var empDataPayload = {
                                email: email,
                                name: name,
                                password: password,
                                roleId: roleId,
                                status: status,
                                phone: phone,
                                expiryDate: expiry,
                                companyId: currentCompanyId,
                                defaultBranch: '',
                                allowedBranches: allowedBranches,
                                customPermissions: ''
                            };

                            Swal.close();
                            var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({
                                empData: empDataPayload,
                                isNew: !isEdit,
                                currentUserEmail: RW_STATE.app.currentUser ? RW_STATE.app.currentUser.email : ''
                            });
                            enqueueSync({
                                type: 'saveEmployee',
                                payload: cleanPayload,
                                onSuccess: function(res) {
                                    if (res && res.status === 'success') {
                                        showToast(isEdit ? 'تم تحديث الموظف بنجاح' : 'تم إضافة الموظف بنجاح', 'success');
                                        _loadEmployees();
                                    } else {
                                        showToast(res && res.msg ? res.msg : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الحفظ', 'error');
                                    }
                                },
                                onFailure: function(err) {
                                    showToast('فشل الحفظ: ' + err.message, 'error');
                                }
                            });
                        });
                    }
                    if (isEdit) {
                        var deleteBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-employee');
                        if (deleteBtn) {
                            deleteBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                                Swal.close();
                                _confirmDelete(empData.email);
                            });
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }

    function _confirmDelete(email) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف',
            text: 'هل أنت متأكد من حذف هذا الموظف؟ لا يمكن التراجع.',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            cancelButtonColor: '#3085d6',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، احذف',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({
                    email: email,
                    currentUserEmail: RW_STATE.app.currentUser ? RW_STATE.app.currentUser.email : ''
                });
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'deleteEmployee',
                    payload: cleanPayload,
                    onSuccess: function(res) {
                        if (res && res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم حذف الموظف بنجاح', 'success');
                            _loadEmployees();
                        } else {
                            showToast(res && res.msg ? res.msg : 'حدث خطأ أثناء الحذف', 'error');
                        }
                    },
                    onFailure: function(err) {
                        showToast('فشل الحذف: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function render() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'المستخدمين والصلاحيات');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'إدارة حسابات الموظفين وصلاحيات الوصول');
        var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-6 gap-3"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fas fa-users-gear ml-2"></i> إدارة المستخدمين والصلاحيات</h2><button id="add-employee-btn" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow transition"><i class="fas fa-plus ml-1"></i> إضافة موظف</button></div><div class="mb-4"><div class="relative"><i class="fas fa-search absolute right-3 top-3 text-gray-400"></i><input type="text" id="user-search" placeholder="بحث بالاسم أو البريد أو الدور..." class="w-full pr-10 p-2 border rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-400"></div></div><div class="overflow-x-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow"><table class="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الاسم</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">البريد</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الدور</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الحالة</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الهاتف</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الفروع المسموحة</th><th class="p-3 text-center text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase">الصلاحيات</th></tr></thead><tbody id="users-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);
        var addBtn = byId('add-employee-btn');
        if (addBtn) addBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { _openModal(null); });
        var searchInput = byId('user-search');
        if (searchInput) searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() { filterText = this.value; _renderTable(); });
        _loadEmployees();
    }

    return {
        render: render,
        _editEmployee: function(email) {
            var emp = null;
            for (var i = 0; i < employeesData.length; i++) {
                if (employeesData[i].email === email) { emp = employeesData[i]; break; }
            }
            if (emp) _openModal(emp);
            else showToast('الموظف غير موجود', 'error');
        },
        _filterBranches: function() {
            var searchInput = document.getElementById('emp-branch-search');
            var dropdown = document.getElementById('emp-branch-dropdown');
            if (!searchInput || !dropdown) return;
            var filter = searchInput.value.toLowerCase();
            var items = dropdown.querySelectorAll('label');
            for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                var text = items[i].innerText.toLowerCase();
                items[i].style.display = text.indexOf(filter) > -1 ? '' : 'none';
            }
        },
        _toggleBranch: function(code, isChecked) {
            var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('#emp-branch-dropdown input[type="checkbox"]');
            if (code === '*') {
                for (var i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) {
                    checkboxes[i].checked = (checkboxes[i].value === '*') ? isChecked : false;
                }
            } else {
                if (isChecked) {
                    var allCheckbox = document.querySelector('#emp-branch-dropdown input[value="*"]');
                    if (allCheckbox) allCheckbox.checked = false;
                }
            }
            RW_Users._updateSelectedBranches();
        },
        _updateSelectedBranches: function() {
            var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('#emp-branch-dropdown input[type="checkbox"]:checked');
            var selected = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) { selected.push(checkboxes[i].value); }
            var hiddenInput = document.getElementById('emp-allowed-branches');
            if (hiddenInput) { hiddenInput.value = selected.join(','); }
            var container = document.getElementById('emp-selected-branches');
            if (container) {
                var html = '';
                for (var i = 0; i < selected.length; i++) {
                    var val = selected[i];
                    var label = val === '*' ? 'جميع الفروع' : val;
                    html += '<span class="inline-flex items-center gap-1 bg-indigo-100 text-indigo-700 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs">' + label + ' <button type="button" class="text-red-500 hover:text-red-700" onclick="RW_Users._removeBranch(\'' + val + '\')">&times;</button></span>';
                }
                container.innerHTML = html;
            }
            var searchInput = document.getElementById('emp-branch-search');
            if (searchInput && searchInput.value.trim() === '') {
                document.getElementById('emp-branch-dropdown').classList.add('hidden');
            }
        },
        _removeBranch: function(code) {
            var checkbox = document.querySelector('#emp-branch-dropdown input[value="' + code + '"]');
            if (checkbox) {
                checkbox.checked = false;
                if (code === '*') {
                    var allCheckboxes = document.querySelectorAll('#emp-branch-dropdown input[type="checkbox"]');
                    for (var i = 0; i < allCheckboxes.length; i++) { allCheckboxes[i].checked = false; }
                }
            }
            RW_Users._updateSelectedBranches();
        },
        _initBranchDropdown: function() {
            var searchInput = document.getElementById('emp-branch-search');
            var dropdown = document.getElementById('emp-branch-dropdown');
            if (!searchInput || !dropdown) return;
            searchInput.addEventListener('focus', function() { dropdown.classList.remove('hidden'); RW_Users._filterBranches(); });
            searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() { dropdown.classList.remove('hidden'); RW_Users._filterBranches(); });
            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                var wrapper = document.querySelector('.relative');
                if (wrapper && !wrapper.contains(e.target)) { dropdown.classList.add('hidden'); }
            });
            var hiddenInput = document.getElementById('emp-allowed-branches');
            if (hiddenInput && hiddenInput.value) {
                var vals = hiddenInput.value.split(',');
                var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('#emp-branch-dropdown input[type="checkbox"]');
                for (var i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) {
                    if (vals.indexOf(checkboxes[i].value) !== -1) { checkboxes[i].checked = true; }
                }
                RW_Users._updateSelectedBranches();
            }
        }
    };
})();
window.RW_Users = RW_Users;
// ============================================================
// RW_Roles – تبويب إدارة أدوار الموظفين
// ============================================================
var RW_Roles = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var rolesData = [];

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
