        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;'; if (m === '<') return '&lt;'; if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _loadRoles() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    rolesData = data || [];
                    _renderTable();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    showToast('فشل تحميل الأدوار: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getRoles();
        }
    }

    function _renderTable() {
        var tbody = byId('roles-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (rolesData.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد أدوار. اضغط "تهيئة الأدوار الافتراضية" لإنشائها.</td></tr>');
            return;
        }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < rolesData.length; i++) {
            var role = rolesData[i];
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Roles._editRole(\'' + role.id + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(role.role_name || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-gray-600">' + _escapeHtml(role.description || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center text-xs">' + (role.is_system ? 'أساسي' : 'مخصص') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><button class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); RW_Roles._editRole(\'' + role.id + '\')"><i class="fa-solid fa-pen"></i></button></td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _seedDefaultRoles() {
        showLoader('جاري تهيئة الأدوار...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                hideLoader();
                if (res.status === 'success') {
                    showToast(res.msg, 'success');
                    _loadRoles();
                } else {
                    showToast(res.msg, 'error');
                }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                hideLoader();
                showToast('فشل التهيئة: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .seedDefaultRoles();
    }

    function _openModal(roleData) {
        var isEdit = !!roleData;
        var title = isEdit ? 'تعديل دور' : 'إضافة دور جديد';
        var perms = [];
        if (isEdit && roleData.permissions) {
            perms = roleData.permissions.map(function(p) { return p.permission_key; });
        }

        var permissionLabels = [
            { key: 'dash', label: 'لوحة التحكم' },
            { key: 'online-store', label: 'المتجر الإلكتروني' },
            { key: 'items', label: 'الأصناف' },
            { key: 'customers', label: 'العملاء' },
            { key: 'pos', label: 'نقطة البيع' },
            { key: 'orders', label: 'الأوردرات' },
            { key: 'runsheets', label: 'الرانشيتات' },
            { key: 'purchases', label: 'المشتريات' },
            { key: 'warehouse', label: 'المخازن' },
            { key: 'branches', label: 'الفروع' },
            { key: 'finance', label: 'الحسابات' },
            { key: 'reports', label: 'التقارير' },
            { key: 'users', label: 'الموظفين' },
            { key: 'settings', label: 'إعدادات النظام' },
            { key: 'roles', label: 'إدارة الأدوار' }
        ];
        var permsHTML = '<div id="role-permissions-checkboxes" class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-2 mt-2">';
        for (var p = 0; p < permissionLabels.length; p++) {
            var pl = permissionLabels[p];
            var checked = perms.indexOf(pl.key) !== -1 ? 'checked' : '';
            permsHTML += '<label class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm"><input type="checkbox" value="' + pl.key + '" ' + checked + '> ' + pl.label + '</label>';
        }
        permsHTML += '</div>';

        var html = '<div class="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 z-50" dir="rtl">';
        html += '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-2xl overflow-hidden">';
        html += '<div class="bg-indigo-600 px-6 py-4 flex justify-between text-white"><h3 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fas fa-user-shield ml-2"></i>' + title + '</h3><button class="text-white/80 hover:text-white" onclick="Swal.close()"><i class="fas fa-xmark text-xl"></i></button></div>';
        html += '<form class="p-6 space-y-6" style="max-height:70vh;overflow-y:auto;">';
        html += '<input type="hidden" id="role-id-hidden" value="' + (isEdit ? roleData.id : '') + '">';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">اسم الدور *</label><input id="role-name" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(roleData.role_name || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الوصف</label><input id="role-desc" value="' + (isEdit ? _escapeHtml(roleData.description || '') : '') + '" type="text" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
        html += '<div class="mt-4"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700 block mb-2">الصلاحيات</label>' + permsHTML + '</div>';
        html += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t">';
        if (isEdit) html += '<button type="button" id="btn-delete-role" class="px-5 py-2.5 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold mr-auto"><i class="fas fa-trash-alt ml-1"></i> حذف</button>';
        html += '<button type="button" class="px-5 py-2.5 border border-gray-300 rounded-xl font-bold" onclick="Swal.close()">إلغاء</button>';
        html += '<button type="button" id="btn-save-role" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-indigo-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold">حفظ</button>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '</form></div></div>';

        Swal.fire({
            html: html, width: '700px', showConfirmButton: false, showCancelButton: false,
            customClass: { popup: '!bg-transparent !shadow-none !p-0' },
            didOpen: function() {
                var saveBtn = document.getElementById('btn-save-role');
                if (saveBtn) {
                    saveBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        var name = document.getElementById('role-name').value.trim();
                        if (!name) { showToast('اسم الدور مطلوب', 'error'); return; }
                        var selPerms = [];
                        var cbs = document.querySelectorAll('#role-permissions-checkboxes input[type="checkbox"]:checked');
                        for (var i = 0; i < cbs.length; i++) selPerms.push(cbs[i].value);
                        var payload = {
                            id: isEdit ? roleData.id : null,
                            role_name: name,
                            description: document.getElementById('role-desc').value.trim(),
                            permissions: selPerms,
                            is_system: isEdit ? roleData.is_system : false
                        };
                        Swal.close();
                        var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript(payload);
                        enqueueSync({
                            type: 'saveRole',
                            payload: cleanPayload,
                            onSuccess: function(res) {
                                if (res && res.status === 'success') {
                                    showToast(isEdit ? 'تم تحديث الدور' : 'تم إضافة الدور', 'success');
                                    _loadRoles();
                                } else { showToast(res.msg || 'خطأ', 'error'); }
                            },
                            onFailure: function(err) { showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); }
                        });
                    });
                }
                if (isEdit) {
                    var delBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-role');
                    if (delBtn) delBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { Swal.close(); _confirmDelete(roleData.id, roleData.role_name); });
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function _confirmDelete(roleId, name) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف', text: 'حذف "' + name + '"؟', icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#d33', confirmButtonText: 'نعم', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(r) {
            if (r.isConfirmed) {
                var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ roleId: roleId });
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'deleteRole',
                    payload: cleanPayload,
                    onSuccess: function(res) {
                        if (res && res.status === 'success') { showToast('تم الحذف', 'success'); _loadRoles(); }
                        else { showToast(res.msg || 'خطأ', 'error'); }
                    },
                    onFailure: function(err) { showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    return {
        _editRole: function(roleId) {
            if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
                google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(perms) {
                    var role = null;
                    for (var i = 0; i < rolesData.length; i++) { if (rolesData[i].id === roleId) { role = rolesData[i]; break; } }
                    if (!role) { showToast('الدور غير موجود', 'error'); return; }
                    role.permissions = perms || [];
                    _openModal(role);
                }).getRolePermissions(roleId);
            }
        },
        render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;
            safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إدارة أدوار الموظفين');
            safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'إنشاء وتعديل الأدوار الوظيفية وصلاحياتها');
            var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-6 gap-3"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fas fa-user-shield ml-2"></i> أدوار الموظفين</h2><div class="flex gap-2"><button id="seed-roles-btn" class="bg-emerald-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow"><i class="fas fa-seedling ml-1"></i> تهيئة الأدوار الافتراضية</button><button id="add-role-btn" class="bg-indigo-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow"><i class="fas fa-plus ml-1"></i> إضافة دور</button></div></div><div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden"><table class="min-w-full"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-3 text-center">اسم الدور</th><th class="p-3 text-center">الوصف</th><th class="p-3 text-center">النوع</th><th class="p-3 text-center">إجراءات</th></tr></thead><tbody id="roles-table-body"><tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>';
            safeHTML(container, html);
            var addBtn = byId('add-role-btn');
            if (addBtn) addBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { _openModal(null); });
            var seedBtn = byId('seed-roles-btn');
            if (seedBtn) seedBtn.addEventListener('click', _seedDefaultRoles);
            _loadRoles();
        }
    };
})();
window.RW_Roles = RW_Roles;
// ============================================================
// RW_OwnerLicense – صفحة إدارة الترخيص للمالك العام
// ============================================================
var RW_OwnerLicense = (function() {
    'use strict';

    function render() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;

        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إدارة الترخيص');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'التحكم في حالة الشركة وفترة الصلاحية');

        var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-6 gap-3"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fas fa-shield-haltered ml-2"></i> إدارة ترخيص الشركة</h2></div><div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6" id="license-page-content"><div class="text-center py-10 text-gray-400"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i> جاري تحميل بيانات الترخيص...</div></div></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        _loadLicenseData();
    }

    function _loadLicenseData() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    if (data.status !== 'success') {
                        showToast(data.msg, 'error');
                        return;
                    }
                    _buildLicenseForm(data);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    showToast('فشل تحميل بيانات الترخيص: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getCompanyLicenseInfo();
        }
    }

function _buildLicenseForm(licenseInfo) {
    var container = byId('license-page-content');
    if (!container) return;

    var currentStatus = licenseInfo.licenseStatus || 'trial';
    var trialEnd = licenseInfo.trialEndDate || '';
    var subEnd = licenseInfo.subscriptionEndDate || '';

    var html = '<form class="space-y-6">';
    html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">حالة الشركة</label><select id="license-status" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg">';
    html += '<option value="trial"' + (currentStatus === 'trial' ? ' selected' : '') + '>فترة تجربة</option>';
    html += '<option value="active"' + (currentStatus === 'active' ? ' selected' : '') + '>نشطة</option>';
    html += '<option value="suspended"' + (currentStatus === 'suspended' ? ' selected' : '') + '>موقوفة</option>';
    html += '<option value="cancelled"' + (currentStatus === 'cancelled' ? ' selected' : '') + '>ملغاة</option>';
    html += '</select></div>';

    html += '<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
    html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">تاريخ انتهاء التجربة</label><input id="license-trial-end" type="date" value="' + trialEnd + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
    html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">تاريخ انتهاء الاشتراك</label><input id="license-sub-end" type="date" value="' + subEnd + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
    html += '</div>';

    html += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t">';
    html += '<button type="button" id="btn-save-license" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white rounded-xl font-bold shadow-md">حفظ التغييرات</button>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '</form>';

    safeHTML(container, html);

    document.getElementById('btn-save-license').addEventListener('click', function() {
        var newStatus = document.getElementById('license-status').value;
        var trialEndDate = document.getElementById('license-trial-end').value;
        var subEndDate = document.getElementById('license-sub-end').value;

        var licensePayload = {
            status: newStatus,
            trialEndDate: trialEndDate,
            subscriptionEndDate: subEndDate
        };

        showLoader('جاري حفظ الترخيص...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                hideLoader();
                if (res.status === 'success') {
                    showToast(res.msg, 'success');
                    _loadLicenseData();
                } else {
                    showToast(res.msg, 'error');
                }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                hideLoader();
                showToast('فشل الحفظ: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .updateCompanyLicense(licensePayload);
    });
}

    return {
        render: render
    };
})();
window.RW_OwnerLicense = RW_OwnerLicense;

// RW_Settings – تبويب إعدادات النظام (رسوم التوصيل والحد الأدنى)
// ============================================================
var RW_Settings = (function() {
    'use strict';

    function render() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إعدادات النظام');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'تخصيص إعدادات التوصيل والفاتورة');

        showLoader('جاري تحميل الإعدادات...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                hideLoader();
                _buildSettingsForm(data);
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                hideLoader();
                showToast('فشل تحميل الإعدادات: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .getAppSettings();
    }

    function _buildSettingsForm(settings) {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;

        var deliveryFee = settings.deliveryFee || 0;
        var minInvoice = settings.minInvoiceAmount || 0;
        var taxRate = settings.taxRate || 0;
        var taxAccountId = settings.taxAccountId || '216';
        var companyName = settings.companyName || 'الروائع';
        var companyLogo = settings.companyLogo || '';

        var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-6 gap-3"><h2 class="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-800"><i class="fas fa-cog ml-2"></i> إعدادات النظام</h2></div><div class="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6"><form class="space-y-6">';
        
        // --- المجموعة الأولى: إعدادات الفاتورة ---
        html += '<h3 class="text-lg font-black text-indigo-600 border-b pb-2 mb-4"><i class="fa-solid fa-file-invoice-dollar ml-2"></i> إعدادات الفاتورة والرسوم</h3>';
        html += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">رسوم التوصيل (EGP)</label><input id="settings-delivery-fee" type="number" value="' + deliveryFee + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">الحد الأدنى للفاتورة (EGP)</label><input id="settings-min-invoice" type="number" value="' + minInvoice + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
        html += '</div>';

        // --- المجموعة الثانية: إعدادات الضريبة ---
        html += '<h3 class="text-lg font-black text-red-600 border-b pb-2 mb-4 mt-6"><i class="fa-solid fa-percent ml-2"></i> إعدادات ضريبة القيمة المضافة (VAT)</h3>';
        html += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">نسبة الضريبة (%)</label><input id="settings-tax-rate" type="number" step="0.01" value="' + taxRate + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"><p class="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">مثلاً: 15.00</p></div>';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">حساب ضريبة القيمة المضافة</label><input id="settings-tax-account" type="text" value="' + taxAccountId + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"><p class="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">كود الحساب من شجرة الحسابات (افتراضي: 216)</p></div>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '<div class="bg-amber-50 border-r-4 border-amber-500 p-4 rounded-lg text-sm text-amber-800"><i class="fa-solid fa-triangle-exclamation ml-2"></i> تنبيه: سيتم استخدام نسبة الضريبة هذه عند إنشاء الفواتير. تأكد من مطابقتها للتشريعات الضريبية السارية. سيتم تسجيل قيمة الضريبة تلقائياً في الحساب المحدد أعلاه.</div>';

        // --- المجموعة الثالثة: معلومات الشركة ---
        html += '<h3 class="text-lg font-black text-slate-600 border-b pb-2 mb-4 mt-6"><i class="fa-solid fa-building ml-2"></i> معلومات الشركة</h3>';
        html += '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">اسم الشركة</label><input id="settings-company-name" type="text" value="' + companyName + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
        html += '<div class="flex flex-col"><label class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-700">رابط شعار الشركة</label><input id="settings-company-logo" type="text" value="' + companyLogo + '" class="p-2.5 bg-gray-50 border rounded-lg"></div>';
        html += '</div>';

        // --- زر الحفظ ---
        html += '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3 pt-4 border-t"><button type="button" id="btn-save-settings" class="px-6 py-2.5 bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-700 text-white rounded-xl font-bold shadow-md">حفظ الإعدادات</button></div></form></div></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        document.getElementById('btn-save-settings').addEventListener('click', function() {
            var deliveryFee = parseFloat(document.getElementById('settings-delivery-fee').value) || 0;
            var minInvoice = parseFloat(document.getElementById('settings-min-invoice').value) || 0;
            var taxRate = parseFloat(document.getElementById('settings-tax-rate').value) || 0;
            var taxAccountId = document.getElementById('settings-tax-account').value.trim() || '216';
            var companyName = document.getElementById('settings-company-name').value.trim() || 'الروائع';
            var companyLogo = document.getElementById('settings-company-logo').value.trim() || '';

            showLoader('جاري حفظ الإعدادات...');
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (res.status === 'success') {
                        showToast('تم حفظ الإعدادات', 'success');
                    } else {
                        showToast(res.msg || 'حدث خطأ', 'error');
                    }
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل الحفظ: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .saveAppSettings(deliveryFee, minInvoice, companyName, companyLogo, taxRate, taxAccountId);
        });
    }

    return {
        render: render
    };
})();
window.RW_Settings = RW_Settings;
// ============================================================
// RW_Orders – تبويب أوردرات المبيعات (مُحدَّث – متوافق مع النسخة B)
// ============================================================
var RW_Orders = (function() {
    'use strict';

    var currentSort = { field: 'orderId', asc: true };

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _renderTable(orders) {
        var tbody = byId('orders-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;

        var data = orders || RW_STATE.data.orders || [];

        if (data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="9" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد أوردرات</td></tr>');
            return;
        }

        var sorted = data.slice().sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[currentSort.field] || '', vb = b[currentSort.field] || '';
            if (currentSort.field === 'total' || currentSort.field === 'itemsAmount') {
                va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb);
            } else if (currentSort.field === 'date') {
                va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb);
            } else {
                va = String(va).toLowerCase(); vb = String(vb).toLowerCase();
            }
            if (va < vb) return currentSort.asc ? -1 : 1;
            if (va > vb) return currentSort.asc ? 1 : -1;
            return 0;
        });

        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < sorted.length; i++) {
            var o = sorted[i];
            var statusClass = '';
            if (o.status === 'Draft') statusClass = 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700';
            else if (o.status === 'Confirmed') statusClass = 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700';
            else if (o.status === 'Pending') statusClass = 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-700';
            else if (o.status === 'Invoiced' || o.status === 'Delivered') statusClass = 'bg-green-100 text-green-700';
            else if (o.status === 'Cancelled') statusClass = 'bg-red-100 text-red-700';
            else statusClass = 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-700';

            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center" onclick="event.stopPropagation()"><input type="checkbox" class="order-checkbox" data-id="' + _escapeHtml(o.orderId) + '"></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold text-blue-600 cursor-pointer" onclick="window.RW_Orders._showOrderDetails(\'' + _escapeHtml(o.orderId) + '\')">' + _escapeHtml(o.orderId) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + (o.date ? new Date(o.date).toLocaleDateString('ar-EG') : '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><p class="font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(o.custName || '') + '</p><p class="text-xs text-gray-500">' + _escapeHtml(o.area || '') + '</p></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (o.itemsAmount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(o.total || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ' + statusClass + '">' + _escapeHtml(o.status || '') + '</span></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + (o.runsheetId || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _applyFilters() {
        var data = RW_STATE.data.orders || [];
        var fdEl = byId('filter-date-from');
        var fd = fdEl ? fdEl.value : '';
        var tdEl = byId('filter-date-to');
        var td = tdEl ? tdEl.value : '';
        var custEl = byId('filter-cust');
        var cust = custEl ? (custEl.value || '').toLowerCase() : '';
        var stEl = byId('filter-status');
        var st = stEl ? stEl.value : '';
        var areaEl = byId('filter-area');
        var area = areaEl ? (areaEl.value || '').toLowerCase() : '';
        var rsEl = byId('filter-rs');
        var rs = rsEl ? (rsEl.value || '').toLowerCase() : '';

        var filtered = data;
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(o) { return o.date && o.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(o) { return o.date && o.date <= td; }); }
        if (cust) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(o) { return o.custName && (o.custName.toLowerCase().indexOf(cust) !== -1); }); }
        if (st) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(o) { return o.status === st; }); }
        if (area) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(o) { return o.area && (o.area.toLowerCase().indexOf(area) !== -1); }); }
        if (rs) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(o) { return o.runsheetId && (o.runsheetId.toLowerCase().indexOf(rs) !== -1); }); }
        _renderTable(filtered);
    }

    function _resetFilters() {
        var ids = ['filter-date-from', 'filter-date-to', 'filter-cust', 'filter-status', 'filter-area', 'filter-rs'];
        for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
            var el = byId(ids[i]);
            if (el) el.value = '';
        }
        _applyFilters();
    }

    function _showOrdersWithoutRunsheet() {
        var data = RW_STATE.data.orders || [];
        var filtered = data.filter(function(o) { return !o.runsheetId || o.runsheetId === ''; });
        _renderTable(filtered);
    }

    function _getSelectedOrders() {
        var selected = [];
        var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.order-checkbox:checked');
        for (var i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) {
            selected.push(checkboxes[i].dataset.id);
        }
        return selected;
    }

    function _createNewRunsheet() {
        var selected = _getSelectedOrders();
        if (selected.length === 0) {
            showToast('يرجى تحديد أوردر واحد على الأقل', 'warning');
            return;
        }

        Swal.fire({
            title: 'إنشاء رانشيت جديد',
            text: 'سيتم تجميع ' + selected.length + ' أوردر في رانشيت جديد. متابعة؟',
            icon: 'question',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، إنشاء',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري إنشاء الرانشيت...');

            var cleanPayload = sanitizeForAppsScript({ selectedOrders: selected });
            enqueueSync({
                type: 'createRunsheet',
                payload: cleanPayload,
                onSuccess: function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (res && res.status === 'success') {
                        showToast('تم إنشاء الرانشيت: ' + res.rsId, 'success');
                        RW_Data.refresh();
                    } else {
                        showToast(res.msg || 'فشل إنشاء الرانشيت', 'error');
                    }
                },
                onFailure: function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                }
            });
        });
    }

    function _appendToExistingRunsheet() {
        var selected = _getSelectedOrders();
        if (selected.length === 0) {
            showToast('يرجى تحديد أوردر واحد على الأقل', 'warning');
            return;
        }

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(allRunsheets) {
                    if (!allRunsheets || allRunsheets.length === 0) {
                        showToast('لا توجد رانشيتات متاحة', 'info');
                        return;
                    }

                    var openSheets = allRunsheets.filter(function(rs) {
                        var status = (rs.status || '').toLowerCase();
                        var closedStatuses = ["picking", "picked", "loading", "loaded", "delivering", "delivered", "returning", "returned", "closed", "cancelled"];
                        return closedStatuses.indexOf(status) === -1;
                    });

                    if (openSheets.length === 0) {
                        showToast('لا توجد رانشيتات مفتوحة. أنشئ رانشيت جديد أولاً.', 'warning');
                        return;
                    }

                    var inputOptions = {};
                    openSheets.forEach(function(rs) {
                        inputOptions[rs.runsheet_code || rs.rsId] = (rs.runsheet_code || rs.rsId) + ' - حالة: ' + (rs.status || 'Open');
                    });

                    Swal.fire({
                        title: 'اختر الرانشيت',
                        input: 'select',
                        inputOptions: inputOptions,
                        showCancelButton: true,
                        confirmButtonText: 'ضم',
                        cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
                    }).then(function(result) {
                        if (!result.isConfirmed || !result.value) return;
                        showLoader('جاري ضم الأوردرات...');
                        google.script.run
                            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                                hideLoader();
                                if (res.status === 'success') {
                                    showToast('تم ضم الأوردرات إلى ' + result.value, 'success');
                                    RW_Data.refresh();
                                } else {
                                    showToast(res.msg || 'فشل الضم', 'error');
                                }
                            })
                            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                                hideLoader();
                                showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                            })
                            .appendToExistRunsheet(result.value, selected);
                    });
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    showToast('فشل جلب الرانشيتات: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getAllRunsheets();
        }
    }

    function _showOrderDetails(orderId) {
        if (typeof google === 'undefined' || !google.script.run) {
            showToast('الخادم غير متصل', 'error');
            return;
        }

        var order = null;
        var orders = RW_STATE.data.orders || [];
        for (var i = 0; i < orders.length; i++) {
            if (orders[i].orderId === orderId) { order = orders[i]; break; }
        }
        if (!order) {
            showToast('الأوردر غير موجود في الذاكرة', 'error');
            return;
        }

        showLoader('جاري تحميل تفاصيل الأوردر...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                hideLoader();
                var items = res.items || [];
                var deliveryFee = res.deliveryFee || 0;

                var warningHtml = '';
                if (order.runsheetId && order.runsheetId !== '') {
                    warningHtml = '<div class="bg-amber-50 border-r-4 border-amber-500 p-3 mb-4 rounded"><p class="text-amber-700 text-sm"><i class="fa-solid fa-link ml-2"></i> مرتبط بالرانشيت: ' + _escapeHtml(order.runsheetId) + '</p></div>';
                }

                var itemsHtml = '';
                var itemsTotal = 0;
                if (items.length > 0) {
                    itemsHtml = '<table class="w-full border"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-2 border">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الوحدة</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">السعر</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الإجمالي</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                    for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                        var it = items[i];
                        var lineTotal = Number(it.total) || (Number(it.qty) * Number(it.price));
                        itemsTotal += lineTotal;
                        itemsHtml += '<tr><td class="p-2 border font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(it.name) + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + (it.unit || 'حبة') + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + it.qty + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + Number(it.price).toLocaleString() + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + Number(lineTotal).toLocaleString() + '</td></tr>';
                    }
                    itemsHtml += '</tbody></table>';
                } else {
                    itemsHtml = '<div class="text-center py-4 text-gray-500">لا توجد أصناف مسجلة لهذا الأوردر</div>';
                }

                var grandTotal = itemsTotal + deliveryFee;

                var html = '<div class="text-right">' + warningHtml;
                html += '<div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-2xl mb-4">';
                html += '<div><p><b>العميل:</b> ' + _escapeHtml(order.custName || '') + '</p><p><b>المنطقة:</b> ' + _escapeHtml(order.area || '') + '</p></div>';
                html += '<div><p><b>الحالة:</b> ' + _escapeHtml(order.status || '') + '</p><p><b>الرانشيت:</b> ' + (order.runsheetId || '---') + '</p></div>';
                html += '</div>';
                html += '<div class="overflow-x-auto">' + itemsHtml + '</div>';
                html += '<div class="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-2xl mt-4">';
                html += '<div class="flex justify-between mb-2"><span>مجموع الأصناف:</span><span>' + Number(itemsTotal).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</span></div>';
                html += '<div class="flex justify-between mb-2 text-blue-600"><span>رسوم التوصيل:</span><span>' + Number(deliveryFee).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</span></div>';
                html += '<div class="flex justify-between pt-2 border-t font-bold"><span>الإجمالي:</span><span class="text-emerald-600 text-lg">' + Number(grandTotal).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</span></div>';
                html += '</div>';
                html += '<div class="flex justify-center gap-3 mt-6 pt-4 border-t"><button id="btn-delete-order-modal" class="bg-red-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash ml-2"></i> حذف الأوردر</button><button id="btn-print-order-modal" class="bg-emerald-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-print ml-2"></i> طباعة الفاتورة</button></div>';
                html += '</div>';

                Swal.fire({
                    title: 'تفاصيل الأوردر: ' + _escapeHtml(orderId),
                    html: html,
                    width: '900px',
                    showCloseButton: true,
                    showConfirmButton: false,
                    showCancelButton: true,
                    cancelButtonText: 'إغلاق',
                    didOpen: function() {
                        var deleteBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-order-modal');
                        var printBtn = document.getElementById('btn-print-order-modal');
                        if (deleteBtn) {
                            deleteBtn.onclick = function() {
                                Swal.close();
                                _deleteOrder(orderId);
                            };
                        }
                        if (printBtn) {
                            printBtn.onclick = function() {
                                _printOrder(orderId);
                            };
                        }
                    }
                });
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                hideLoader();
                showToast('فشل تحميل التفاصيل: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .getOrderDetailsFromServer(orderId);
    }

    function _printOrder(orderId) {
        var order = null;
        var orders = RW_STATE.data.orders || [];
        for (var i = 0; i < orders.length; i++) {
            if (orders[i].orderId === orderId) { order = orders[i]; break; }
        }
        if (!order) return;

        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                var items = res.items || [];
                var deliveryFee = Number(res.deliveryFee) || 0;

                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(settings) {
                        var taxRate = Number(settings.taxRate) || 0;
                        var companyName = settings.companyName || RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
                        var vatNumber = '310000000000003';
                        _buildPrintWindow(order, items, deliveryFee, taxRate, companyName, vatNumber);
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function() {
                        var taxRate = 0;
                        var companyName = RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
                        var vatNumber = '310000000000003';
                        _buildPrintWindow(order, items, deliveryFee, taxRate, companyName, vatNumber);
                    })
                    .getAppSettings();
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                showToast('فشل تحميل بيانات الطباعة: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .getOrderDetailsFromServer(orderId);
    }

    function _buildPrintWindow(order, items, deliveryFee, taxRate, companyName, vatNumber) {
        var printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
        if (!printWindow) { showToast('الرجاء السماح بالنوافذ المنبثقة', 'warning'); return; }

        var itemsTotal = 0;
        var itemsHtml = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            var it = items[i];
            var lineTotal = Number(it.total) || (Number(it.qty) * Number(it.price));
            itemsTotal += lineTotal;
            itemsHtml += '<tr><td class="border p-2">' + _escapeHtml(it.name) + '</td><td class="border p-2 text-center">' + (it.unit || 'حبة') + '</td><td class="border p-2 text-center">' + it.qty + '</td><td class="border p-2 text-center">' + Number(it.price).toLocaleString() + '</td><td class="border p-2 text-center">' + Number(lineTotal).toLocaleString() + '</td></tr>';
        }
        var grandTotal = itemsTotal + deliveryFee;
        var beforeTax = itemsTotal + deliveryFee;
        var taxAmount = Math.round(beforeTax * taxRate) / 100;

        // QR Code يظهر دائماً لجميع الفواتير
        var qrBase64 = generateQRInvoiceBase64(companyName, vatNumber, new Date().toISOString(), String(grandTotal), String(taxAmount));
        var qrCodeSection = '<div style="text-align:center;margin-top:20px;padding-top:15px;border-top:1px dashed #ccc;">' +
            '<p style="font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:8px;">رمز الفاتورة الإلكترونية</p>' +
            '<div id="print-qrcode-container" style="display:inline-block;"></div>' +
            '<p style="font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-top:8px;">امسح الكود للتحقق من الفاتورة</p>' +
            '</div>';

        var html = '<!DOCTYPE html><html dir="rtl"><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><title>فاتورة ' + _escapeHtml(order.orderId) + '</title>' +
            '<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/qrcodejs@1.0.0/qrcode.min.js"><\/script>' +
            '<style>body{font-family:"Cairo",sans-serif;padding:20px}.header{text-align:center;border-bottom:2px solid #000;padding-bottom:10px}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse}th,td{border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;text-align:right}th{background:#f2f2f2}.total{font-weight:bold;font-size:18px;margin-top:20px}</style></head>' +
            '<body><div class="header"><h1>فاتورة بيع</h1><p>رقم: ' + _escapeHtml(order.orderId) + '</p><p>التاريخ: ' + (order.date ? new Date(order.date).toLocaleDateString('ar-EG') : '') + '</p></div>' +
            '<p><strong>العميل:</strong> ' + _escapeHtml(order.custName || '') + '</p><p><strong>المنطقة:</strong> ' + _escapeHtml(order.area || '') + '</p>' +
            '<table><thead><tr><th>الصنف</th><th>الوحدة</th><th>الكمية</th><th>السعر</th><th>الإجمالي</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + itemsHtml + '</tbody></table>' +
            '<div class="total">الإجمالي: ' + Number(order.total || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div>' +
            qrCodeSection +
            '<div style="margin-top:50px;text-align:center;">شكراً لتعاملكم معنا</div>' +
            '<script>window.onload=function(){' +
            'try{var c=document.getElementById("print-qrcode-container");if(c&&typeof QRCode!=="undefined"){c.innerHTML="";new QRCode(c,{text:"' + qrBase64 + '",width:150,height:150,colorDark:"#000000",colorLight:"#ffffff",correctLevel:QRCode.CorrectLevel.M});}}catch(e){}' +
            'window.print();};<\/script></body></html>';
        printWindow.document.write(html);
        printWindow.document.close();
    }

    function _deleteOrder(orderId) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف',
            text: 'هل أنت متأكد من إلغاء الأوردر ' + orderId + '؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، ألغِ',
            cancelButtonText: 'تراجع'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري إلغاء الأوردر...');
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (res.status === 'success') {
                        // تحديث محلي فوري
                        var orders = RW_STATE.data.orders || [];
                        var found = false;
                        for (var i = 0; i < orders.length; i++) {
                            if (orders[i].orderId === orderId) {
                                orders[i].status = 'Cancelled';
                                found = true;
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                        if (found) {
                            _applyFilters(); // يعيد عرض الجدول بالحالة الجديدة
                        }
                        showToast('تم إلغاء الأوردر', 'success');
                    } else {
                        showToast(res.msg || 'فشل الإلغاء', 'error');
                    }
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .deleteOrder(orderId);
        });
    }

    function _sortTable(field) {
        if (currentSort.field === field) {
            currentSort.asc = !currentSort.asc;
        } else {
            currentSort.field = field;
            currentSort.asc = true;
        }
        _applyFilters();
    }

    return {
        render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;

            safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'أوردرات المبيعات');
            safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'عرض وإدارة جميع أوردرات المبيعات');

            var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center gap-2 mb-3"><h3 class="font-bold text-lg">فلترة الأوردرات</h3><div class="flex gap-2"><button onclick="window.RW_Orders._applyFilters()" class="bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm font-bold">تحديث</button><button onclick="window.RW_Orders._showOrdersWithoutRunsheet()" class="bg-amber-50 text-amber-600 px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm font-bold">بدون رانشيت</button><button onclick="window.RW_Orders._resetFilters()" class="bg-gray-50 text-gray-600 px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm font-bold">إعادة تعيين</button></div></div><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2"><input type="date" id="filter-date-from" onchange="window.RW_Orders._applyFilters()" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm"><input type="date" id="filter-date-to" onchange="window.RW_Orders._applyFilters()" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm"><input type="text" id="filter-cust" oninput="window.RW_Orders._applyFilters()" placeholder="العميل" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm"><select id="filter-status" onchange="window.RW_Orders._applyFilters()" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm"><option value="">الحالة</option><option>Draft</option><option>Confirmed</option><option>Pending</option><option>Invoiced</option><option>Delivered</option><option>Returned</option><option>Cancelled</option></select><input type="text" id="filter-area" oninput="window.RW_Orders._applyFilters()" placeholder="المنطقة" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm"><input type="text" id="filter-rs" oninput="window.RW_Orders._applyFilters()" placeholder="الرانشيت" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm"></div></div><div class="flex flex-wrap gap-3 mb-4"><button onclick="window.RW_Orders._createNewRunsheet()" class="bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-bold shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-truck-fast ml-2"></i> رانشيت جديد</button><button onclick="window.RW_Orders._appendToExistingRunsheet()" class="bg-emerald-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-bold shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-folder-plus ml-2"></i> ضم لرانشيت مفتوح</button></div><div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1200px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0 z-10"><tr><th class="p-3 text-center"><input type="checkbox" id="check-all-orders" class="rounded" onchange="var cbs=document.querySelectorAll(\'.order-checkbox\'); for(var i=0;i<cbs.length;i++)cbs[i].checked=this.checked;"></th><th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Orders._sortTable(\'orderId\')">رقم الأوردر <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th><th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Orders._sortTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th><th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Orders._sortTable(\'custName\')">العميل والمنطقة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th><th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Orders._sortTable(\'itemsAmount\')">عدد الأصناف <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th><th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Orders._sortTable(\'total\')">القيمة (EGP) <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th><th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Orders._sortTable(\'status\')">الحالة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th><th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Orders._sortTable(\'runsheetId\')">الرانشيت <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th></tr></thead><tbody id="orders-table-body"><tr><td colspan="9" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>';

            safeHTML(container, html);
            _applyFilters();
        },
        _applyFilters: _applyFilters,
        _resetFilters: _resetFilters,
        _showOrdersWithoutRunsheet: _showOrdersWithoutRunsheet,
        _createNewRunsheet: _createNewRunsheet,
        _appendToExistingRunsheet: _appendToExistingRunsheet,
        _showOrderDetails: _showOrderDetails,
        _printOrder: _printOrder,
        _deleteOrder: _deleteOrder,
        _sortTable: _sortTable
    };
})();
window.RW_Orders = RW_Orders;
// ============================================================
// RW_Runsheets – تبويب الرانشيتات (متكامل مع الخلفية)
// ============================================================
var RW_Runsheets = (function() {
    'use strict';

    var currentSort = { field: 'rsId', asc: true };

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _renderTable(runsheets) {
        var tbody = byId('runsheets-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;

        var data = runsheets || RW_STATE.data.runsheets || [];
        if (data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد رانشيتات</td></tr>');
            return;
        }

        var sorted = data.slice().sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[currentSort.field] || '', vb = b[currentSort.field] || '';
            if (currentSort.field === 'totalAmount' || currentSort.field === 'orderCount') {
                va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb);
            } else if (currentSort.field === 'date') {
                va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb);
            } else {
                va = String(va).toLowerCase(); vb = String(vb).toLowerCase();
            }
            if (va < vb) return currentSort.asc ? -1 : 1;
            if (va > vb) return currentSort.asc ? 1 : -1;
            return 0;
        });

        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < sorted.length; i++) {
            var rs = sorted[i];
            var statusClass = '';
            if (rs.status === 'Open') statusClass = 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-700';
            else if (rs.status === 'Picking' || rs.status === 'Picked') statusClass = 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-700';
            else if (rs.status === 'Loading' || rs.status === 'Loaded') statusClass = 'bg-orange-100 text-orange-700';
            else if (rs.status === 'Delivering' || rs.status === 'Delivered') statusClass = 'bg-green-100 text-green-700';
            else if (rs.status === 'Returning' || rs.status === 'Returned') statusClass = 'bg-red-100 text-red-700';
            else statusClass = 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-700';

            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Runsheets._showDetails(\'' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId) + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold text-emerald-600">' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + (rs.date ? new Date(rs.date).toLocaleDateString('ar-EG') : '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(rs.driverEmail || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(rs.vehicleId || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (rs.orderCount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(rs.totalAmount || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold ' + statusClass + '">' + _escapeHtml(rs.status || '') + '</span></td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _applyFilters() {
        var data = RW_STATE.data.runsheets || [];
        var idEl = document.getElementById('rs-filter-id');
        var id = idEl ? (idEl.value || '').toLowerCase() : '';
        var stEl = document.getElementById('rs-filter-status');
        var st = stEl ? stEl.value : '';
        var driverEl = document.getElementById('rs-filter-driver');
        var driver = driverEl ? (driverEl.value || '').toLowerCase() : '';
        var fdEl = document.getElementById('rs-filter-date-from');
        var fd = fdEl ? fdEl.value : '';
        var tdEl = document.getElementById('rs-filter-date-to');
        var td = tdEl ? tdEl.value : '';

        var filtered = data;
        if (id) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.rsId && (r.rsId.toLowerCase().indexOf(id) !== -1); }); }
        if (st) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.status === st; }); }
        if (driver) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.driverEmail && (r.driverEmail.toLowerCase().indexOf(driver) !== -1); }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date <= td; }); }
        _renderTable(filtered);
    }

    function _showDetails(rsId) {
        if (typeof google === 'undefined' || !google.script.run) {
            showToast('الخادم غير متصل', 'error');
            return;
        }

        showLoader('جاري تحميل تفاصيل الرانشيت...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                hideLoader();
                var orders = data.orders || [];
                var items = data.items || [];

                var ordersHtml = '';
                if (orders.length > 0) {
                    ordersHtml = '<div class="mb-4"><h4 class="font-bold text-lg mb-2">الأوردرات المرتبطة (' + orders.length + ')</h4><div class="bg-gray-50 rounded-lg p-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2">';
                    for (var i = 0; i < orders.length; i++) {
                        ordersHtml += '<span class="inline-block bg-white rounded px-3 py-1 text-sm shadow-sm">' + _escapeHtml(orders[i].orderId) + ' - ' + _escapeHtml(orders[i].custName) + '</span>';
                    }
                    ordersHtml += '</div></div>';
                } else {
                    ordersHtml = '<div class="mb-4 text-gray-500">لا توجد أوردرات مرتبطة</div>';
                }

                var itemsHtml = '';
                var grandTotal = 0;
                if (items.length > 0) {
                    itemsHtml = '<div class="overflow-x-auto mt-4"><table class="w-full border"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-2 border">الكود</th><th class="p-2 border">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">السعر</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الإجمالي</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                    for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                        var it = items[i];
                        var lineTotal = Number(it.total) || (Number(it.qty) * Number(it.price));
                        grandTotal += lineTotal;
                        itemsHtml += '<tr><td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(it.code || '') + '</td><td class="p-2 border font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(it.name || '') + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + (it.qty || 0) + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + Number(it.price || 0).toLocaleString() + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + Number(lineTotal).toLocaleString() + '</td></tr>';
                    }
                    itemsHtml += '</tbody></table></div>';
                    itemsHtml += '<div class="mt-3 text-left font-bold text-lg">الإجمالي: ' + Number(grandTotal).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div>';
                } else {
                    itemsHtml = '<div class="text-center py-4 text-gray-500">لا توجد أصناف</div>';
                }

                var html = '<div class="text-right">' + ordersHtml + itemsHtml + '</div>';
                html += '<div class="flex justify-center gap-3 mt-6 pt-4 border-t"><button id="btn-print-rs-modal" class="bg-blue-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-print ml-2"></i> طباعة</button><button id="btn-delete-rs-modal" class="bg-red-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash ml-2"></i> حذف</button></div>';

                Swal.fire({
                    title: 'تفاصيل الرانشيت: ' + _escapeHtml(rsId),
                    html: html,
                    width: '900px',
                    showCloseButton: true,
                    showConfirmButton: false,
                    showCancelButton: true,
                    cancelButtonText: 'إغلاق',
                    didOpen: function() {
                        var printBtn = document.getElementById('btn-print-rs-modal');
                        var deleteBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-rs-modal');
                        if (printBtn) {
                            printBtn.onclick = function() {
                                _printManifest(rsId);
                            };
                        }
                        if (deleteBtn) {
                            deleteBtn.onclick = function() {
                                Swal.close();
                                _deleteRunsheet(rsId);
                            };
                        }
                    }
                });
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                hideLoader();
                showToast('فشل تحميل التفاصيل: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .getRunsheetDetailsWithOrders(rsId);
    }
        function _deleteRunsheet(rsId) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف',
            text: 'هل أنت متأكد من حذف الرانشيت ' + rsId + '؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، احذف',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري حذف الرانشيت...');
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (res.status === 'success') {
                        // تحديث محلي فوري
                        var runsheets = RW_STATE.data.runsheets || [];
                        var newRunsheets = [];
                        for (var i = 0; i < runsheets.length; i++) {
                            if (runsheets[i].rsId !== rsId) {
                                newRunsheets.push(runsheets[i]);
                            }
                        }
                        RW_STATE.data.runsheets = newRunsheets;
                        _applyFilters(); // إعادة عرض الجدول
                        showToast('تم حذف الرانشيت', 'success');
                    } else {
                        showToast(res.msg || 'فشل الحذف', 'error');
                    }
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .deleteRunsheetAndFreeOrders(rsId);
        });
    }

    function _printManifest(rsId) {
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                var items = data.items || [];
                var printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
                if (!printWindow) {
                    showToast('الرجاء السماح بالنوافذ المنبثقة', 'warning');
                    return;
                }

                var itemsHtml = '';
                var total = 0;
                for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                    var it = items[i];
                    var lineTotal = Number(it.total) || (Number(it.qty) * Number(it.price));
                    total += lineTotal;
                    itemsHtml += '<tr><td class="border p-2">' + _escapeHtml(it.code || '') + '</td><td class="border p-2">' + _escapeHtml(it.name || '') + '</td><td class="border p-2 text-center">' + (it.qty || 0) + '</td><td class="border p-2 text-center">' + Number(it.price || 0).toLocaleString() + '</td><td class="border p-2 text-center">' + Number(lineTotal).toLocaleString() + '</td></tr>';
                }

                var html = '<!DOCTYPE html><html dir="rtl"><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><title>مانيفست ' + rsId + '</title><style>body{font-family:"Cairo",sans-serif;padding:20px}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse}th,td{border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;text-align:right}th{background:#3b82f6;color:white}</style></head><body><h1>بيان رحلة: ' + rsId + '</h1><table><thead><tr><th>الكود</th><th>الصنف</th><th>الكمية</th><th>السعر</th><th>الإجمالي</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + itemsHtml + '</tbody></table><div style="font-weight:bold;font-size:20px;margin-top:20px">الإجمالي: ' + Number(total).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div><script>window.print();<\/script></body></html>';
                printWindow.document.write(html);
                printWindow.document.close();
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                showToast('فشل تحميل بيانات الطباعة: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .getRunsheetDetailsWithOrders(rsId);
    }

    function _sortTable(field) {
        if (currentSort.field === field) {
            currentSort.asc = !currentSort.asc;
        } else {
            currentSort.field = field;
            currentSort.asc = true;
        }
        _applyFilters();
    }

    return {
        render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;

            safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الرانشيتات');
            safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'عرض وإدارة جميع الرانشيتات');

            var html = '<div class="p-4"><div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2">';
            html += '<input type="text" id="rs-filter-id" placeholder="رقم الرانشيت..." class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Runsheets._applyFilters()">';
            html += '<select id="rs-filter-status" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Runsheets._applyFilters()"><option value="">الحالة</option><option>Open</option><option>Picking</option><option>Picked</option><option>Loading</option><option>Loaded</option><option>Delivering</option><option>Delivered</option><option>Returning</option><option>Returned</option></select>';
            html += '<input type="text" id="rs-filter-driver" placeholder="السائق..." class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Runsheets._applyFilters()">';
            html += '<input type="date" id="rs-filter-date-from" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Runsheets._applyFilters()">';
            html += '<input type="date" id="rs-filter-date-to" class="p-2 bg-gray-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Runsheets._applyFilters()">';
            html += '<button onclick="RW_Runsheets._applyFilters()" class="bg-gray-600 text-white px-3 rounded text-sm font-bold">تطبيق</button>';
            html += '</div></div>';
            html += '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1000px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0 z-10"><tr>';
            html += '<th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Runsheets._sortTable(\'rsId\')">رقم الرانشيت <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>';
            html += '<th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Runsheets._sortTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>';
            html += '<th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Runsheets._sortTable(\'driverEmail\')">السائق <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>';
            html += '<th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Runsheets._sortTable(\'vehicleId\')">السيارة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>';
            html += '<th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Runsheets._sortTable(\'orderCount\')">عدد الأوردرات <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>';
            html += '<th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Runsheets._sortTable(\'totalAmount\')">القيمة (EGP) <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>';
            html += '<th class="p-3 text-center cursor-pointer text-xs font-bold uppercase" onclick="RW_Runsheets._sortTable(\'status\')">الحالة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>';
            html += '</tr></thead><tbody id="runsheets-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>';

            safeHTML(container, html);
            _applyFilters();
        },
        _applyFilters: _applyFilters,
        _showDetails: _showDetails,
        _printManifest: _printManifest,
        _sortTable: _sortTable,
        _deleteRunsheet: _deleteRunsheet    };
})();
window.RW_Runsheets = RW_Runsheets;

// ============================================================
// RW_POS – تبويب نقطة البيع (POS) – كاشير الفرع
// ============================================================
var RW_POS = (function() {
    'use strict';

    var posCart = [];
    var deliveryFeeValue = 0;
    var minInvoiceAmount = 0;
    var taxRate = 0;

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _loadSettings() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
                    deliveryFeeValue = Number(s.deliveryFee) || 0;
                    minInvoiceAmount = Number(s.minInvoiceAmount) || 0;
                    taxRate = Number(s.taxRate) || 0;
                    _renderCart();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    console.error('POS: فشل تحميل إعدادات التوصيل:', err);
                    deliveryFeeValue = 0;
                    minInvoiceAmount = 0;
                    taxRate = 0;
                    _renderCart();
                })
                .getAppSettings();
        }
    }

    function _renderCustomerSelect() {
        var select = byId('pos-customer-select');
        if (!select) return;
        var customers = RW_STATE.data.customers || [];
        var html = '<option value="">-- اختر عميلاً --</option>';
        for (var i = 0; i < customers.length; i++) {
            var c = customers[i];
            html += '<option value="' + _escapeHtml(c.code || c.id || '') + '">' + _escapeHtml(c.name || '') + ' (' + _escapeHtml(c.area || '') + ')</option>';
        }
        safeHTML(select, html);
    }

    function _onCustomerChange() {
        var select = byId('pos-customer-select');
        var areaInput = byId('pos-area');
        if (!select || !areaInput) return;
        var customers = RW_STATE.data.customers || [];
        var selected = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < customers.length; i++) {
            if (customers[i].code === select.value || customers[i].id === select.value) {
                selected = customers[i];
                break;
            }
        }
        areaInput.value = selected ? (selected.area || '') : '';
    }

    function _searchItems(query) {
        var dropdown = byId('pos-item-dropdown');
        if (!dropdown) return;
        if (!query || query.trim().length < 1) {
            dropdown.classList.add('hidden');
            return;
        }
        var q = query.toLowerCase();
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
        var filtered = items.filter(function(item) {
            var available = item.availableStock || item.stock || 0;
            return available > 0 && (
                String(item.name || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1 ||
                String(item.code || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1 ||
                String(item.barcode || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1
            );
        });

        if (filtered.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(dropdown, '<div class="p-3 text-center text-gray-400">لا توجد أصناف متاحة</div>');
            dropdown.classList.remove('hidden');
            return;
        }

        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < filtered.length; i++) {
            var item = filtered[i];
            var available = item.availableStock || item.stock || 0;
            html += '<div onclick="RW_POS._addToCart(\'' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '\')" class="p-3 hover:bg-blue-50 cursor-pointer flex justify-between border-b">';
            html += '<div><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(item.name) + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-400">كود: ' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + ' | متاح: ' + available + (item.maxQty > 0 ? ' | حد أقصى: ' + item.maxQty : '') + '</div></div>';
            html += '<div class="font-bold text-blue-600">' + Number(item.sPrice || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div>';
            html += '</div>';
        }
        safeHTML(dropdown, html);
        dropdown.classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    function _addToCart(itemCode) {
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
        var item = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            if (items[i].code === itemCode) { item = items[i]; break; }
        }
        if (!item) return;

        var available = item.availableStock || 0;
        if (available <= 0) {
            showToast('الصنف غير متوفر', 'warning');
            return;
        }

        var existing = null;
        for (var j = 0; j < posCart.length; j++) {
            if (posCart[j].code === itemCode) { existing = posCart[j]; break; }
        }
        var currentQty = existing ? existing.qty : 0;
        if (item.maxQty > 0 && currentQty + 1 > item.maxQty) {
            showToast('لا يمكن إضافة أكثر من ' + item.maxQty, 'warning');
            return;
        }
        if (currentQty + 1 > available) {
            showToast('الرصيد المتاح غير كافٍ (' + available + ')', 'warning');
            return;
        }

        if (existing) {
            existing.qty++;
        } else {
            posCart.unshift({
                code: item.code,
                name: item.name,
                price: Number(item.sPrice) || 0,
                unit: item.unit || 'حبة',
                qty: 1,
                maxQty: item.maxQty || 0,
                availableStock: available
            });
        }

        var searchInput = byId('pos-item-search');
        if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
        var dropdown = byId('pos-item-dropdown');
        if (dropdown) dropdown.classList.add('hidden');
        _renderCart();
    }

    function _updateQty(index, val) {
        var q = parseFloat(val);
        if (isNaN(q) || q <= 0) {
            posCart.splice(index, 1);
        } else {
            var item = posCart[index];
            if (item.maxQty > 0 && q > item.maxQty) {
                showToast('الحد الأقصى: ' + item.maxQty, 'warning');
            } else if (q > (item.availableStock || 0)) {
                showToast('الرصيد المتاح غير كافٍ (' + item.availableStock + ')', 'warning');
            } else {
                posCart[index].qty = q;
            }
        }
        _renderCart();
    }

    function _removeItem(index) {
        posCart.splice(index, 1);
        _renderCart();
    }

    function _clearCart() {
        if (posCart.length === 0) {
            showToast('السلة فارغة بالفعل', 'info');
            return;
        }
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد مسح السلة',
            text: 'سيتم حذف جميع الأصناف من السلة. هل أنت متأكد؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، امسح',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                posCart = [];
                _renderCart();
                showToast('تم مسح السلة', 'success');
            }
        });
    }

    function _renderCart() {
        var tbody = byId('pos-cart-body');
        var subtotalSpan = byId('pos-subtotal');
        var deliverySpan = byId('pos-delivery-fee');
        var totalSpan = byId('pos-total');
        var countSpan = byId('pos-items-count');
        var taxRow = byId('pos-tax-row');
        var taxSpan = byId('pos-tax-amount');
        var grandSpan = byId('pos-grand-total');

        if (posCart.length === 0) {
            if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="5" class="p-6 text-center text-gray-400">لا توجد أصناف في السلة</td></tr>');
            if (subtotalSpan) safeText(subtotalSpan, '0');
            if (deliverySpan) safeText(deliverySpan, '0');
            var deliveryRowEmpty = byId('pos-delivery-row');
            if (deliveryRowEmpty) deliveryRowEmpty.classList.add('hidden');
            if (totalSpan) safeText(totalSpan, '0');
            if (countSpan) safeText(countSpan, '0');
            if (taxRow) taxRow.classList.add('hidden');
            if (grandSpan) safeText(grandSpan, '0');
            return;
        }

        var subtotal = 0;
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < posCart.length; i++) {
            var item = posCart[i];
            var line = item.price * item.qty;
            subtotal += line;
            html += '<tr class="bg-white shadow-sm rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">';
            html += '<td class="p-4 rounded-r-2xl border-y border-r"><p class="font-black text-slate-700">' + _escapeHtml(item.name) + '</p><p class="text-xs text-slate-400">' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '</p></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-4 border-y font-bold text-blue-600">' + Number(item.price).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-4 border-y"><input type="number" value="' + item.qty + '" onchange="RW_POS._updateQty(' + i + ', this.value)" class="w-20 p-2 bg-slate-50 border-2 rounded-xl text-center font-black outline-none" min="1" max="' + (item.maxQty || 999) + '"></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-4 border-y font-black text-slate-800">' + Number(line).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-4 rounded-l-2xl border-y border-l text-center"><button onclick="RW_POS._removeItem(' + i + ')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-600"><i class="fa-solid fa-circle-xmark text-xl"></i></button></td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        var delivery = deliveryFeeValue || 0;
        var beforeTax = subtotal + delivery;
        var taxAmount = Math.round(beforeTax * taxRate) / 100;
        var grandTotal = beforeTax + taxAmount;

        if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, html);
        if (subtotalSpan) safeText(subtotalSpan, Number(subtotal).toLocaleString());
            var deliveryRow = byId('pos-delivery-row');
            if (deliveryRow) {
                if (delivery > 0) {
                    deliveryRow.classList.remove('hidden');
                    if (deliverySpan) safeText(deliverySpan, Number(delivery).toLocaleString());
                } else {
                    deliveryRow.classList.add('hidden');
                }
            }
        if (taxRow) {
            if (taxRate > 0 && subtotal > 0) {
                taxRow.classList.remove('hidden');
                if (taxSpan) safeText(taxSpan, Number(taxAmount).toLocaleString());
            } else {
                taxRow.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        }
        if (totalSpan) safeText(totalSpan, Number(beforeTax).toLocaleString());
        if (grandSpan) safeText(grandSpan, Number(grandTotal).toLocaleString());
        if (countSpan) safeText(countSpan, String(posCart.length));
    }

    function _processFinalOrder() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
                    taxRate = Number(s.taxRate) || 0;
                    deliveryFeeValue = Number(s.deliveryFee) || 0;
                    RW_POS._companyName = s.companyName || RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
                    RW_POS._vatNumber = '310000000000003';
                    _processFinalOrderAfterLoad();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function() {
                    RW_POS._companyName = RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
                    RW_POS._vatNumber = '310000000000003';
