                    _processFinalOrderAfterLoad();
                })
                .getAppSettings();
        } else {
            RW_POS._companyName = RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
            RW_POS._vatNumber = '310000000000003';
            _processFinalOrderAfterLoad();
        }
    }

    function _processFinalOrderAfterLoad() {
        var select = byId('pos-customer-select');
        var custId = select ? select.value : '';
        if (!custId) { showToast('اختر عميلاً أولاً', 'warning'); return; }
        if (posCart.length === 0) { showToast('أضف أصنافاً إلى السلة', 'warning'); return; }

        var subtotal = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < posCart.length; i++) { subtotal += posCart[i].price * posCart[i].qty; }
        var delivery = deliveryFeeValue || 0;
        var beforeTax = subtotal + delivery;
        var taxAmount = Math.round(beforeTax * taxRate) / 100;
        var grandTotal = beforeTax + taxAmount;

        if (minInvoiceAmount > 0 && grandTotal < minInvoiceAmount) { showToast('الحد الأدنى للفاتورة: ' + minInvoiceAmount + ' EGP', 'warning'); return; }

        var customers = RW_STATE.data.customers || [];
        var customer = null;
        for (var j = 0; j < customers.length; j++) { if (customers[j].code === custId || customers[j].id === custId) { customer = customers[j]; break; } }

        var orderHeader = {
            custId: custId, custName: customer ? customer.name : '', area: customer ? customer.area : '',
            total: grandTotal, deliveryFees: delivery, status: "Invoiced", paymentType: "نقدي",
            taxAmount: taxAmount, taxRate: taxRate
        };

        var itemsList = posCart.map(function(item) { return { code: item.code, name: item.name, price: item.price, qty: item.qty, unit: item.unit }; });
        var branchId = (RW_STATE.app.currentUser && RW_STATE.app.currentUser.defaultBranch) || "MAIN";

        var finalTaxAmount = taxAmount;
        var finalGrandTotal = grandTotal;
        var finalTaxRate = taxRate;
        var finalCompanyName = RW_POS._companyName || 'الروائع';
        var finalVatNumber = RW_POS._vatNumber || '310000000000003';

        showLoader('جاري حفظ الفاتورة...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (res.status === 'success') {
                        var orderId = res.orderID || '';
                        if (orderId) {
                            var invoiceDate = new Date().toISOString();
                            var qrBase64 = generateQRInvoiceBase64(finalCompanyName, finalVatNumber, invoiceDate, String(finalGrandTotal), String(finalTaxAmount));

                            var qrHtml = '<div style="text-align:center;margin-top:15px;">';
                            qrHtml += '<p style="font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:8px;">رمز الفاتورة الإلكترونية</p>';
                            qrHtml += '<div id="pos-qrcode-container" style="display:inline-block;"></div>';
                            qrHtml += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:#6b7280;margin-top:8px;">امسح الكود للتحقق من الفاتورة</p>';
                            qrHtml += '</div>';

                            Swal.fire({
                                title: 'تم الحفظ',
                                html: '<p style="text-align:center;">رقم الفاتورة: <strong>' + orderId + '</strong></p>' + qrHtml,
                                icon: 'success',
                                timer: 4000,
                                showConfirmButton: true,
                                confirmButtonText: 'حسناً',
                                didOpen: function() {
                                    try {
                                        var container = document.getElementById('pos-qrcode-container');
                                        if (container && typeof QRCode !== 'undefined') {
                                            container.innerHTML = '';
                                            new QRCode(container, {
                                                text: qrBase64,
                                                width: 150,
                                                height: 150,
                                                colorDark: '#000000',
                                                colorLight: '#ffffff',
                                                correctLevel: QRCode.CorrectLevel.M
                                            });
                                        }
                                    } catch(e) { console.error('QR Code error:', e); }
                                }
                            });
                        } else {
                            Swal.fire({ title: 'تم', text: 'رقم الفاتورة: ' + orderId, icon: 'success', timer: 2500, showConfirmButton: false });
                        }
                        posCart = [];
                        _renderCart();
                        if (select) select.value = '';
                        _onCustomerChange();
                        RW_Data.refresh();
                    }
                    else { showToast(res.msg || 'فشل حفظ الفاتورة', 'error'); }
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
                .saveSalesInvoice(orderHeader, itemsList, branchId);
        } else { hideLoader(); showToast('تمت محاكاة البيع (غير متصل)', 'info'); posCart = []; _renderCart(); if (select) select.value = ''; _onCustomerChange(); }
    }

    function _renderUI(container) {
        var html = '<div class="max-w-[1400px] mx-auto grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6 p-6">';
        html += '<div class="lg:col-span-1 space-y-6">';
        html += '<div class="bg-white p-6 rounded-[30px] shadow-sm"><label class="text-xs font-black text-slate-400 mb-2 block uppercase">1. اختيار العميل</label><select id="pos-customer-select" onchange="RW_POS._onCustomerChange()" class="w-full p-4 bg-slate-50 rounded-2xl border-none outline-none font-bold"><option value="">-- اختر عميلاً --</option></select><div class="mt-4 p-4 bg-blue-50 rounded-2xl"><p class="text-xs text-blue-400 font-black">المنطقة</p><input id="pos-area" readonly class="bg-transparent font-bold text-blue-800 outline-none w-full" placeholder="---"></div></div>';
        html += '<div class="bg-white p-6 rounded-[30px] shadow-sm relative border-2 border-blue-50"><label class="text-xs font-black text-blue-400 mb-2 block uppercase">البحث عن صنف</label><div class="relative"><input type="text" id="pos-item-search" oninput="RW_POS._searchItems(this.value)" autocomplete="off" placeholder="أدخل اسم الصنف أو الباركود..." class="w-full p-4 bg-slate-50 rounded-2xl border-2 border-transparent focus:border-blue-600 focus:bg-white outline-none font-bold text-lg transition-all"><div id="pos-item-dropdown" class="absolute z-[9999] left-0 right-0 mt-2 bg-white shadow-2xl rounded-2xl max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto hidden border border-slate-100"></div></div></div>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '<div class="lg:col-span-3 bg-white rounded-[40px] shadow-xl overflow-hidden flex flex-col min-h-[600px]">';
        html += '<div class="p-6 bg-slate-800 text-white flex justify-between items-center"><h2 class="font-black text-xl">قائمة طلب البيع</h2><div><p class="text-xs opacity-60">إجمالي البنود</p><p id="pos-items-count" class="text-xl font-black">0</p></div></div>';
        html += '<div class="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6"><table class="w-full text-right border-separate border-spacing-y-3"><thead><tr class="text-slate-400 text-xs font-black uppercase tracking-widest"><th class="px-4">الصنف</th><th class="px-4">السعر (EGP)</th><th class="px-4 w-32">الكمية</th><th class="px-4">الإجمالي (EGP)</th><th class="px-4"></th></tr></thead><tbody id="pos-cart-body"></tbody></table></div>';
        html += '<div class="p-8 bg-slate-50 border-t flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center gap-6">';
        html += '<div><div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-2"><span class="text-slate-400 font-bold ml-4">مجموع الأصناف:</span><span id="pos-subtotal" class="text-xl font-bold text-slate-600">0</span></div><div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-2" id="pos-delivery-row"><span class="text-slate-400 font-bold ml-4">رسوم التوصيل:</span><span id="pos-delivery-fee" class="text-xl font-bold text-blue-600">0</span></div><div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-2" id="pos-tax-row"><span class="text-slate-400 font-bold ml-4">ضريبة القيمة المضافة:</span><span id="pos-tax-amount" class="text-xl font-bold text-red-600">0</span></div><div class="flex justify-between items-center"><span class="text-slate-400 font-bold ml-4">الإجمالي النهائي:</span><span id="pos-grand-total" class="text-5xl font-black text-emerald-700">0.00</span></div></div>';
        html += '<div class="flex gap-3"><button onclick="RW_POS._clearCart()" class="bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600 text-white px-8 py-5 rounded-2xl font-black text-lg shadow">مسح الكل</button><button onclick="RW_POS._processFinalOrder()" class="bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white px-16 py-5 rounded-2xl font-black text-xl shadow-lg">حفظ الفاتورة</button></div>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '</div>';

        safeHTML(container, html);
        _renderCustomerSelect();
        _renderCart();
    }

    return {
        render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;
            safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'نقطة البيع');
            safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'الكاشير – بيع مباشر مع خصم فوري من المخزون');

            posCart = [];
            _loadSettings();

            var self = this;
            if (!RW_STATE.data.items || RW_STATE.data.items.length === 0) {
                showLoader('جاري تحميل الأصناف...');
                if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script.run) {
                    google.script.run
                        .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                            hideLoader();
                            RW_STATE.data.items = data || [];
                            self._renderUI(container);
                        })
                        .withFailureHandler(function() {
                            hideLoader();
                            self._renderUI(container);
                        })
                        .loadItemsData(1, 500);
                } else {
                    hideLoader();
                    self._renderUI(container);
                }
            } else {
                self._renderUI(container);
            }
        },

        _renderUI: _renderUI,
        _searchItems: _searchItems,
        _addToCart: _addToCart,
        _updateQty: _updateQty,
        _removeItem: _removeItem,
        _clearCart: _clearCart,
        _onCustomerChange: _onCustomerChange,
        _processFinalOrder: _processFinalOrder
    };
})();
window.RW_POS = RW_POS;
var RW_OnlineStore = (function() {
    'use strict';

    var cart = {};
    var activeCategory = 'الكل';
    var deliveryFeeValue = 0;
    var taxRate = 0;
    var lastCustomerData = { name: '', phone: '', area: '', notes: '' };

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    function _loadStoreSettings() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
                    deliveryFeeValue = Number(s.deliveryFee) || 0;
                    taxRate = Number(s.taxRate) || 0;
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    console.error('OnlineStore: فشل تحميل إعدادات التوصيل:', err);
                    deliveryFeeValue = 0;
                    taxRate = 0;
                })
                .getAppSettings();
        }
    }

    function _clearCart() {
        if (Object.keys(cart).length === 0) {
            showToast('السلة فارغة بالفعل', 'info');
            return;
        }
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد مسح السلة',
            text: 'سيتم حذف جميع الأصناف من السلة. هل أنت متأكد؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#d33',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، امسح',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                cart = {};
                _renderProductCards();
                showToast('تم مسح السلة', 'success');
            }
        });
    }

    function _renderProductCards() {
    var grid = byId('online-store-grid');
    if (!grid) return;

    var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
    var searchInput = byId('online-store-search');
    var searchQuery = '';
    if (searchInput) {
        searchQuery = (searchInput.value || '').toLowerCase();
    }

    var filtered = items.filter(function(item) {
        var matchCat = (activeCategory === 'الكل' || item.cat === activeCategory);
        var matchSearch = true;
        if (searchQuery) {
            matchSearch = String(item.name || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(searchQuery) !== -1 ||
                          String(item.code || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(searchQuery) !== -1;
        }
        var showInStore = (item.showInStore !== false);
        return matchCat && matchSearch && showInStore;
    });

    if (filtered.length === 0) {
        safeHTML(grid, '<div class="col-span-full text-center py-10 text-gray-400">لا توجد منتجات</div>');
        return;
    }

    var html = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < filtered.length; i++) {
        var item = filtered[i];
        var qty = cart[item.code] || 0;
        var imgSrc = item.image || 'https://via.placeholder.com/150';

        html += '<div class="bg-white rounded-xl p-3 border cursor-pointer shadow-sm hover:shadow-md transition-shadow" onclick="RW_OnlineStore._showProduct(\'' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '\')">';
        html += '<img src="' + imgSrc + '" class="w-full h-35 object-cover rounded-lg mb-2">';
        html += '<div class="font-bold text-sm">' + _escapeHtml(item.name || '') + '</div>';
        html += '<div class="font-black text-blue-600 mb-2">' + Number(item.sPrice || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div>';

        if (qty === 0) {
            html += '<button onclick="event.stopPropagation(); RW_OnlineStore._addToCart(\'' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '\')" class="bg-blue-600 text-white w-full py-1 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold">إضافة للسلة</button>';
        } else {
            html += '<div class="flex items-center justify-between bg-slate-100 rounded-lg px-2 py-1">';
            html += '<button onclick="event.stopPropagation(); RW_OnlineStore._updateCart(\'' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '\', -1)" class="text-lg font-bold text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700">-</button>';
            html += '<span class="font-black text-blue-600">' + qty + '</span>';
            html += '<button onclick="event.stopPropagation(); RW_OnlineStore._updateCart(\'' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '\', 1)" class="text-lg font-bold text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700">+</button>';
            html += '</div>';
        }
        html += '</div>';
    }
    safeHTML(grid, html);
    _updateBadge();
}

    function _addToCart(code) {
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items;
        if (!items) return;
        var item = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            if (items[i].code === code) { item = items[i]; break; }
        }
        if (!item) return;
        cart[code] = (cart[code] || 0) + 1;
        _renderProductCards();
    }

    function _updateCart(code, delta) {
        var current = cart[code] || 0;
        var newQty = current + delta;
        if (newQty <= 0) {
            delete cart[code];
        } else {
            cart[code] = newQty;
        }
        _renderProductCards();
    }

    function _updateBadge() {
        var badge = byId('online-cart-badge');
        if (!badge) return;
        var total = 0;
        for (var k in cart) {
            total += cart[k];
        }
        safeText(badge, total);
    }

    function _updateCartFromModal(code, delta) {
        _updateCart(code, delta);
        var container = Swal.getHtmlContainer();
        if (!container) return;

        var itemsArr = [];
        var subtotal = 0;
        for (var c in cart) {
            var items = RW_STATE.data.items;
            if (!items) continue;
            var itm = null;
            for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                if (items[i].code === c) { itm = items[i]; break; }
            }
            if (!itm) continue;
            var qty = cart[c];
            var price = Number(itm.sPrice) || 0;
            var line = price * qty;
            subtotal += line;
            itemsArr.push({ code: c, name: itm.name, qty: qty, price: price });
        }

        if (itemsArr.length === 0) {
            Swal.close();
            _renderProductCards();
            return;
        }

        container.innerHTML = _getCartModalHTML(itemsArr, subtotal);
        _renderProductCards();
    }

    function _getCartModalHTML(itemsArr, subtotal, customerData) {
        var cust = customerData || { name: '', phone: '', area: '', notes: '' };
        var delivery = deliveryFeeValue || 0;
        var beforeTax = subtotal + delivery;
        var taxAmount = Math.round(beforeTax * taxRate) / 100;
        var grandTotal = beforeTax + taxAmount;
        var itemsHtml = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < itemsArr.length; i++) {
            var ci = itemsArr[i];
            itemsHtml += '<div class="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl mb-2">';
            itemsHtml += '<div class="flex-1"><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(ci.name) + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-500">' + Number(ci.price).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div></div>';
            itemsHtml += '<div class="flex items-center gap-2">';
            itemsHtml += '<button onclick="RW_OnlineStore._updateCartFromModal(\'' + _escapeHtml(ci.code) + '\', -1)" class="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-300 font-bold">-</button>';
            itemsHtml += '<span class="font-black w-8 text-center">' + ci.qty + '</span>';
            itemsHtml += '<button onclick="RW_OnlineStore._updateCartFromModal(\'' + _escapeHtml(ci.code) + '\', 1)" class="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-300 font-bold">+</button>';
            itemsHtml += '</div>';
            itemsHtml += '<div class="text-left font-bold text-blue-600">' + Number(ci.qty * ci.price).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div>';
            itemsHtml += '</div>';
        }

        var html = '<div class="text-right space-y-3">';
        html += itemsHtml;
        html += '<div class="border-t pt-3 mt-3">';
        html += '<div class="flex justify-between mb-2"><span class="font-bold">المجموع الفرعي:</span><span>' + Number(subtotal).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</span></div>';
        if (delivery > 0) {
            html += '<div class="flex justify-between mb-2"><span class="font-bold text-blue-600">رسوم التوصيل:</span><span class="text-blue-600">' + Number(delivery).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</span></div>';
        }
        if (taxRate > 0 && subtotal > 0) {
            html += '<div class="flex justify-between mb-2"><span class="font-bold text-red-600">ضريبة القيمة المضافة (' + Number(taxRate).toFixed(2) + '%)</span><span class="text-red-600">' + Number(taxAmount).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</span></div>';
        }
        html += '<div class="flex justify-between mb-4"><span class="font-black text-lg">الإجمالي الكلي:</span><span class="font-black text-lg text-emerald-600">' + Number(grandTotal).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</span></div>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '<button id="clear-cart-btn" class="w-full py-2 bg-red-100 text-red-600 rounded-xl font-bold mb-3">مسح الكل</button>';
        html += '<input id="online-cust-name" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border mb-2" placeholder="الاسم الكامل" value="' + _escapeHtml(cust.name) + '">';
        html += '<input id="online-cust-phone" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border mb-2" placeholder="رقم الهاتف" value="' + _escapeHtml(cust.phone) + '">';
        html += '<input id="online-cust-area" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border mb-2" placeholder="العنوان / المنطقة" value="' + _escapeHtml(cust.area) + '">';
        html += '<input id="online-cust-notes" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border mb-2" placeholder="ملاحظات إضافية (اختياري)" value="' + _escapeHtml(cust.notes) + '">';
        html += '</div>';

        return html;
    }

    function _saveCustomerData() {
        var nameEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-name');
        var phoneEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-phone');
        var areaEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-area');
        var notesEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-notes');
        lastCustomerData = {
            name: nameEl ? (nameEl.value ? nameEl.value.trim() : '') : '',
            phone: phoneEl ? (phoneEl.value ? phoneEl.value.trim() : '') : '',
            area: areaEl ? (areaEl.value ? areaEl.value.trim() : '') : '',
            notes: notesEl ? (notesEl.value ? notesEl.value.trim() : '') : ''
        };
    }

    function _showCart() {
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(freshSettings) {
                    taxRate = Number(freshSettings.taxRate) || 0;
                    deliveryFeeValue = Number(freshSettings.deliveryFee) || 0;
                    RW_OnlineStore._companyName = freshSettings.companyName || RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
                    RW_OnlineStore._vatNumber = '310000000000003';
                    _renderCartModal();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    console.error("فشل جلب الإعدادات:", err);
                    RW_OnlineStore._companyName = RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
                    RW_OnlineStore._vatNumber = '310000000000003';
                    _renderCartModal();
                })
                .getAppSettings();
        } else {
            RW_OnlineStore._companyName = RW_STATE.app.company.name || 'الروائع';
            RW_OnlineStore._vatNumber = '310000000000003';
            _renderCartModal();
        }
    }

    function _renderCartModal() {
        var initialItemsArr = [];
        var initialSubtotal = 0;
        for (var code in cart) {
            if (cart.hasOwnProperty(code)) {
                var items = RW_STATE.data.items;
                if (!items) continue;
                var itm = null;
                for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                    if (items[i].code === code) { itm = items[i]; break; }
                }
                if (!itm) continue;
                var qty = cart[code];
                var price = Number(itm.sPrice) || 0;
                var line = price * qty;
                initialSubtotal += line;
                initialItemsArr.push({ code: code, name: itm.name, qty: qty, price: price });
            }
        }

        if (initialItemsArr.length === 0) {
            if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('السلة فارغة', 'info');
            return;
        }

        Swal.fire({
            title: 'سلة التسوق',
            html: _getCartModalHTML(initialItemsArr, initialSubtotal, lastCustomerData),
            width: '800px',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'إرسال الطلب',
            cancelButtonText: 'متابعة التسوق',
            didOpen: function() {
                var nameEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-name');
                var phoneEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-phone');
                var areaEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-area');
                var notesEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-notes');
                if (nameEl && lastCustomerData.name) nameEl.value = lastCustomerData.name;
                if (phoneEl && lastCustomerData.phone) phoneEl.value = lastCustomerData.phone;
                if (areaEl && lastCustomerData.area) areaEl.value = lastCustomerData.area;
                if (notesEl && lastCustomerData.notes) notesEl.value = lastCustomerData.notes;

                var clearBtn = document.getElementById('clear-cart-btn');
                if (clearBtn) {
                    clearBtn.onclick = function() {
                        Swal.close();
                        _clearCart();
                    };
                }
            },
            preConfirm: function() {
                _saveCustomerData();
                var finalItemsArr = [];
                var finalSubtotal = 0;
                for (var code in cart) {
                    if (cart.hasOwnProperty(code)) {
                        var items = RW_STATE.data.items;
                        if (!items) continue;
                        var itm = null;
                        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                            if (items[i].code === code) { itm = items[i]; break; }
                        }
                        if (!itm) continue;
                        var qty = cart[code];
                        var price = Number(itm.sPrice) || 0;
                        var line = price * qty;
                        finalSubtotal += line;
                        finalItemsArr.push({ code: code, name: itm.name, qty: qty, price: price });
                    }
                }

                var nameEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-name');
                var phoneEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-phone');
                var areaEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-area');
                var notesEl = document.getElementById('online-cust-notes');
                var name = nameEl ? (nameEl.value ? nameEl.value.trim() : '') : '';
                var phone = phoneEl ? (phoneEl.value ? phoneEl.value.trim() : '') : '';
                var area = areaEl ? (areaEl.value ? areaEl.value.trim() : '') : '';
                var notes = notesEl ? (notesEl.value ? notesEl.value.trim() : '') : '';
                if (!name || !phone || !area) {
                    Swal.showValidationMessage('الرجاء إكمال جميع البيانات');
                    return false;
                }
                return { 
                    name: name, phone: phone, area: area, notes: notes,
                    itemsArr: finalItemsArr, subtotal: finalSubtotal
                };
            }
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
            if (typeof showLoader === 'function') showLoader('جاري إرسال الطلب...');

            var currentTaxRate = taxRate;
            var currentDeliveryFee = deliveryFeeValue;
            var currentCompanyName = RW_OnlineStore._companyName || 'الروائع';
            var currentVatNumber = RW_OnlineStore._vatNumber || '310000000000003';

            if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(orderId) {
                        if (typeof hideLoader === 'function') hideLoader();
                        if (typeof orderId === 'string' && orderId.indexOf('Error:') === 0) {
                            Swal.fire({
                                title: 'تنبيه',
                                text: orderId.substring(7),
                                icon: 'warning',
                                confirmButtonText: 'حسناً',
                                willClose: function() {
                                    _showCart();
                                }
                            });
                        } else {
                            var beforeTax = result.value.subtotal + currentDeliveryFee;
                            var taxAmt = Math.round(beforeTax * currentTaxRate) / 100;
                            var grandTotal = beforeTax + taxAmt;

                            var invoiceDate = new Date().toISOString();
                            var qrBase64 = generateQRInvoiceBase64(currentCompanyName, currentVatNumber, invoiceDate, String(grandTotal), String(taxAmt));

                            var qrHtml = '<div style="text-align:center;margin-top:15px;">';
                            qrHtml += '<p style="font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:8px;">رمز الفاتورة الإلكترونية</p>';
                            qrHtml += '<div id="store-qrcode-container" style="display:inline-block;"></div>';
                            qrHtml += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:#6b7280;margin-top:8px;">امسح الكود للتحقق من الفاتورة</p>';
                            qrHtml += '</div>';

                            Swal.fire({
                                title: 'تم',
                                html: '<p style="text-align:center;">رقم الطلب: <strong>' + orderId + '</strong></p>' + qrHtml,
                                icon: 'success',
                                confirmButtonText: 'حسناً',
                                didOpen: function() {
                                    try {
                                        var container = document.getElementById('store-qrcode-container');
                                        if (container && typeof QRCode !== 'undefined') {
                                            container.innerHTML = '';
                                            new QRCode(container, {
                                                text: qrBase64,
                                                width: 150,
                                                height: 150,
                                                colorDark: '#000000',
                                                colorLight: '#ffffff',
                                                correctLevel: QRCode.CorrectLevel.M
                                            });
                                        }
                                    } catch(e) { console.error('QR Code error:', e); }
                                }
                            });
                            cart = {};
                            lastCustomerData = { name: '', phone: '', area: '', notes: '' };
                            _renderProductCards();
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        if (typeof hideLoader === 'function') hideLoader();
                        if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('فشل إرسال الطلب: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .submitOnlineOrder(
                        result.value,
                        result.value.itemsArr,
                        result.value.subtotal + currentDeliveryFee,
                        currentDeliveryFee,
                        currentTaxRate
                    );
            }
        });
    }

    function _showProduct(code) {
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items;
        if (!items) return;
        var item = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            if (items[i].code === code) { item = items[i]; break; }
        }
        if (!item) return;
        Swal.fire({
            imageUrl: item.image || 'https://via.placeholder.com/150',
            imageWidth: 200,
            title: item.name,
            text: item.desc || '',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: (cart[code] || 0) > 0 ? 'الكمية: ' + (cart[code] || 0) : 'إضافة للسلة',
            cancelButtonText: 'إغلاق'
        }).then(function(res) {
            if (res.isConfirmed && (cart[code] || 0) === 0) {
                _addToCart(code);
            }
        });
    }

    function _trackOrder() {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تتبع حالة الطلب',
            input: 'text',
            inputLabel: 'أدخل رقم الطلب (مثل ORD-1001)',
            inputPlaceholder: 'رقم الطلب',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'استعلام',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            preConfirm: function(orderCode) {
                if (!orderCode) {
                    Swal.showValidationMessage('الرجاء إدخال رقم الطلب');
                    return false;
                }
                return orderCode;
            }
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري جلب حالة الطلب...');
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (!res.found) {
                        Swal.fire({
                            title: 'الطلب غير موجود',
                            text: 'لم يتم العثور على طلب بهذا الرقم.',
                            icon: 'error',
                            confirmButtonText: 'حسناً'
                        });
                        return;
                    }

                    var items = res.items || [];
                    var statusLabel = '';
                    var statusColor = '';
                    if (res.orderStatus === 'Pending') { statusLabel = 'قيد الانتظار'; statusColor = 'text-yellow-600'; }
                    else if (res.orderStatus === 'Confirmed') { statusLabel = 'مؤكد'; statusColor = 'text-blue-600'; }
                    else if (res.orderStatus === 'Invoiced') { statusLabel = 'تمت الفوترة'; statusColor = 'text-green-600'; }
                    else if (res.orderStatus === 'Delivered') { statusLabel = 'تم التوصيل'; statusColor = 'text-green-700'; }
                    else if (res.orderStatus === 'Cancelled') { statusLabel = 'ملغي'; statusColor = 'text-red-600'; }
                    else { statusLabel = res.orderStatus; statusColor = 'text-gray-600'; }

                    var itemsHtml = '';
                    var total = 0;
                    if (items.length > 0) {
                        itemsHtml = '<table class="w-full border text-sm"><thead><tr class="bg-gray-100"><th class="p-2 border">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">السعر</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الإجمالي</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                            var it = items[i];
                            var lineTotal = Number(it.total) || (Number(it.qty) * Number(it.price));
                            total += lineTotal;
                            itemsHtml += '<tr><td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(it.name) + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + it.qty + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + Number(it.price).toLocaleString() + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + Number(lineTotal).toLocaleString() + '</td></tr>';
                        }
                        itemsHtml += '</tbody></table>';
                    } else {
                        itemsHtml = '<div class="text-center py-4 text-gray-500">لا توجد أصناف مسجلة لهذا الطلب</div>';
                    }

                    var detailHtml = '<div class="text-right">';
                    detailHtml += '<p class="mb-3"><strong>حالة الطلب:</strong> <span class="font-bold ' + statusColor + '">' + statusLabel + '</span></p>';
                    detailHtml += itemsHtml;
                    detailHtml += '<div class="mt-4 font-bold text-lg">الإجمالي: ' + Number(total).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</div>';
                    detailHtml += '</div>';

                    Swal.fire({
                        title: 'تفاصيل الطلب: ' + result.value,
                        html: detailHtml,
                        width: '700px',
                        showCloseButton: true,
                        showConfirmButton: false
                    });
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل جلب بيانات الطلب: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getOrderDetailsFromServer(result.value);
        });
    }

    return {
        render: function() {
            var container = byId('rw-page-container');
            if (!container) return;

            safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'المتجر الإلكتروني');
            safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'استعراض المنتجات وإرسال الطلبات');
            cart = {};

            var self = this;

            if (!RW_STATE.data.items || RW_STATE.data.items.length === 0) {
                showLoader('جاري تحميل المنتجات...');
                if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
                    google.script.run
                        .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                            hideLoader();
                            RW_STATE.data.items = data || [];
                            self._buildUI(container);
                        })
                        .withFailureHandler(function() {
                            hideLoader();
                            self._buildUI(container);
                        })
                        .loadItemsData(1, 500);
                } else {
                    hideLoader();
                    self._buildUI(container);
                }
            } else {
                self._buildUI(container);
            }
        },

        _buildUI: function(container) {
            _loadStoreSettings();

            var html = '<div class="p-4">';
            html += '<div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center mb-4 gap-3">';
            html += '<div class="flex overflow-x-auto gap-2 pb-2" id="online-categories-bar"></div>';
            html += '<div class="flex gap-2">';
            html += '<button onclick="RW_OnlineStore._trackOrder()" class="bg-white border border-blue-200 text-blue-600 px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold text-sm"><i class="fa-solid fa-magnifying-glass ml-1"></i> تتبع الطلب</button>';
            html += '<button onclick="RW_OnlineStore._showCart()" class="bg-slate-100 px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold relative">🛒 <span id="online-cart-badge">0</span></button>';
            html += '</div>';
            html += '</div>';
            html += '<input type="text" id="online-store-search" class="w-full p-3 bg-white rounded-xl border mb-4" placeholder="ابحث عن منتج..." oninput="RW_OnlineStore._renderProductCards()">';
            html += '<div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4" id="online-store-grid"></div>';
            html += '</div>';

            safeHTML(container, html);

            var catBar = byId('online-categories-bar');
            if (catBar) {
                var cats = ['الكل'];
                var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
                for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
                    if (items[i].cat && cats.indexOf(items[i].cat) === -1) cats.push(items[i].cat);
                }
                var catHtml = '';
                for (var c = 0; c < cats.length; c++) {
                    var cn = cats[c];
                    catHtml += '<button class="sub-tab-btn ' + (activeCategory === cn ? 'active-sub' : '') + '" onclick="RW_OnlineStore._setCategory(\'' + _escapeHtml(cn) + '\')">' + _escapeHtml(cn) + '</button>';
                }
                safeHTML(catBar, catHtml);
            }

            _renderProductCards();
        },

        _setCategory: function(cat) {
            activeCategory = cat;
            _renderProductCards();
        },

        _renderProductCards: _renderProductCards,
        _addToCart: _addToCart,
        _updateCart: _updateCart,
        _updateCartFromModal: _updateCartFromModal,
        _showCart: _showCart,
        _showProduct: _showProduct,
        _trackOrder: _trackOrder,
        _clearCart: _clearCart,
        _getCartModalHTML: _getCartModalHTML
    };
})();
window.RW_OnlineStore = RW_OnlineStore;
// ============================================================
// RW_Warehouse – تبويب العمليات المخزنية (تحضير، تحميل، توصيل...)
// ============================================================
var RW_Warehouse = (function() {
    'use strict';
    var pickingData = [];
    var pickingSort = { field: 'rsId', asc: true };
    var loadingData = [];
    var loadingSort = { field: 'rsId', asc: true };
    var deliveryData = [];
    var deliverySort = { field: 'rsId', asc: true };
    var returnData = [];
    var returnSort = { field: 'rsId', asc: true };
    var unloadingData = [];
    var unloadingSort = { field: 'rsId', asc: true };

    function _escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        return String(str).replace(/[&<>]/g, function(m) {
            if (m === '&') return '&amp;';
            if (m === '<') return '&lt;';
            if (m === '>') return '&gt;';
            return m;
        });
    }

    // ==================== التحضير (Picking) ====================
    function loadPicking() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التحضير (Picking)');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'تحضير الرانشيتات الجاهزة');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="pick-filter-id" placeholder="رقم الرانشيت..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyPickingFilters()">' +
            '<select id="pick-filter-status" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyPickingFilters()"><option value="">كل الحالات</option><option value="Available">متاح</option><option value="Open">مفتوح</option><option value="Picking">جاري التحضير</option><option value="Picked">تم التحضير</option></select>' +
            '<input type="text" id="pick-filter-driver" placeholder="السائق..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyPickingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="pick-filter-date-from" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyPickingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="pick-filter-date-to" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyPickingFilters()">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._applyPickingFilters()" class="bg-gray-600 text-white px-3 rounded text-sm font-bold">تطبيق</button>' +
            '</div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1000px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortPickingTable(\'rsId\')">الرانشيت <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortPickingTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">السائق</th><th class="p-3">السيارة</th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortPickingTable(\'orderCount\')">الأوردرات <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortPickingTable(\'totalAmount\')">القيمة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">الحالة</th></tr></thead>' +
            '<tbody id="picking-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    pickingData = data || [];
                    _applyPickingFilters();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('picking-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">فشل تحميل البيانات</td></tr>');
                })
                .getRunsheetsForPicking();
        }
    }

    function _renderPickingTable(data) {
        var tbody = byId('picking-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (!data || data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد رانشيتات جاهزة للتحضير</td></tr>');
            return;
        }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var rs = data[i];
            var statusBadge = '';
            var st = rs.status || '';
            if (st === 'Available' || st === 'Open') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-blue-100 text-blue-700">جاهز</span>';
            else if (st === 'Picking') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-purple-100 text-purple-700">جاري التحضير</span>';
            else if (st === 'Picked') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-green-100 text-green-700">تم التحضير</span>';
            else statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-gray-100 text-gray-700">' + _escapeHtml(st) + '</span>';

            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._openPickingModal(\'' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '\', \'' + _escapeHtml(rs.status || 'Open') + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 font-bold text-emerald-600">' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.driverEmail || rs.driver || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.vehicleId || rs.vehicle || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (rs.orderCount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(rs.totalAmount || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + statusBadge + '</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _openPickingModal(rsId, originalStatus) {
        if (!originalStatus) originalStatus = 'Open';
        showLoader('جاري تحميل بيانات الرانشيت...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(items) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (!items || items.length === 0) {
                        showToast('لا توجد أصناف في هذا الرانشيت', 'info');
                        return;
                    }
                    _buildPickingModal(rsId, items, originalStatus);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل تحميل بيانات الرانشيت: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getRunsheetItemsForOperation(rsId);
        }
    }

    function _buildPickingModal(rsId, items, originalStatus) {
        var html = '<div class="text-right" dir="rtl"><div class="max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto"><table class="w-full border"><thead class="bg-slate-100"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الوحدة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية المطلوبة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية المحضرة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">ملاحظات</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            var it = items[i];
            html += '<tr><td class="p-2 border"><p class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemName || '') + '</p><p class="text-xs">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemCode || '') + '</p></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center">' + _escapeHtml(it.unit || 'حبة') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + (it.qty_ordered || it.orderedQty || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center"><input type="number" id="picked_qty_' + i + '" class="w-24 p-2 border rounded text-center" step="1" min="0" value="' + (it.qty_ordered || it.orderedQty || 0) + '"></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center"><input type="text" id="picked_note_' + i + '" class="w-32 p-2 border rounded text-sm" placeholder="سبب النقص"></td></tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table></div></div>';

        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تحضير الرانشيت: ' + _escapeHtml(rsId),
            html: html,
            width: '1000px',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'حفظ التحضير',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            showDenyButton: true,
            denyButtonText: 'بدء التحضير',
            preConfirm: function() {
                var itemsData = [];
                var allZero = true;
                for (var j = 0; j < items.length; j++) {
                    var qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('picked_qty_' + j).value) || 0;
                    var note = document.getElementById('picked_note_' + j).value || '';
                    if (qty > 0) allZero = false;
                    itemsData.push({ itemCode: items[j].itemCode, pickedQty: qty, notes: note, itemName: items[j].itemName || '' });
                }
                if (allZero) {
                    Swal.showValidationMessage('يجب تحضير كمية واحدة على الأقل');
                    return false;
                }
                return itemsData;
            }
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                showLoader('جاري حفظ التحضير...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم حفظ التحضير بنجاح', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < pickingData.length; i++) {
                                if (pickingData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    pickingData[i].status = 'Picked';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderPickingTable(pickingData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل حفظ التحضير', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .completePicking(rsId, result.value);
            } else if (result.isDenied) {
                showLoader('جاري بدء التحضير...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم بدء التحضير', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < pickingData.length; i++) {
                                if (pickingData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    pickingData[i].status = 'Picking';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderPickingTable(pickingData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل بدء التحضير', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .startPicking(rsId);
            }
        });
    }

    // ==================== التحميل (Loading) ====================
    function loadLoading() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التحميل (Loading)');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'تحميل الرانشيتات المحضّرة');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="load-filter-id" placeholder="رقم الرانشيت..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyLoadingFilters()">' +
            '<select id="load-filter-status" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyLoadingFilters()"><option value="">كل الحالات</option><option value="Picked">جاهز للتحميل</option><option value="Loading">جاري التحميل</option><option value="Loaded">تم التحميل</option></select>' +
            '<input type="text" id="load-filter-driver" placeholder="السائق..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyLoadingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="load-filter-date-from" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyLoadingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="load-filter-date-to" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyLoadingFilters()">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._applyLoadingFilters()" class="bg-gray-600 text-white px-3 rounded text-sm font-bold">تطبيق</button>' +
            '</div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1000px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortLoadingTable(\'rsId\')">الرانشيت <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortLoadingTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">السائق</th><th class="p-3">السيارة</th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortLoadingTable(\'orderCount\')">الأوردرات <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortLoadingTable(\'totalAmount\')">القيمة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">الحالة</th></tr></thead>' +
            '<tbody id="loading-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    loadingData = data || [];
                    _applyLoadingFilters();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('loading-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">فشل تحميل البيانات</td></tr>');
                })
                .getRunsheetsForLoading();
        }
    }

    function _renderLoadingTable(data) {
        var tbody = byId('loading-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (!data || data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد رانشيتات جاهزة للتحميل</td></tr>');
            return;
        }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var rs = data[i];
            var statusBadge = '';
            var st = rs.status || '';
            if (st === 'Picked') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-blue-100 text-blue-700">جاهز للتحميل</span>';
            else if (st === 'Loading') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-purple-100 text-purple-700">جاري التحميل</span>';
            else if (st === 'Loaded') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-green-100 text-green-700">تم التحميل</span>';
            else statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-gray-100 text-gray-700">' + _escapeHtml(st) + '</span>';

            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._openLoadingModal(\'' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '\', \'' + _escapeHtml(rs.status || 'Picked') + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 font-bold text-emerald-600">' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.driverEmail || rs.driver || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.vehicleId || rs.vehicle || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (rs.orderCount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(rs.totalAmount || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + statusBadge + '</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _openLoadingModal(rsId, originalStatus) {
        if (!originalStatus) originalStatus = 'Picked';
        showLoader('جاري تحميل بيانات الرانشيت...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(items) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (!items || items.length === 0) {
                        showToast('لا توجد أصناف في هذا الرانشيت', 'info');
                        return;
                    }
                    _buildLoadingModal(rsId, items, originalStatus);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل تحميل بيانات الرانشيت: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getRunsheetItemsForOperation(rsId);
        }
    }

    function _buildLoadingModal(rsId, items, originalStatus) {
        var html = '<div class="text-right" dir="rtl"><div class="max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto"><table class="w-full border"><thead class="bg-slate-100"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الوحدة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية المطلوبة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية المحضّرة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية المحمّلة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            var it = items[i];
            var orderedQty = it.qty_ordered || it.orderedQty || 0;
            var pickedQty = it.qty_picked || it.pickedQty || 0;
            html += '<tr><td class="p-2 border"><p class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemName || '') + '</p><p class="text-xs">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemCode || '') + '</p></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center">' + _escapeHtml(it.unit || 'حبة') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + orderedQty + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + pickedQty + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center"><input type="number" id="loaded_qty_' + i + '" class="w-24 p-2 border rounded text-center" step="1" min="0" max="' + pickedQty + '" value="' + pickedQty + '"></td></tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table></div></div>';

        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تحميل الرانشيت: ' + _escapeHtml(rsId),
            html: html,
            width: '1000px',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'حفظ التحميل',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            showDenyButton: true,
            denyButtonText: 'بدء التحميل',
            preConfirm: function() {
                var itemsData = [];
                var allZero = true;
                for (var j = 0; j < items.length; j++) {
                    var qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('loaded_qty_' + j).value) || 0;
                    var note = ''; // ملاحظات التحميل غير موجودة في الخادم الحالي، سيتم تجاهلها
                    if (qty > 0) allZero = false;
                    itemsData.push({ itemCode: items[j].itemCode, loadedQty: qty, notes: note, itemName: items[j].itemName || '' });
                }
                if (allZero) {
                    Swal.showValidationMessage('يجب تحميل كمية واحدة على الأقل');
                    return false;
                }
                return itemsData;
            }
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                showLoader('جاري حفظ التحميل...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم حفظ التحميل بنجاح', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < loadingData.length; i++) {
                                if (loadingData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    loadingData[i].status = 'Loaded';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderLoadingTable(loadingData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل حفظ التحميل', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .completeLoading(rsId, result.value);
            } else if (result.isDenied) {
                showLoader('جاري بدء التحميل...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم بدء التحميل', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < loadingData.length; i++) {
                                if (loadingData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    loadingData[i].status = 'Loading';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderLoadingTable(loadingData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل بدء التحميل', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .startLoading(rsId);
            }
        });
    }
    // ==================== التوصيل (Delivery) ====================
    function loadDelivery() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التوصيل (Delivery)');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'توصيل الرانشيتات المحمّلة');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="del-filter-id" placeholder="رقم الرانشيت..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyDeliveryFilters()">' +
            '<select id="del-filter-status" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyDeliveryFilters()"><option value="">كل الحالات</option><option value="Loaded">جاهز للتوصيل</option><option value="Delivering">جاري التوصيل</option><option value="Delivered">تم التوصيل</option></select>' +
            '<input type="text" id="del-filter-driver" placeholder="السائق..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyDeliveryFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="del-filter-date-from" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyDeliveryFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="del-filter-date-to" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyDeliveryFilters()">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._applyDeliveryFilters()" class="bg-gray-600 text-white px-3 rounded text-sm font-bold">تطبيق</button>' +
            '</div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1000px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortDeliveryTable(\'rsId\')">الرانشيت <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortDeliveryTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">السائق</th><th class="p-3">السيارة</th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortDeliveryTable(\'orderCount\')">الأوردرات <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortDeliveryTable(\'totalAmount\')">القيمة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">الحالة</th></tr></thead>' +
            '<tbody id="delivery-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    deliveryData = data || [];
                    _applyDeliveryFilters();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('delivery-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">فشل تحميل البيانات</td></tr>');
                })
                .getRunsheetsForDelivery();
        }
    }

    function _renderDeliveryTable(data) {
        var tbody = byId('delivery-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (!data || data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد رانشيتات جاهزة للتوصيل</td></tr>');
            return;
        }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var rs = data[i];
            var statusBadge = '';
            var st = rs.status || '';
            if (st === 'Loaded') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-blue-100 text-blue-700">جاهز للتوصيل</span>';
            else if (st === 'Delivering') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-purple-100 text-purple-700">جاري التوصيل</span>';
            else if (st === 'Delivered') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-green-100 text-green-700">تم التوصيل</span>';
            else statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-gray-100 text-gray-700">' + _escapeHtml(st) + '</span>';

            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._openDeliveryModal(\'' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '\', \'' + _escapeHtml(rs.status || 'Loaded') + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 font-bold text-emerald-600">' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.driverEmail || rs.driver || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.vehicleId || rs.vehicle || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (rs.orderCount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(rs.totalAmount || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + statusBadge + '</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _openDeliveryModal(rsId, originalStatus) {
        if (!originalStatus) originalStatus = 'Loaded';
        showLoader('جاري تحميل بيانات التوصيل...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(ordersData) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (!ordersData || ordersData.length === 0) {
                        showToast('لا توجد أوردرات في هذا الرانشيت', 'info');
                        return;
                    }
                    _buildDeliveryModal(rsId, ordersData, originalStatus);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل تحميل بيانات التوصيل: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getOrderDeliveryDetails(rsId);
        }
    }

    function _buildDeliveryModal(rsId, ordersData, originalStatus) {
        var html = '<div class="text-right" dir="rtl"><div class="max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto">';
        for (var o = 0; o < ordersData.length; o++) {
            var order = ordersData[o];
            html += '<div class="mb-4 p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg"><h4 class="font-bold text-blue-600 mb-2">' + _escapeHtml(order.orderId) + ' - ' + _escapeHtml(order.custName) + '</h4>';
            html += '<table class="w-full border"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-1">الصنف</th><th class="p-1 text-center">محملة</th><th class="p-1 text-center">مُسلّمة</th><th class="p-1 text-center">مرفوضة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
            for (var j = 0; j < order.items.length; j++) {
                var it = order.items[j];
                var loadedQty = it.loadedQty || 0;
                html += '<tr><td class="p-1">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemName || '') + '</td>';
                html += '<td class="p-1 text-center font-bold">' + loadedQty + '</td>';
                html += '<td class="p-1 text-center"><input type="number" id="del_qty_' + o + '_' + j + '" class="w-20 p-1 border rounded text-center" min="0" max="' + loadedQty + '" value="' + loadedQty + '" oninput="RW_Warehouse._updateRefusedAuto(\'' + o + '_' + j + '\', ' + loadedQty + ')"></td>';
                html += '<td class="p-1 text-center"><input type="text" id="ref_qty_' + o + '_' + j + '" class="w-16 p-1 bg-gray-100 border rounded text-center font-bold text-red-600" readonly></td></tr>';
            }
            html += '</tbody></table></div>';
        }
        html += '</div></div>';

        Swal.fire({
            title: 'توصيل الرانشيت: ' + _escapeHtml(rsId),
            html: html,
            width: '900px',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'إنهاء التوصيل',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            showDenyButton: true,
            denyButtonText: 'بدء التوصيل',
            preConfirm: function() {
                var finalOrdersData = [];
                for (var o = 0; o < ordersData.length; o++) {
                    var order = ordersData[o];
                    var orderItems = [];
                    for (var j = 0; j < order.items.length; j++) {
                        var delQty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('del_qty_' + o + '_' + j).value) || 0;
                        orderItems.push({ itemCode: order.items[j].itemCode, deliveredQty: delQty, refusedQty: 0, reason: '' });
                    }
                    finalOrdersData.push({ orderId: order.orderId, items: orderItems });
                }
                return finalOrdersData;
            }
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                showLoader('جاري إنهاء التوصيل...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم إنهاء التوصيل بنجاح', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < deliveryData.length; i++) {
                                if (deliveryData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    deliveryData[i].status = 'Delivered';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderDeliveryTable(deliveryData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل إنهاء التوصيل', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .completeDelivery(rsId, result.value);
            } else if (result.isDenied) {
                showLoader('جاري بدء التوصيل...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم بدء التوصيل', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < deliveryData.length; i++) {
                                if (deliveryData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    deliveryData[i].status = 'Delivering';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderDeliveryTable(deliveryData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل بدء التوصيل', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .startDelivery(rsId);
            }
        });
    }

    function _updateRefusedAuto(key, loadedQty) {
        var delInput = document.getElementById('del_qty_' + key);
        var refInput = document.getElementById('ref_qty_' + key);
        if (delInput && refInput) {
            var delivered = parseFloat(delInput.value) || 0;
            refInput.value = Math.max(0, loadedQty - delivered);
        }
    }
        // ==================== المرتجعات (Return) ====================
    function loadReturn() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'المرتجعات (Return)');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'مرتجعات الرانشيتات الموصّلة');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="ret-filter-id" placeholder="رقم الرانشيت..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyReturnFilters()">' +
            '<select id="ret-filter-status" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyReturnFilters()"><option value="">كل الحالات</option><option value="Delivered">جاهز للمرتجعات</option><option value="Returning">جاري المرتجعات</option><option value="Returned">تم الارتجاع</option></select>' +
            '<input type="text" id="ret-filter-driver" placeholder="السائق..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyReturnFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="ret-filter-date-from" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyReturnFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="ret-filter-date-to" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyReturnFilters()">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._applyReturnFilters()" class="bg-gray-600 text-white px-3 rounded text-sm font-bold">تطبيق</button>' +
            '</div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1000px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReturnTable(\'rsId\')">الرانشيت <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReturnTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">السائق</th><th class="p-3">السيارة</th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReturnTable(\'orderCount\')">الأوردرات <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReturnTable(\'totalAmount\')">القيمة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">الحالة</th></tr></thead>' +
            '<tbody id="return-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    returnData = data || [];
                    _applyReturnFilters();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('return-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">فشل تحميل البيانات</td></tr>');
                })
