                .getRunsheetsForReturn();
        }
    }

    function _renderReturnTable(data) {
        var tbody = byId('return-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (!data || data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد رانشيتات قابلة للمرتجعات</td></tr>');
            return;
        }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var rs = data[i];
            var statusBadge = '';
            var st = rs.status || '';
            if (st === 'Delivered') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-blue-100 text-blue-700">جاهز للمرتجعات</span>';
            else if (st === 'Returning') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-purple-100 text-purple-700">جاري المرتجعات</span>';
            else if (st === 'Returned') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-green-100 text-green-700">تم الارتجاع</span>';
            else statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-gray-100 text-gray-700">' + _escapeHtml(st) + '</span>';

            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._openReturnModal(\'' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '\', \'' + _escapeHtml(rs.status || 'Delivered') + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 font-bold text-emerald-600">' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.driverEmail || rs.driver || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.vehicleId || rs.vehicle || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (rs.orderCount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(rs.totalAmount || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + statusBadge + '</td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _openReturnModal(rsId, originalStatus) {
        if (!originalStatus) originalStatus = 'Delivered';
        showLoader('جاري تحميل بيانات المرتجعات...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(items) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (!items || items.length === 0) {
                        showToast('لا توجد أصناف في هذا الرانشيت', 'info');
                        return;
                    }
                    _buildReturnModal(rsId, items, originalStatus);
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    hideLoader();
                    showToast('فشل تحميل بيانات المرتجعات: ' + err.message, 'error');
                })
                .getReturnItemsData(rsId);
        }
    }

    function _buildReturnModal(rsId, items, originalStatus) {
        var html = '<div class="text-right" dir="rtl"><div class="max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto"><table class="w-full border"><thead class="bg-slate-100"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الوحدة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">المحمّلة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">المرتجعة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">سبب المرتجع</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            var it = items[i];
            var loadedQty = it.loadedQty || 0;
            html += '<tr><td class="p-2 border"><p class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemName || '') + '</p><p class="text-xs">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemCode || '') + '</p></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center">' + _escapeHtml(it.unit || 'حبة') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + loadedQty + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center"><input type="number" id="returned_qty_' + i + '" class="w-24 p-2 border rounded text-center" step="1" min="0" max="' + loadedQty + '" value="0"></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 border text-center"><input type="text" id="returned_reason_' + i + '" class="w-32 p-2 border rounded text-sm" placeholder="سبب المرتجع"></td></tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table></div></div>';

        Swal.fire({
            title: 'مرتجعات الرانشيت: ' + _escapeHtml(rsId),
            html: html,
            width: '1000px',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'حفظ المرتجعات',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            showDenyButton: true,
            denyButtonText: 'بدء المرتجعات',
            preConfirm: function() {
                var itemsData = [];
                var allZero = true;
                for (var j = 0; j < items.length; j++) {
                    var qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('returned_qty_' + j).value) || 0;
                    var reason = document.getElementById('returned_reason_' + j).value || '';
                    if (qty > 0) allZero = false;
                    itemsData.push({ itemCode: items[j].itemCode, returnedQty: qty, reason: reason, itemName: items[j].itemName || '' });
                }
                if (allZero) {
                    Swal.showValidationMessage('يجب إدخال كمية مرتجعة واحدة على الأقل');
                    return false;
                }
                return itemsData;
            }
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                showLoader('جاري حفظ المرتجعات...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم حفظ المرتجعات بنجاح', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < returnData.length; i++) {
                                if (returnData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    returnData[i].status = 'Returned';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderReturnTable(returnData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل حفظ المرتجعات', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .completeReturn(rsId, result.value);
            } else if (result.isDenied) {
                showLoader('جاري بدء المرتجعات...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم بدء المرتجعات', 'success');
                            for (var i = 0; i < returnData.length; i++) {
                                if (returnData[i].rsId === rsId) {
                                    returnData[i].status = 'Returning';
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            _renderReturnTable(returnData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل بدء المرتجعات', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .startReturn(rsId);
            }
        });
    }
        // ==================== التفريغ (Unloading) ====================
    function loadUnloading() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'التفريغ (Unloading)');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'تفريغ الرانشيتات المحمّلة');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="unload-filter-id" placeholder="رقم الرانشيت..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyUnloadingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="text" id="unload-filter-driver" placeholder="السائق..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyUnloadingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="unload-filter-date-from" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyUnloadingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="unload-filter-date-to" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyUnloadingFilters()">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._applyUnloadingFilters()" class="bg-gray-600 text-white px-3 rounded text-sm font-bold">تطبيق</button>' +
            '</div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1000px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortUnloadingTable(\'rsId\')">الرانشيت <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortUnloadingTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">السائق</th><th class="p-3">السيارة</th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortUnloadingTable(\'orderCount\')">الأوردرات <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortUnloadingTable(\'totalAmount\')">القيمة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">الحالة</th></tr></thead>' +
            '<tbody id="unloading-table-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    unloadingData = data || [];
                    _applyUnloadingFilters();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('unloading-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">فشل تحميل البيانات</td></tr>');
                })
                .getRunsheetsForUnloading();
        }
    }

    function _renderUnloadingTable(data) {
        var tbody = byId('unloading-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (!data || data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد رانشيتات محمّلة للتفريغ</td></tr>');
            return;
        }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var rs = data[i];
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._confirmUnload(\'' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 font-bold text-emerald-600">' + _escapeHtml(rs.rsId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.driverEmail || rs.driver || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(rs.vehicleId || rs.vehicle || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (rs.orderCount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + Number(rs.totalAmount || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-orange-100 text-orange-700">محمّل</span></td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _confirmUnload(rsId) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد التفريغ',
            text: 'سيتم إعادة جميع الكميات إلى المخزون. متابعة؟',
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، فرّغ',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            confirmButtonColor: '#d97706'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (result.isConfirmed) {
                showLoader('جاري التفريغ...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (res.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم التفريغ بنجاح', 'success');
                            var newData = [];
                            for (var i = 0; i < unloadingData.length; i++) {
                                if (unloadingData[i].rsId !== rsId) {
                                    newData.push(unloadingData[i]);
                                }
                            }
                            unloadingData = newData;
                            _renderUnloadingTable(unloadingData);
                        } else {
                            showToast(res.msg || 'فشل التفريغ', 'error');
                        }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                        hideLoader();
                        showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .unloading(rsId);
            }
        });
    }
    function _applyPickingFilters() {
        if (!pickingData.length) { _renderPickingTable([]); return; }
        var id = (byId('pick-filter-id') ? byId('pick-filter-id').value : '') || '';
        var st = (byId('pick-filter-status') ? byId('pick-filter-status').value : '') || '';
        var dr = (byId('pick-filter-driver') ? byId('pick-filter-driver').value : '') || '';
        var fd = (byId('pick-filter-date-from') ? byId('pick-filter-date-from').value : '') || '';
        var td = (byId('pick-filter-date-to') ? byId('pick-filter-date-to').value : '') || '';

        var filtered = pickingData;
        if (id) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.rsId && r.rsId.toLowerCase().indexOf(id.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (st) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.status === st; }); }
        if (dr) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return (r.driverEmail || r.driver || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(dr.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date <= td; }); }
        _renderPickingTable(filtered);
    }

    function _sortPickingTable(field) {
        if (pickingSort.field === field) { pickingSort.asc = !pickingSort.asc; }
        else { pickingSort.field = field; pickingSort.asc = true; }
        pickingData.sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[field] || '', vb = b[field] || '';
            if (field === 'totalAmount' || field === 'orderCount') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            if (field === 'date') { va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb); }
            if (typeof va === 'string') { va = va.toLowerCase(); vb = vb.toLowerCase(); }
            return (va < vb ? -1 : va > vb ? 1 : 0) * (pickingSort.asc ? 1 : -1);
        });
        _applyPickingFilters();
    }
        function _applyLoadingFilters() {
        if (!loadingData.length) { _renderLoadingTable([]); return; }
        var id = (byId('load-filter-id') ? byId('load-filter-id').value : '') || '';
        var st = (byId('load-filter-status') ? byId('load-filter-status').value : '') || '';
        var dr = (byId('load-filter-driver') ? byId('load-filter-driver').value : '') || '';
        var fd = (byId('load-filter-date-from') ? byId('load-filter-date-from').value : '') || '';
        var td = (byId('load-filter-date-to') ? byId('load-filter-date-to').value : '') || '';

        var filtered = loadingData;
        if (id) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.rsId && r.rsId.toLowerCase().indexOf(id.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (st) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.status === st; }); }
        if (dr) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return (r.driverEmail || r.driver || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(dr.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date <= td; }); }
        _renderLoadingTable(filtered);
    }

    function _sortLoadingTable(field) {
        if (loadingSort.field === field) { loadingSort.asc = !loadingSort.asc; }
        else { loadingSort.field = field; loadingSort.asc = true; }
        loadingData.sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[field] || '', vb = b[field] || '';
            if (field === 'totalAmount' || field === 'orderCount') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            if (field === 'date') { va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb); }
            if (typeof va === 'string') { va = va.toLowerCase(); vb = vb.toLowerCase(); }
            return (va < vb ? -1 : va > vb ? 1 : 0) * (loadingSort.asc ? 1 : -1);
        });
        _applyLoadingFilters();
    }
        function _applyDeliveryFilters() {

        var filtered = deliveryData;

        if (dr) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return (r.driverEmail || r.driver || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(dr.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date <= td; }); }

    }

    function _sortDeliveryTable(field) {
        if (deliverySort.field === field) { deliverySort.asc = !deliverySort.asc; }
        else { deliverySort.field = field; deliverySort.asc = true; }
        deliveryData.sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[field] || '', vb = b[field] || '';
            if (field === 'totalAmount' || field === 'orderCount') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            if (field === 'date') { va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb); }
            if (typeof va === 'string') { va = va.toLowerCase(); vb = vb.toLowerCase(); }
            return (va < vb ? -1 : va > vb ? 1 : 0) * (deliverySort.asc ? 1 : -1);
        });
        _applyDeliveryFilters();
    }
        function _applyReturnFilters() {
        if (!returnData.length) { _renderReturnTable([]); return; }
        var id = (byId('ret-filter-id') ? byId('ret-filter-id').value : '') || '';
        var st = (byId('ret-filter-status') ? byId('ret-filter-status').value : '') || '';
        var dr = (byId('ret-filter-driver') ? byId('ret-filter-driver').value : '') || '';
        var fd = (byId('ret-filter-date-from') ? byId('ret-filter-date-from').value : '') || '';
        var td = (byId('ret-filter-date-to') ? byId('ret-filter-date-to').value : '') || '';
        var filtered = returnData;
        if (id) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.rsId && r.rsId.toLowerCase().indexOf(id.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (st) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.status === st; }); }
        if (dr) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return (r.driverEmail || r.driver || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(dr.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date <= td; }); }
        _renderReturnTable(filtered);
    }

    function _sortReturnTable(field) {
        if (returnSort.field === field) { returnSort.asc = !returnSort.asc; }
        else { returnSort.field = field; returnSort.asc = true; }
        returnData.sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[field] || '', vb = b[field] || '';
            if (field === 'totalAmount' || field === 'orderCount') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            if (field === 'date') { va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb); }
            if (typeof va === 'string') { va = va.toLowerCase(); vb = vb.toLowerCase(); }
            return (va < vb ? -1 : va > vb ? 1 : 0) * (returnSort.asc ? 1 : -1);
        });
        _applyReturnFilters();
    }
        function _applyUnloadingFilters() {
        if (!unloadingData.length) { _renderUnloadingTable([]); return; }
        var id = (byId('unload-filter-id') ? byId('unload-filter-id').value : '') || '';
        var dr = (byId('unload-filter-driver') ? byId('unload-filter-driver').value : '') || '';
        var fd = (byId('unload-filter-date-from') ? byId('unload-filter-date-from').value : '') || '';
        var td = (byId('unload-filter-date-to') ? byId('unload-filter-date-to').value : '') || '';
        var filtered = unloadingData;
        if (id) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.rsId && r.rsId.toLowerCase().indexOf(id.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (dr) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return (r.driverEmail || r.driver || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(dr.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date <= td; }); }
        _renderUnloadingTable(filtered);
    }

    function _sortUnloadingTable(field) {
        if (unloadingSort.field === field) { unloadingSort.asc = !unloadingSort.asc; }
        else { unloadingSort.field = field; unloadingSort.asc = true; }
        unloadingData.sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[field] || '', vb = b[field] || '';
            if (field === 'totalAmount' || field === 'orderCount') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            if (field === 'date') { va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb); }
            if (typeof va === 'string') { va = va.toLowerCase(); vb = vb.toLowerCase(); }
            return (va < vb ? -1 : va > vb ? 1 : 0) * (unloadingSort.asc ? 1 : -1);
        });
        _applyUnloadingFilters();
    }
        // ==================== الاستلام (Receiving) ====================
    var receivingData = [];
    var receivingSort = { field: 'opId', asc: true };

    function loadReceiving() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الاستلام (Receiving)');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'سجل عمليات استلام البضاعة');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4"><div class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="rec-op-filter-id" placeholder="رقم العملية..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyReceivingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="text" id="rec-op-filter-po" placeholder="رقم أمر الشراء..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyReceivingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="text" id="rec-op-filter-resp" placeholder="المسؤول..." class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyReceivingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="rec-op-filter-date-from" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyReceivingFilters()">' +
            '<input type="date" id="rec-op-filter-date-to" class="p-2 bg-slate-50 rounded text-sm" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyReceivingFilters()">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._applyReceivingFilters()" class="bg-gray-600 text-white px-3 rounded text-sm font-bold">تطبيق</button>' +
            '</div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border overflow-auto" style="max-height:65vh;"><table class="w-full min-w-[1000px]"><thead class="bg-gray-50 sticky top-0"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReceivingTable(\'opId\')">رقم العملية <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReceivingTable(\'date\')">التاريخ <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReceivingTable(\'poNumber\')">أمر الشراء <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReceivingTable(\'responsible\')">المسؤول <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReceivingTable(\'itemsCount\')">عدد الأصناف <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '<th class="p-3 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._sortReceivingTable(\'status\')">الحالة <i class="fa-solid fa-sort"></i></th>' +
            '</tr></thead>' +
            '<tbody id="receiving-table-body"><tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8">جاري التحميل...</td></tr></tbody></table></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    receivingData = data || [];
                    _applyReceivingFilters();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var tbody = byId('receiving-table-body');
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">فشل تحميل البيانات</td></tr>');
                })
                .getReceivingOperations();
        }
    }

    function _renderReceivingTable(data) {
        var tbody = byId('receiving-table-body');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (!data || data.length === 0) {
            safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="6" class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد عمليات استلام</td></tr>');
            return;
        }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var op = data[i];
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Warehouse._showReceivingDetails(\'' + _escapeHtml(op.opId || '') + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-3 font-bold text-blue-600">' + _escapeHtml(op.opId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(op.date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(op.poNumber || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(op.responsible || '---') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center font-bold">' + (op.itemsCount || 0) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-3 text-center"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-green-100 text-green-700">' + _escapeHtml(op.status || 'مكتمل') + '</span></td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
    }

    function _applyReceivingFilters() {
        if (!receivingData.length) { _renderReceivingTable([]); return; }
        var id = (byId('rec-op-filter-id') ? byId('rec-op-filter-id').value : '') || '';
        var po = (byId('rec-op-filter-po') ? byId('rec-op-filter-po').value : '') || '';
        var resp = (byId('rec-op-filter-resp') ? byId('rec-op-filter-resp').value : '') || '';
        var fd = (byId('rec-op-filter-date-from') ? byId('rec-op-filter-date-from').value : '') || '';
        var td = (byId('rec-op-filter-date-to') ? byId('rec-op-filter-date-to').value : '') || '';

        var filtered = receivingData;
        if (id) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.opId && r.opId.toLowerCase().indexOf(id.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (po) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.poNumber && r.poNumber.toLowerCase().indexOf(po.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (resp) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.responsible && r.responsible.toLowerCase().indexOf(resp.toLowerCase()) !== -1; }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(r) { return r.date && r.date <= td; }); }
        _renderReceivingTable(filtered);
    }

    function _sortReceivingTable(field) {
        if (receivingSort.field === field) { receivingSort.asc = !receivingSort.asc; }
        else { receivingSort.field = field; receivingSort.asc = true; }
        receivingData.sort(function(a, b) {
            var va = a[field] || '', vb = b[field] || '';
            if (field === 'itemsCount') { va = Number(va); vb = Number(vb); }
            if (field === 'date') { va = new Date(va); vb = new Date(vb); }
            if (typeof va === 'string') { va = va.toLowerCase(); vb = vb.toLowerCase(); }
            return (va < vb ? -1 : va > vb ? 1 : 0) * (receivingSort.asc ? 1 : -1);
        });
        _applyReceivingFilters();
    }

    function _showReceivingDetails(opId) {
        showLoader('جاري تحميل التفاصيل...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(details) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (!details || details.length === 0) {
                        showToast('لا توجد تفاصيل لهذه العملية', 'info');
                        return;
                    }
                    var html = '<div class="text-right"><div class="overflow-x-auto"><table class="w-full border text-sm"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr>' +
                        '<th class="p-2 border">الكود</th><th class="p-2 border">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الوحدة</th>' +
                        '<th class="p-2 border text-center">المطلوب</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الفعلي</th>' +
                        '<th class="p-2 border text-center">الفرق</th><th class="p-2 border">السبب</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                    for (var i = 0; i < details.length; i++) {
                        var d = details[i];
                        html += '<tr><td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(d.itemCode || '') + '</td><td class="p-2 border font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(d.itemName || '') + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 border text-center">' + _escapeHtml(d.unit || '') + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 border text-center">' + (d.qtyExpected || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + (d.qtyActual || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 border text-center ' + (d.difference > 0 ? 'text-green-600' : d.difference < 0 ? 'text-red-600' : '') + '">' + (d.difference || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(d.reason || '') + '</td></tr>';
                    }
                    html += '</tbody></table></div></div>';
                    Swal.fire({ title: 'تفاصيل العملية: ' + _escapeHtml(opId), html: html, width: '800px', showConfirmButton: false, showCancelButton: true, cancelButtonText: 'إغلاق' });
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل تحميل التفاصيل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
                .getReceivingDetails(opId);
        } else { showToast('الخادم غير متاح', 'error'); }
    }
        // ==================== الأذونات المخزنية (Vouchers) ====================
    var vouchersData = [];
    var voucherCart = [];
    var currentVoucherType = '';
    var currentVoucherParams = {};
    var currentEntityLabel = '';
    var showVoucherPrice = false;

    function loadVouchers() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'الأذونات المخزنية');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'سجل الأذونات المخزنية');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4">' +
            '<div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between items-center gap-3 mb-4">' +
            '<h2 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-file-signature ml-2 text-indigo-600"></i>سجل الأذونات المخزنية</h2>' +
            '<div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2">' +
            '<select id="voucherFilterType" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyVoucherFilters()" class="p-2 bg-white border rounded-lg text-sm font-bold"><option value="">كل الأنواع</option><option value="Transfer">تحويل</option><option value="DirectSale">صرف مباشر</option><option value="DirectReturn">مرتجع مباشر</option><option value="SupplierReturn">مرتجع لمورد</option><option value="Scrap">إتلاف</option><option value="Adjustment">جرد</option><option value="Picking">تحضير</option><option value="Loading">تحميل</option><option value="Return">مرتجع</option><option value="Unloading">تفريغ</option></select>' +
            '<select id="voucherFilterStatus" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyVoucherFilters()" class="p-2 bg-white border rounded-lg text-sm font-bold"><option value="">كل الحالات</option><option value="Draft">مسودة</option><option value="Sent">مُرسل</option><option value="Received">مُستلم</option><option value="Confirmed">محجوز</option><option value="Completed">مكتمل</option><option value="Cancelled">ملغي</option></select>' +
            '<input type="date" id="voucherFilterFrom" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyVoucherFilters()" class="p-2 bg-white border rounded-lg text-sm">' +
            '<input type="date" id="voucherFilterTo" onchange="RW_Warehouse._applyVoucherFilters()" class="p-2 bg-white border rounded-lg text-sm">' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2">' +
            '<input type="text" id="voucherSearchInput" oninput="RW_Warehouse._applyVoucherFilters()" placeholder="بحث برقم الإذن..." class="p-2 bg-white border rounded-lg text-sm w-40">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._openNewVoucherModal()" class="bg-indigo-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold text-sm shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-plus ml-1"></i> إذن جديد</button>' +
            '</div></div>' +
            '<div class="overflow-x-auto" style="max-height:60vh;overflow-y:auto;position:relative;" id="vouchers-table-container"></div></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                    vouchersData = data || [];
                    _applyVoucherFilters();
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                    var container2 = byId('vouchers-table-container');
                    if (container2) safeHTML(container2, '<div class="text-center py-8 text-red-500">فشل تحميل البيانات</div>');
                })
                .getStockVouchers({});
        }
    }

    function _renderVouchersTable(data) {
        if (!data || data.length === 0) return '<div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد أذونات مخزنية</div>';
        var html = '<table class="w-full text-right"><thead class="bg-slate-800 text-white sticky top-0 z-10"><tr class="text-xs font-black uppercase">' +
            '<th class="p-3">رقم الإذن</th><th class="p-3">النوع</th><th class="p-3">التاريخ</th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">الحالة</th><th class="p-3">المرجع</th><th class="p-3">من</th>' +
            '<th class="p-3">إلى</th><th class="p-3 text-center">إجراءات</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var v = data[i];
            var statusBadge = '';
            if (v.status === 'Draft') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-gray-100 text-gray-600">مسودة</span>';
            else if (v.status === 'Sent') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-blue-100 text-blue-700">مُرسل</span>';
            else if (v.status === 'Received') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-purple-100 text-purple-700">مُستلم</span>';
            else if (v.status === 'Confirmed') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700">محجوز</span>';
            else if (v.status === 'Completed') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-green-100 text-green-700">مكتمل</span>';
            else if (v.status === 'Cancelled') statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-red-100 text-red-600">ملغي</span>';
            else statusBadge = '<span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-gray-100 text-gray-700">' + _escapeHtml(v.status || '') + '</span>';

            var actions = '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._viewVoucherDetails(\'' + _escapeHtml(v.voucherId) + '\')" class="text-blue-600 mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-eye"></i></button>';
            if (v.status === 'Draft' && !v.isSystemGenerated) {
                actions += '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._reserveVoucher(\'' + _escapeHtml(v.voucherId) + '\')" class="text-yellow-600 mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-lock"></i></button>';
                actions += '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._sendVoucher(\'' + _escapeHtml(v.voucherId) + '\')" class="text-blue-600 mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i></button>';
            }
            if (v.status === 'Sent') {
                actions += '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._receiveVoucher(\'' + _escapeHtml(v.voucherId) + '\')" class="text-green-600 mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-check-circle"></i></button>';
            }
            if (v.status === 'Confirmed') {
                actions += '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._executeVoucher(\'' + _escapeHtml(v.voucherId) + '\')" class="text-green-600 mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-check-circle"></i></button>';
            }
            if ((v.status === 'Draft' || v.status === 'Confirmed') && !v.isSystemGenerated) {
                actions += '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._cancelVoucher(\'' + _escapeHtml(v.voucherId) + '\')" class="text-red-500 mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-ban"></i></button>';
            }

            html += '<tr class="hover:bg-slate-50 border-t"><td class="p-3 font-bold text-indigo-700">' + _escapeHtml(v.voucherId) + '</td>' +
                '<td class="p-3">' + _escapeHtml(v.type) + '</td><td class="p-3 text-sm">' + _escapeHtml(v.date || '') + '</td>' +
                '<td class="p-3">' + statusBadge + '</td><td class="p-3 text-sm">' + _escapeHtml(v.reference || '-') + '</td>' +
                '<td class="p-3 text-sm">' + _escapeHtml(v.fromId || '-') + '</td><td class="p-3 text-sm">' + _escapeHtml(v.toId || '-') + '</td>' +
                '<td class="p-3 text-center">' + actions + '</td></tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table>';
        return html;
    }

    function _applyVoucherFilters() {
        if (!vouchersData.length) {
            var container2 = byId('vouchers-table-container');
            if (container2) safeHTML(container2, '<div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد أذونات</div>');
            return;
        }
        var type = (byId('voucherFilterType') ? byId('voucherFilterType').value : '') || '';
        var status = (byId('voucherFilterStatus') ? byId('voucherFilterStatus').value : '') || '';
        var fd = (byId('voucherFilterFrom') ? byId('voucherFilterFrom').value : '') || '';
        var td = (byId('voucherFilterTo') ? byId('voucherFilterTo').value : '') || '';
        var search = (byId('voucherSearchInput') ? byId('voucherSearchInput').value : '').toLowerCase();

        var filtered = vouchersData;
        if (type) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(v) { return v.type === type; }); }
        if (status) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(v) { return v.status === status; }); }
        if (fd) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(v) { return v.date && v.date >= fd; }); }
        if (td) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(v) { return v.date && v.date <= td; }); }
        if (search) { filtered = filtered.filter(function(v) { return v.voucherId && v.voucherId.toLowerCase().indexOf(search) !== -1; }); }

        var container2 = byId('vouchers-table-container');
        if (container2) safeHTML(container2, _renderVouchersTable(filtered));
    }

    function _viewVoucherDetails(voucherId) {
        showLoader('جاري تحميل التفاصيل...');
        if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.script && google.script.run) {
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(details) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (!details || details.length === 0) { showToast('لا توجد تفاصيل', 'info'); return; }
                    var html = '<div class="text-right"><table class="w-full border text-sm"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-2 border">الكود</th><th class="p-2 border">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الوحدة</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">المستلمة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                    for (var i = 0; i < details.length; i++) {
                        var d = details[i];
                        html += '<tr><td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(d.itemCode || '') + '</td><td class="p-2 border font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(d.itemName || '') + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + _escapeHtml(d.unit || '') + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + (d.qty || 0) + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center">' + (d.receivedQty || 0) + '</td></tr>';
                    }
                    html += '</tbody></table></div>';
                    Swal.fire({ title: 'تفاصيل الإذن: ' + _escapeHtml(voucherId), html: html, width: '700px', showConfirmButton: false, showCancelButton: true, cancelButtonText: 'إغلاق' });
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل التحميل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
                .getStockVoucherDetails(voucherId);
        }
    }

    function _sendVoucher(voucherId) {
        Swal.fire({ title: 'تأكيد الإرسال', text: 'سيتم إرسال الإذن وخصم المخزون من المصدر. متابعة؟', icon: 'warning', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#2563eb', confirmButtonText: 'نعم، أرسل', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء' }).then(function(res) {
            if (!res.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري الإرسال...');
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { hideLoader(); if (r.status === 'success') { showToast(r.msg, 'success'); loadVouchers(); } else { showToast(r.msg || 'فشل', 'error'); } }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error'); }).sendStockVoucher(voucherId);
        });
    }

    function _receiveVoucher(voucherId) {
        showLoader('جاري تحميل تفاصيل الإذن...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(details) {
                hideLoader();
                if (!details || details.length === 0) { showToast('لا توجد تفاصيل', 'info'); return; }
                var html = '<div class="text-right"><table class="w-full border text-sm"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-2 border">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الكمية المرسلة</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الكمية المستلمة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                for (var i = 0; i < details.length; i++) {
                    var d = details[i];
                    html += '<tr><td class="p-2 border font-semibold">' + _escapeHtml(d.itemName || '') + ' (' + _escapeHtml(d.itemCode || '') + ')</td><td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + (d.qty || 0) + '</td><td class="p-2 border text-center"><input type="number" id="vrec_qty_' + i + '" value="' + (d.qty || 0) + '" class="w-20 p-1 border rounded text-center" min="0"></td></tr>';
                }
                html += '</tbody></table></div>';
                Swal.fire({
                    title: 'استلام الإذن: ' + _escapeHtml(voucherId),
                    html: html, width: '700px', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'تأكيد الاستلام', confirmButtonColor: '#10b981', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
                    preConfirm: function() {
                        var items = [];
                        for (var j = 0; j < details.length; j++) {
                            var qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('vrec_qty_' + j).value) || 0;
                            items.push({ itemCode: details[j].itemCode || '', itemName: details[j].itemName || '', unit: details[j].unit || 'حبة', receivedQty: qty });
                        }
                        return items;
                    }
                }).then(function(result) {
                    if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
                    showLoader('جاري الاستلام...');
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { hideLoader(); if (r.status === 'success') { showToast(r.msg, 'success'); loadVouchers(); } else { showToast(r.msg || 'فشل', 'error'); } }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); }).receiveStockVoucher(voucherId, result.value);
                });
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
            .getStockVoucherDetails(voucherId);
    }

    function _reserveVoucher(voucherId) {
        Swal.fire({ title: 'تأكيد الحجز', text: 'سيتم حجز الكميات المطلوبة. متابعة؟', icon: 'question', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'نعم', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء' }).then(function(res) {
            if (!res.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري الحجز...');
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { hideLoader(); if (r.status === 'success') { showToast(r.msg, 'success'); loadVouchers(); } else { showToast(r.msg || 'فشل', 'error'); } }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); }).reserveStockVoucher(voucherId);
        });
    }

    function _executeVoucher(voucherId) {
        Swal.fire({ title: 'تأكيد التنفيذ', text: 'سيتم خصم الكميات من المخزون الفعلي. متابعة؟', icon: 'warning', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#e74c3c', confirmButtonText: 'نعم، نفذ', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء' }).then(function(res) {
            if (!res.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري التنفيذ...');
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { hideLoader(); if (r.status === 'success') { showToast(r.msg, 'success'); loadVouchers(); } else { showToast(r.msg || 'فشل', 'error'); } }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); }).executeStockVoucher(voucherId);
        });
    }

    function _cancelVoucher(voucherId) {
        Swal.fire({ title: 'تأكيد الإلغاء', text: 'هل أنت متأكد من إلغاء هذا الإذن؟', icon: 'warning', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#e74c3c', confirmButtonText: 'نعم', cancelButtonText: 'تراجع' }).then(function(res) {
            if (!res.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري الإلغاء...');
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { hideLoader(); if (r.status === 'success') { showToast(r.msg, 'success'); loadVouchers(); } else { showToast(r.msg || 'فشل', 'error'); } }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); }).cancelStockVoucher(voucherId);
        });
    }

    function _openNewVoucherModal() {
        var html = '<div class="text-right space-y-3">' +
            '<div><label class="text-xs font-bold">نوع الإذن</label><select id="newVoucherType" class="swal2-input w-full"><option value="Transfer">تحويل داخلي</option><option value="DirectSale">صرف سيارة بيع مباشر</option><option value="DirectReturn">استلام مرتجع سيارة</option><option value="SupplierReturn">مرتجع لمورد</option><option value="Adjustment">جرد</option></select></div>' +
            '<div><label class="text-xs font-bold">المرجع (اختياري)</label><input id="newVoucherRef" class="swal2-input w-full" placeholder="رقم مرجعي"></div>' +
            '<div><label class="text-xs font-bold">ملاحظات</label><textarea id="newVoucherNotes" rows="2" class="swal2-input w-full"></textarea></div></div>';
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'إنشاء إذن مخزني جديد', html: html, showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'إنشاء', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            preConfirm: function() {
                var type = document.getElementById('newVoucherType').value;
                var ref = document.getElementById('newVoucherRef').value.trim();
                var notes = document.getElementById('newVoucherNotes').value.trim();
                if (!type) { Swal.showValidationMessage('اختر نوع الإذن'); return false; }
                return { type: type, ref: ref, notes: notes };
            }
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
            var d = result.value;
            showLoader('جاري الإنشاء...');
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (res.status === 'success') {
                        showToast('تم إنشاء الإذن ' + res.voucherId, 'success');
                        loadVouchers();
                    } else { showToast(res.msg || 'فشل الإنشاء', 'error'); }
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
                .createStockVoucher(d.type, d.ref, 'Branch', 'MAIN', 'Branch', '', [], d.notes);
        });
    }

    // ==================== نماذج إنشاء الأذونات حسب النوع ====================
    function loadVoucherForm(type) {
        voucherCart = [];
        currentVoucherType = type;
        var config = {
            'Transfer': { title: 'تحويل مخزني', entityLabel: 'الفرع المحول إليه', showPrice: false, fromType: 'Branch', fromId: 'MAIN', toType: 'Branch', toId: '' },
            'DirectSale': { title: 'صرف سيارة بيع مباشر', entityLabel: 'المندوب / السيارة', showPrice: true, fromType: 'Branch', fromId: 'MAIN', toType: 'Vehicle', toId: '' },
            'DirectReturn': { title: 'استلام مرتجع سيارة', entityLabel: 'المندوب / السيارة', showPrice: true, fromType: 'Vehicle', fromId: '', toType: 'Branch', toId: 'MAIN' },
            'SupplierReturn': { title: 'مرتجع لمورد', entityLabel: 'المورد', showPrice: true, fromType: 'Branch', fromId: 'MAIN', toType: 'Supplier', toId: '' }
        };
        var c = config[type];
        if (!c) { showToast('نوع غير معروف', 'error'); return; }
        currentVoucherParams = { fromType: c.fromType, fromId: c.fromId, toType: c.toType, toId: c.toId };
        currentEntityLabel = c.entityLabel;
        showVoucherPrice = c.showPrice;

        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4">' +
            '<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4"><h2 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-file-signature ml-2 text-indigo-600"></i>' + c.title + '</h2><button onclick="RW_Warehouse.loadVouchers()" class="text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark text-xl"></i></button></div>' +
            '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-4">' +
            '<div><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">' + c.entityLabel + '</label><select id="voucherEntitySelect" class="border rounded-lg p-2 w-full"><option value="">-- اختر --</option></select></div>' +
            '<div><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">ملاحظات</label><textarea id="voucherNotesLarge" rows="2" class="border rounded-lg p-2 w-full" placeholder="ملاحظات..."></textarea></div>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">بحث عن صنف</label><div class="relative"><input type="text" id="voucherItemSearch" oninput="RW_Warehouse._searchVoucherItem(this.value)" autocomplete="off" placeholder="ابحث بالاسم أو الباركود..." class="border rounded-lg p-2 w-full"><div id="voucherSearchResults" class="absolute z-50 left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-white shadow-xl rounded-xl max-h-60 overflow-y-auto hidden border"></div></div></div>' +
            '<div class="mb-4 overflow-y-auto" style="max-height:300px;" id="voucherItemsTable"><div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-400">أضف أصنافاً</div></div>' +
            '<div class="p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg flex justify-between items-center mb-4"><span class="font-bold">عدد الأصناف: <span id="voucherTotalItems">0</span></span></div>' +
            '<div class="flex justify-end gap-3"><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._clearVoucherCart()" class="px-4 py-2 bg-gray-500 text-white rounded-lg font-bold">مسح الكل</button><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._saveAndSendVoucher()" class="px-6 py-2 bg-indigo-600 text-white rounded-lg font-bold">حفظ وإرسال (Sent)</button></div></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);
        _loadVoucherEntityOptions(type);
        _renderVoucherCart();
    }

    function _loadVoucherEntityOptions(type) {
        var select = byId('voucherEntitySelect');
        if (!select) return;
        if (type === 'Transfer') {
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(branches) {
                var html = '<option value="">-- اختر فرعاً --</option>';
                for (var i = 0; i < branches.length; i++) {
                    html += '<option value="' + _escapeHtml(branches[i].branch_code || branches[i].id || '') + '">' + _escapeHtml(branches[i].name || branches[i].branch_name || '') + '</option>';
                }
                safeHTML(select, html);
            }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { showToast('فشل تحميل الفروع', 'error'); }).getBranches();
        } else if (type === 'SupplierReturn') {
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(suppliers) {
                var html = '<option value="">-- اختر مورداً --</option>';
                for (var i = 0; i < suppliers.length; i++) {
                    html += '<option value="' + _escapeHtml(suppliers[i].code || suppliers[i].id || '') + '">' + _escapeHtml(suppliers[i].name || '') + '</option>';
                }
                safeHTML(select, html);
            }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { showToast('فشل تحميل الموردين', 'error'); }).getSuppliersList();
        } else if (type === 'DirectSale' || type === 'DirectReturn') {
            google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                var html = '<option value="">-- اختر مندوباً --</option>';
                var drivers = data.drivers || [];
                for (var i = 0; i < drivers.length; i++) {
                    html += '<option value="' + _escapeHtml(drivers[i].email || '') + '">' + _escapeHtml(drivers[i].name || '') + ' (' + _escapeHtml(drivers[i].email || '') + ')</option>';
                }
                safeHTML(select, html);
            }).withFailureHandler(function(err) { showToast('فشل تحميل المناديب', 'error'); }).getDriversAndVehicles();
        }
    }

    function _searchVoucherItem(query) {
        var div = byId('voucherSearchResults');
        if (!div) return;
        if (!query || query.trim().length < 1) { div.classList.add('hidden'); return; }
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
        var q = query.toLowerCase();
        var filtered = items.filter(function(i) { return (String(i.name || '') + String(i.code || '') + String(i.barcode || '')).toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1; });
        if (filtered.length > 0) {
            var html = '';
            for (var idx = 0; idx < Math.min(filtered.length, 20); idx++) {
                var item = filtered[idx];
                html += '<div onclick="RW_Warehouse._addVoucherItem(\'' + _escapeHtml(item.code || '') + '\')" class="p-3 hover:bg-indigo-50 cursor-pointer flex justify-between border-b"><div><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(item.name || '') + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-400">' + _escapeHtml(item.code || '') + '</div></div><div class="font-bold text-indigo-600">' + (item.stock || 0) + ' ' + _escapeHtml(item.unit || '') + '</div></div>';
            }
            safeHTML(div, html);
            div.classList.remove('hidden');
        } else { safeHTML(div, '<div class="p-3 text-center text-gray-400">لا توجد نتائج</div>'); div.classList.remove('hidden'); }
    }

    function _addVoucherItem(itemCode) {
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
        var item = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) { if (items[i].code === itemCode) { item = items[i]; break; } }
        if (!item) return;
        var existing = null;
        for (var j = 0; j < voucherCart.length; j++) { if (voucherCart[j].code === itemCode) { existing = voucherCart[j]; break; } }
        if (existing) { existing.qty++; } else {
            voucherCart.push({ code: item.code, name: item.name, unit: item.unit || 'حبة', qty: 1, price: showVoucherPrice ? (Number(item.sPrice) || 0) : 0 });
        }
        var searchInput = byId('voucherItemSearch');
        if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
        var dropdown = byId('voucherSearchResults');
        if (dropdown) dropdown.classList.add('hidden');
        _renderVoucherCart();
    }

    function _renderVoucherCart() {
        var tbody = byId('voucherItemsTable');
        var countSpan = byId('voucherTotalItems');
        if (voucherCart.length === 0) { safeHTML(tbody, '<div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-400">أضف أصنافاً</div>'); if (countSpan) countSpan.innerText = '0'; return; }
        var html = '<table class="w-full text-right border"><thead class="bg-gray-100 text-xs uppercase"><tr><th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية</th>';
        if (showVoucherPrice) html += '<th class="p-2 text-center">السعر</th>';
        html += '<th class="p-2 text-center">حذف</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < voucherCart.length; i++) {
            var item = voucherCart[i];
            html += '<tr class="border-b"><td class="p-2"><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(item.name) + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-400">' + _escapeHtml(item.code) + '</div></td>' +
                '<td class="p-2 text-center"><input type="number" value="' + item.qty + '" onchange="RW_Warehouse._updateVoucherQty(' + i + ', this.value)" class="w-16 p-1 border rounded text-center" min="1"></td>';
            if (showVoucherPrice) html += '<td class="p-2 text-center"><input type="number" value="' + item.price + '" onchange="RW_Warehouse._updateVoucherPrice(' + i + ', this.value)" class="w-20 p-1 border rounded text-center" step="0.01" min="0"></td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 text-center"><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._removeVoucherItem(' + i + ')" class="text-red-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></td></tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table>';
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
        if (countSpan) countSpan.innerText = String(voucherCart.length);
    }

    function _updateVoucherQty(idx, val) { var q = parseInt(val); if (q > 0) voucherCart[idx].qty = q; else voucherCart.splice(idx, 1); _renderVoucherCart(); }
    function _updateVoucherPrice(idx, val) { voucherCart[idx].price = parseFloat(val) || 0; _renderVoucherCart(); }
    function _removeVoucherItem(idx) { voucherCart.splice(idx, 1); _renderVoucherCart(); }
    function _clearVoucherCart() { voucherCart = []; _renderVoucherCart(); }

    function _saveAndSendVoucher() {
        if (voucherCart.length === 0) { showToast('أضف أصنافاً للإذن', 'warning'); return; }
        var entity = byId('voucherEntitySelect') ? byId('voucherEntitySelect').value : '';
        if (!entity) { showToast('يرجى اختيار ' + currentEntityLabel, 'warning'); return; }
        var notes = byId('voucherNotesLarge') ? byId('voucherNotesLarge').value : '';
        var params = currentVoucherParams;
        if (params.toType === 'Branch' && currentVoucherType === 'Transfer') params.toId = entity;
        else if (params.toType === 'Vehicle') params.toId = entity;
        else if (params.toType === 'Supplier') params.toId = entity;
        else if (params.fromType === 'Vehicle') params.fromId = entity;

        var items = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < voucherCart.length; i++) {
            items.push({ itemCode: voucherCart[i].code, qty: voucherCart[i].qty, unitPrice: voucherCart[i].price || 0, notes: '' });
        }

        showLoader('جاري حفظ وإرسال الإذن...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(createRes) {
                if (createRes.status !== 'success') { hideLoader(); showToast(createRes.msg || 'فشل الحفظ', 'error'); return; }
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(sendRes) {
                        hideLoader();
                        if (sendRes.status === 'success') {
                            showToast('تم إنشاء وإرسال الإذن ' + createRes.voucherId, 'success');
                            voucherCart = [];
                            _renderVoucherCart();
                        } else { showToast(sendRes.msg || 'فشل الإرسال', 'error'); }
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
                    .sendStockVoucher(createRes.voucherId);
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل الاتصال: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
            .createStockVoucher(currentVoucherType, '', params.fromType, params.fromId, params.toType, params.toId, items, notes);
    }
        // ==================== الجرد (Inventory Count) ====================
    var invCountCart = [];
    var currentInvType = '';
    var barcodeActive = false;
    var barcodeStream = null;
    var lastScannedBarcode = '';
    var scanCooldown = false;

    function _startBarcodeScanner(prefix) {
        if (barcodeActive) {
            _stopBarcodeScanner();
            return;
        }
        if (!('BarcodeDetector' in window)) {
            showToast('متصفحك لا يدعم ماسح الباركود. استخدم البحث اليدوي.', 'warning');
            return;
        }
        barcodeActive = true;
        lastScannedBarcode = '';
        navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: { facingMode: 'environment' } }).then(function(stream) {
            barcodeStream = stream;
            var detector = new BarcodeDetector({ formats: ['ean_13', 'ean_8', 'code_128', 'code_39', 'qr_code'] });
            function scanLoop() {
                if (!barcodeActive) return;
                detector.detect(stream.getVideoTracks()[0]).then(function(barcodes) {
                    if (barcodes.length > 0) {
                        var code = barcodes[0].rawValue;
                        if (code !== lastScannedBarcode && !scanCooldown) {
                            lastScannedBarcode = code;
                            scanCooldown = true;
                            var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
                            var found = null;
                            for (var f = 0; f < items.length; f++) {
                                if (String(items[f].barcode || '') === code || String(items[f].code || '') === code) {
                                    found = items[f];
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            if (found) {
                                _addToInvCart(prefix, found.code);
                                showToast('تم: ' + found.name, 'success');
                            } else {
                                showToast('صنف غير معروف: ' + code, 'warning');
                            }
                            setTimeout(function() { scanCooldown = false; }, 1500);
                        }
                    }
                });
                requestAnimationFrame(scanLoop);
            }
            requestAnimationFrame(scanLoop);
        }).catch(function(err) {
            barcodeActive = false;
            showToast('تعذر الوصول للكاميرا', 'error');
        });
    }

    function _stopBarcodeScanner() {
        barcodeActive = false;
        if (barcodeStream) {
            barcodeStream.getTracks().forEach(function(t) { t.stop(); });
            barcodeStream = null;
        }
    }

    function _smartSearchInvItems(prefix, query) {
        var div = byId(prefix + '-item-results');
        if (!div) return;
        if (!query || query.trim().length < 1) { div.classList.add('hidden'); return; }
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
        var q = query.toLowerCase();
        var filtered = items.filter(function(i) { return (String(i.name || '') + String(i.code || '') + String(i.barcode || '') + String(i.cat || '')).toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1; });
        if (filtered.length > 0) {
            var html = '';
            for (var idx = 0; idx < Math.min(filtered.length, 30); idx++) {
                var item = filtered[idx];
                html += '<div onclick="RW_Warehouse._addToInvCart(\'' + prefix + '\', \'' + _escapeHtml(item.code || '') + '\')" class="p-3 hover:bg-blue-50 cursor-pointer border-b flex items-center"><div><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(item.name || '') + '</div><div class="text-xs text-slate-400">كود: ' + _escapeHtml(item.code || '') + ' | رصيد: ' + (item.stock || 0) + '</div></div></div>';
            }
            safeHTML(div, html);
            div.classList.remove('hidden');
        } else { safeHTML(div, '<div class="p-3 text-center text-gray-400">لا توجد نتائج</div>'); div.classList.remove('hidden'); }
    }

    function _addToInvCart(prefix, itemCode) {
        var items = RW_STATE.data.items || [];
        var item = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) { if (items[i].code === itemCode) { item = items[i]; break; } }
        if (!item) return;
        var existing = null;
        for (var j = 0; j < invCountCart.length; j++) { if (invCountCart[j].code === itemCode) { existing = invCountCart[j]; break; } }
        if (existing) { existing.qty = (parseInt(existing.qty) || 0) + 1; } else {
            invCountCart.push({ code: item.code, name: item.name, unit: item.unit || 'حبة', qty: 1 });
        }
        var searchInput = byId(prefix + '-item-search');
        if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
        var dropdown = byId(prefix + '-item-results');
        if (dropdown) dropdown.classList.add('hidden');
        _renderInvCart(prefix);
    }

    function _renderInvCart(prefix) {
        var tbody = byId(prefix + '-cart-table');
        var countSpan = byId(prefix + '-cart-count');
        if (!tbody) return;
        if (invCountCart.length === 0) { safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="4" class="p-6 text-center">أضف أصنافاً</td></tr>'); if (countSpan) countSpan.innerText = '0'; return; }
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < invCountCart.length; i++) {
            var it = invCountCart[i];
            html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-slate-50"><td class="p-2"><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(it.name) + '</div><div class="text-xs">' + _escapeHtml(it.code) + '</div></td><td class="p-2 text-center">' + _escapeHtml(it.unit) + '</td><td class="p-2 text-center"><input type="number" value="' + it.qty + '" onchange="RW_Warehouse._updateInvCartQty(' + i + ', this.value, \'' + prefix + '\')" class="w-20 p-1 border rounded text-center" min="0"></td><td class="p-2 text-center"><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._removeInvCartItem(' + i + ', \'' + prefix + '\')" class="text-red-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button></td></tr>';
        }
        safeHTML(tbody, html);
        if (countSpan) countSpan.innerText = String(invCountCart.length);
    }

    function _updateInvCartQty(idx, val, prefix) {
        var q = parseInt(val);
        if (isNaN(q) || q <= 0) { invCountCart.splice(idx, 1); } else { invCountCart[idx].qty = q; }
        _renderInvCart(prefix);
    }

    function _removeInvCartItem(idx, prefix) { invCountCart.splice(idx, 1); _renderInvCart(prefix); }

    function _saveInvCount(type, entityId, reference) {
        if (invCountCart.length === 0) { showToast('أضف أصنافاً', 'warning'); return; }
        var items = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < invCountCart.length; i++) {
            items.push({ itemCode: invCountCart[i].code, itemName: invCountCart[i].name, unit: invCountCart[i].unit, qty: parseInt(invCountCart[i].qty) || 0, unitPrice: 0, notes: '' });
        }
        showLoader('جاري حفظ الجرد...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                hideLoader();
                if (res.status === 'success') {
                    showToast(res.msg + ' (' + res.voucherId + ')', 'success');
                    invCountCart = [];
                    var prefix = type === 'vehicle' ? 'vc' : (type === 'branch' ? 'bc' : 'gc');
                    _renderInvCart(prefix);
                } else { showToast(res.msg || 'فشل الحفظ', 'error'); }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
            .saveInventoryCount(type, entityId, reference, items);
    }

    // ---------- جرد سيارة ----------
    function loadVehicleCount() {
        currentInvType = 'vehicle';
        invCountCart = [];
        _stopBarcodeScanner();
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'جرد سيارة');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'جرد عهدة مندوب أو سيارة');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4 grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">' +
            '<div><label class="text-xs font-bold block mb-1">المندوب</label><input type="text" id="vc-driver-search" oninput="RW_Warehouse._smartSearchDriver(this.value)" autocomplete="off" placeholder="ابحث باسم أو بريد المندوب..." class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-slate-200 focus:border-blue-500 outline-none"><div id="vc-driver-results" class="absolute z-50 bg-white shadow-xl rounded-xl max-h-48 overflow-y-auto hidden border mt-1" style="width:calc(33%-2rem);"></div></div>' +
            '<div><label class="text-xs font-bold block mb-1">الرانشيت (اختياري)</label><select id="vc-runsheet-select" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-slate-200 font-bold"><option value="">-- اختر --</option></select></div>' +
            '<div><label class="text-xs font-bold block mb-1">ملاحظات</label><input id="vc-notes" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-slate-200" placeholder="ملاحظات..."></div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4 relative"><label class="text-xs font-bold block mb-2">البحث عن صنف</label><div class="relative"><input type="text" id="vc-item-search" oninput="RW_Warehouse._smartSearchInvItems(\'vc\', this.value)" autocomplete="off" placeholder="امسح الباركود أو ابحث..." class="w-full p-4 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2 focus:border-emerald-500 outline-none font-bold text-lg"><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._startBarcodeScanner(\'vc\')" class="absolute left-2 top-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white p-3 rounded-xl"><i class="fa-solid fa-camera"></i></button></div><div id="vc-item-results" class="absolute z-50 left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-white shadow-xl rounded-xl max-h-60 overflow-y-auto hidden border"></div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm overflow-auto" style="max-height:50vh;"><table class="w-full"><thead class="bg-slate-800 text-white"><tr><th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الوحدة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 text-center">حذف</th></tr></thead><tbody id="vc-cart-table"><tr><td colspan="4" class="p-6 text-center">أضف أصنافاً</td></tr></tbody></table></div>' +
            '<div class="mt-2">عدد الأصناف: <span id="vc-cart-count">0</span></div>' +
            '<div class="mt-4 flex justify-end gap-3"><button onclick="invCountCart=[]; RW_Warehouse._renderInvCart(\'vc\')" class="bg-gray-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold text-sm">مسح الكل</button><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._saveVehicleCount()" class="bg-blue-600 text-white px-8 py-3 rounded-2xl font-black text-lg shadow-lg"><i class="fa-solid fa-check ml-2"></i> حفظ الجرد</button></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
            var sel = byId('vc-runsheet-select');
            if (sel && data) {
                for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                    sel.innerHTML += '<option value="' + _escapeHtml(data[i].rsId || '') + '">' + _escapeHtml(data[i].rsId || '') + ' - ' + _escapeHtml(data[i].driverEmail || '') + '</option>';
                }
            }
        }).withFailureHandler(function() {}).getRunsheetsForVehicleCount();
    }

    function _smartSearchDriver(query) {
        var div = byId('vc-driver-results');
        if (!div) return;
        if (!query || query.trim().length < 1) { div.classList.add('hidden'); return; }
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
            var drivers = data.drivers || [];
            var q = query.toLowerCase();
            var filtered = drivers.filter(function(d) { return (d.name || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1 || (d.email || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1; });
            if (filtered.length > 0) {
                var html = '';
                for (var i = 0; i < filtered.length; i++) {
                    var d = filtered[i];
                    html += '<div onclick="RW_Warehouse._selectDriver(\'' + _escapeHtml(d.email) + '\', \'' + _escapeHtml(d.name || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\')" class="p-3 hover:bg-blue-50 cursor-pointer border-b"><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(d.name) + '</div><div class="text-xs text-slate-400">' + _escapeHtml(d.email) + '</div></div>';
                }
                safeHTML(div, html);
                div.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else { safeHTML(div, '<div class="p-3 text-center">لا توجد نتائج</div>'); div.classList.remove('hidden'); }
        }).withFailureHandler(function() {}).getDriversAndVehicles();
    }

    function _selectDriver(email, name) {
        window._selectedDriver = email;
        var search = byId('vc-driver-search');
        if (search) search.value = name + ' (' + email + ')';
        var results = byId('vc-driver-results');
        if (results) results.classList.add('hidden');
    }

    function _saveVehicleCount() {
        var entityId = window._selectedDriver || '';
        if (!entityId) { showToast('يجب اختيار مندوب', 'warning'); return; }
        var reference = (byId('vc-runsheet-select') ? byId('vc-runsheet-select').value : '') || '';
        var notes = (byId('vc-notes') ? byId('vc-notes').value : '') || '';
        if (notes) reference = reference ? reference + ' | ' + notes : notes;
        _saveInvCount('vehicle', entityId, reference || 'جرد سيارة');
    }

    // ---------- جرد فرع ----------
    function loadBranchCount() {
        currentInvType = 'branch';
        invCountCart = [];
        _stopBarcodeScanner();

            '<div><label class="text-xs font-bold block mb-1">ملاحظات</label><input id="bc-notes" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-slate-200" placeholder="ملاحظات..."></div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4 relative"><label class="text-xs font-bold block mb-2">البحث عن صنف</label><div class="relative"><input type="text" id="bc-item-search" oninput="RW_Warehouse._smartSearchInvItems(\'bc\', this.value)" autocomplete="off" placeholder="امسح الباركود أو ابحث..." class="w-full p-4 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2 focus:border-emerald-500 outline-none font-bold text-lg"><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._startBarcodeScanner(\'bc\')" class="absolute left-2 top-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white p-3 rounded-xl"><i class="fa-solid fa-camera"></i></button></div><div id="bc-item-results" class="absolute z-50 left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-white shadow-xl rounded-xl max-h-60 overflow-y-auto hidden border"></div></div>' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm overflow-auto" style="max-height:50vh;"><table class="w-full"><thead class="bg-slate-800 text-white"><tr><th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الوحدة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">الكمية</th><th class="p-2 text-center">حذف</th></tr></thead><tbody id="bc-cart-table"><tr><td colspan="4" class="p-6 text-center">أضف أصنافاً</td></tr></tbody></table></div>' +
            '<div class="mt-2">عدد الأصناف: <span id="bc-cart-count">0</span></div>' +
            '<div class="mt-4 flex justify-end gap-3"><button onclick="invCountCart=[]; RW_Warehouse._renderInvCart(\'bc\')" class="bg-gray-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold text-sm">مسح الكل</button><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._saveBranchCount()" class="bg-blue-600 text-white px-8 py-3 rounded-2xl font-black text-lg shadow-lg"><i class="fa-solid fa-check ml-2"></i> حفظ الجرد</button></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);
    }

    function _saveBranchCount() {
        var entityId = (byId('bc-branch-select') ? byId('bc-branch-select').value : '') || '';
        if (!entityId) { showToast('يجب اختيار فرع', 'warning'); return; }
        var section = (byId('bc-section') ? byId('bc-section').value : '') || '';
        var notes = (byId('bc-notes') ? byId('bc-notes').value : '') || '';
        var reference = section ? ('قسم: ' + section) : '';
        if (notes) reference = reference ? reference + ' | ' + notes : notes;
        _saveInvCount('branch', entityId, reference || 'جرد فرع');
    }
