    function _saveGeneralCount() {
        var entityId = (byId('gc-branch-select') ? byId('gc-branch-select').value : '') || 'MAIN';
        var section = (byId('gc-section') ? byId('gc-section').value : '') || '';
        var notes = (byId('gc-notes') ? byId('gc-notes').value : '') || '';
        var reference = 'جرد عام';
        if (section) reference = reference + ' - ' + section;
        if (notes) reference = reference + ' | ' + notes;
        _saveInvCount('general', entityId, reference);
    }
        // ==================== إغلاق اليومية (Daily Settlement) ====================
    var settlementData = null;

    function loadSettlement() {
        var container = byId('rw-page-container');
        if (!container) return;
        safeText(byId('rw-header-title'), 'إغلاق اليومية');
        safeText(byId('rw-header-subtitle'), 'تسوية عهدة المندوب وترحيل العجز');

        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 mb-4">' +
            '<label class="text-xs font-bold block mb-2">اختيار الرانشيت</label>' +
            '<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">' +
            '<div class="md:col-span-2"><select id="settlement-rs-select" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2 border-slate-200 font-bold" onchange="RW_Warehouse._onSettlementRsChange()"><option value="">-- اختر رانشيتاً --</option></select></div>' +
            '<div><button onclick="RW_Warehouse._loadSettlementsList()" class="w-full p-3 bg-indigo-100 text-indigo-700 rounded-xl font-bold">عرض التسويات السابقة</button></div>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div id="settlement-rs-info" class="mt-3 text-sm text-slate-500"></div></div>' +
            '<div id="settlement-details-container" class="hidden">' +
            '<div class="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm overflow-auto mb-4" style="max-height:50vh;"><table class="w-full"><thead class="bg-slate-800 text-white sticky top-0"><tr>' +
            '<th class="p-2">الصنف</th><th class="p-2 text-center">محمّلة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">مسلّمة</th>' +
            '<th class="p-2 text-center">مرتجعة</th><th class="p-2 text-center">مجرودة</th>' +
            '<th class="p-2 text-center">العجز</th><th class="p-2 text-center">قيمة العجز</th></tr></thead>' +
            '<tbody id="settlement-items-body"><tr><td colspan="7" class="p-6 text-center">اختر رانشيتاً</td></tr></tbody></table></div>' +
            '<div id="settlement-summary" class="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm mb-4 hidden">' +
            '<div class="grid grid-cols-4 gap-4">' +
            '<div class="text-center"><span class="text-xs text-gray-500">إجمالي العجز</span><div id="sum-shortage" class="text-2xl font-black text-red-600">0</div></div>' +
            '<div class="text-center"><span class="text-xs text-gray-500">قيمة العجز</span><div id="sum-shortage-value" class="text-2xl font-black text-red-600">0</div></div>' +
            '<div class="text-center"><span class="text-xs text-gray-500">أصناف إضافية</span><div id="sum-extra" class="text-2xl font-black text-amber-600">0</div></div>' +
            '<div class="text-center"><span class="text-xs text-gray-500">الجرد المرجعي</span><div id="sum-voucher" class="text-sm font-bold text-blue-600">---</div></div></div></div>' +
            '<div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between gap-2 mt-4">' +
            '<div class="flex-1"><input id="settlement-notes" class="w-full p-3 bg-slate-50 rounded-xl border-2" placeholder="ملاحظات التسوية..."></div>' +
            '<div class="flex gap-2">' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._resetSettlement()" class="bg-gray-500 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-2xl font-black">إلغاء</button>' +
            '<button onclick="RW_Warehouse._saveSettlement()" class="bg-emerald-600 text-white px-8 py-3 rounded-2xl font-black shadow-lg"><i class="fa-solid fa-check ml-2"></i> حفظ التسوية وترحيل العجز</button></div></div></div>';
        safeHTML(container, html);

        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                var sel = byId('settlement-rs-select');
                if (sel && data) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                        sel.innerHTML += '<option value="' + _escapeHtml(data[i].rsId || '') + '">' + _escapeHtml(data[i].rsId || '') + ' - ' + _escapeHtml(data[i].driverEmail || '') + '</option>';
                    }
                }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function() {})
            .getRunsheetsForVehicleCount();
    }

    function _onSettlementRsChange() {
        var rsId = (byId('settlement-rs-select') ? byId('settlement-rs-select').value : '') || '';
        if (!rsId) {
            var detailsContainer = byId('settlement-details-container');
            if (detailsContainer) detailsContainer.classList.add('hidden');
            return;
        }
        showLoader('جاري تحميل بيانات التسوية...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                hideLoader();
                if (data.status !== 'success') { showToast(data.msg || 'فشل التحميل', 'error'); return; }
                settlementData = data;
                var infoDiv = byId('settlement-rs-info');
                if (infoDiv) {
                    var rsInfo = data.runsheet || {};
                    infoDiv.innerHTML = '<strong>المندوب:</strong> ' + _escapeHtml(rsInfo.driverEmail || '---') +
                        ' | <strong>السيارة:</strong> ' + _escapeHtml(rsInfo.vehicleId || '---') +
                        ' | <strong>التاريخ:</strong> ' + _escapeHtml(rsInfo.date || '---');
                }
                var tbody = byId('settlement-items-body');
                if (!data.items || data.items.length === 0) {
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, '<tr><td colspan="7" class="p-6 text-center">لا توجد بيانات مقارنة لهذا الرانشيت</td></tr>');
                } else {
                    var html = '';
                    for (var i = 0; i < data.items.length; i++) {
                        var it = data.items[i];
                        var shortageClass = it.shortage > 0 ? 'text-red-600 font-bold' : (it.shortage < 0 ? 'text-green-600 font-bold' : '');
                        html += '<tr class="border-b hover:bg-slate-50"><td class="p-2"><div class="font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemName || '') + '</div><div class="text-xs text-gray-400">' + _escapeHtml(it.itemCode || '') + '</div></td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 text-center">' + (it.loadedQty || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 text-center">' + (it.deliveredQty || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 text-center">' + (it.returnedQty || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 text-center font-bold">' + (it.countedQty || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 text-center ' + shortageClass + '">' + (it.shortage || 0) + '</td>' +
                            '<td class="p-2 text-center">' + (Math.abs(it.shortageValue || 0)).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td></tr>';
                    }
                    if (tbody) safeHTML(tbody, html);
                }
                var summaryDiv = byId('settlement-summary');
                if (summaryDiv) summaryDiv.classList.remove('hidden');
                safeText(byId('sum-shortage'), String(data.totalShortage || 0));
                safeText(byId('sum-shortage-value'), (data.totalShortageValue || 0).toLocaleString() + ' EGP');
                safeText(byId('sum-extra'), String(data.extraItemsCount || 0));
                safeText(byId('sum-voucher'), data.inventoryVoucherId || 'لا يوجد');
                var detailsContainer = byId('settlement-details-container');
                if (detailsContainer) detailsContainer.classList.remove('hidden');
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
                hideLoader();
                showToast('فشل التحميل: ' + err.message, 'error');
            })
            .getDailySettlementData(rsId);
    }

    function _resetSettlement() {
        settlementData = null;
        var detailsContainer = byId('settlement-details-container');
        if (detailsContainer) detailsContainer.classList.add('hidden');
        var sel = byId('settlement-rs-select');
        if (sel) sel.value = '';
        var info = byId('settlement-rs-info');
        if (info) info.innerHTML = '';
    }

    function _saveSettlement() {
        if (!settlementData) { showToast('اختر رانشيتاً أولاً', 'warning'); return; }
        var notes = (byId('settlement-notes') ? byId('settlement-notes').value : '') || '';
        var rs = settlementData.runsheet || {};
        var driverEmail = rs.driverEmail || '';
        var driverName = rs.driverEmail || '';
        var vehicleId = rs.vehicleId || '';
        var inventoryVoucherId = settlementData.inventoryVoucherId || '';

        var totalShortageValue = settlementData.totalShortageValue || 0;
        var totalShortage = settlementData.totalShortage || 0;
        var extraCount = settlementData.extraItemsCount || 0;

        var confirmMsg = 'سيتم حفظ تسوية إغلاق اليومية وترحيل العجز كمديونية إضافية على المندوب.\n\n';
        confirmMsg += 'المندوب: ' + driverEmail + '\n';
        confirmMsg += 'إجمالي العجز: ' + totalShortage + ' قطعة\n';
        confirmMsg += 'قيمة العجز: ' + totalShortageValue.toLocaleString() + ' EGP\n';
        if (extraCount > 0) confirmMsg += 'أصناف إضافية مكتشفة: ' + extraCount + '\n';
        confirmMsg += '\nملاحظة: هذا يضاف إلى رصيد المندوب التراكمي ولا يُصفّر عهدته.';

        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد حفظ التسوية',
            text: confirmMsg,
            icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonColor: '#10b981',
            confirmButtonText: 'نعم، حفظ وترحيل',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(result) {
            if (!result.isConfirmed) return;
            showLoader('جاري حفظ التسوية...');
            google.script.run
                .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
                    hideLoader();
                    if (res.status === 'success') {
                        showToast(res.msg + ' (' + res.settlementId + ')', 'success');
                        _resetSettlement();
                    } else { showToast(res.msg || 'فشل الحفظ', 'error'); }
                })
                .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
                .saveDailySettlement(rs.rsId || '', driverEmail, driverName, vehicleId, inventoryVoucherId, settlementData.items || [], notes);
        });
    }

    function _loadSettlementsList() {
        showLoader('جاري تحميل التسويات...');
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                hideLoader();
                if (!data || data.length === 0) { showToast('لا توجد تسويات سابقة', 'info'); return; }
                var html = '<div class="text-right"><table class="w-full border text-sm"><thead class="bg-gray-100"><tr><th class="p-2 border">كود التسوية</th><th class="p-2 border">التاريخ</th><th class="p-2 border">الرانشيت</th><th class="p-2 border">المندوب</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">العجز</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">قيمة العجز</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">الحالة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
                for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
                    var s = data[i];
                    html += '<tr class="border-b"><td class="p-2 border font-bold">' + _escapeHtml(s.settlement_code || s.settlementId || '') + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(s.settlement_date || s.date || '') + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(s.runsheet_id || s.rsId || '---') + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="p-2 border">' + _escapeHtml(s.driver_id || s.driverName || '---') + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold">' + (s.total_shortage || s.totalShortage || 0) + '</td>' +
                        '<td class="p-2 border text-center font-bold text-red-600">' + (Number(s.total_shortage_value || s.totalShortageValue || 0)).toLocaleString() + ' EGP</td>' +
                        '<td class="p-2 border text-center"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold bg-green-100 text-green-700">' + _escapeHtml(s.status || 'مكتمل') + '</span></td></tr>';
                }
                html += '</tbody></table></div>';
                Swal.fire({ title: 'التسويات السابقة', html: html, width: '900px', showConfirmButton: false, showCancelButton: true, cancelButtonText: 'إغلاق' });
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideLoader(); showToast('فشل التحميل: ' + err.message, 'error'); })
            .getSettlementsList();
    }
    return {
        loadPicking: loadPicking,
        _applyPickingFilters: _applyPickingFilters,
        _sortPickingTable: _sortPickingTable,
        _openPickingModal: _openPickingModal,
        loadLoading: loadLoading,
        _applyLoadingFilters: _applyLoadingFilters,
        _sortLoadingTable: _sortLoadingTable,
        _openLoadingModal: _openLoadingModal,
        loadDelivery: loadDelivery,
        _applyDeliveryFilters: _applyDeliveryFilters,
        _sortDeliveryTable: _sortDeliveryTable,
        _openDeliveryModal: _openDeliveryModal,
        _updateRefusedAuto: _updateRefusedAuto,
        loadReturn: loadReturn,
        _applyReturnFilters: _applyReturnFilters,
        _sortReturnTable: _sortReturnTable,
        _openReturnModal: _openReturnModal,
        loadUnloading: loadUnloading,
        _applyUnloadingFilters: _applyUnloadingFilters,
        _sortUnloadingTable: _sortUnloadingTable,
        _confirmUnload: _confirmUnload,
        loadReceiving: loadReceiving,
        _applyReceivingFilters: _applyReceivingFilters,
        _sortReceivingTable: _sortReceivingTable,
        _showReceivingDetails: _showReceivingDetails,
        loadVouchers: loadVouchers,
        _applyVoucherFilters: _applyVoucherFilters,
        _viewVoucherDetails: _viewVoucherDetails,
        _sendVoucher: _sendVoucher,
        _receiveVoucher: _receiveVoucher,
        _reserveVoucher: _reserveVoucher,
        _executeVoucher: _executeVoucher,
        _cancelVoucher: _cancelVoucher,
        _openNewVoucherModal: _openNewVoucherModal,
        loadVoucherForm: loadVoucherForm,
        _searchVoucherItem: _searchVoucherItem,
        _addVoucherItem: _addVoucherItem,
        _updateVoucherQty: _updateVoucherQty,
        _updateVoucherPrice: _updateVoucherPrice,
        _removeVoucherItem: _removeVoucherItem,
        _clearVoucherCart: _clearVoucherCart,
        _saveAndSendVoucher: _saveAndSendVoucher,
        loadVehicleCount: loadVehicleCount,
        loadBranchCount: loadBranchCount,
        loadGeneralCount: loadGeneralCount,
        _startBarcodeScanner: _startBarcodeScanner,
        _smartSearchInvItems: _smartSearchInvItems,
        _addToInvCart: _addToInvCart,
        _renderInvCart: _renderInvCart,
        _updateInvCartQty: _updateInvCartQty,
        _removeInvCartItem: _removeInvCartItem,
        _saveInvCount: _saveInvCount,
        _smartSearchDriver: _smartSearchDriver,
        _selectDriver: _selectDriver,
        _saveVehicleCount: _saveVehicleCount,
        _saveBranchCount: _saveBranchCount,
        _saveGeneralCount: _saveGeneralCount,
        loadSettlement: loadSettlement,
        _onSettlementRsChange: _onSettlementRsChange,
        _resetSettlement: _resetSettlement,
        _saveSettlement: _saveSettlement,
        _loadSettlementsList: _loadSettlementsList

    };
})();
window.RW_Warehouse = RW_Warehouse;
// ============================================================
// RW_Finance – الإدارة المالية والحسابات (نسخة نهائية مصححة)
// ============================================================
var RW_Finance = (function() {
    'use strict';

    // ==================== دوال مساعدة دفاعية ====================
    function _getEl(id) {
        try {
            if (typeof byId === 'function') return byId(id);
            return document.getElementById(id);
        } catch(e) { return null; }
    }

    function _safeHtml(el, html) {
        try {
            if (!el) return;
            if (typeof safeHTML === 'function') safeHTML(el, html);
            else el.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) { console.error('_safeHtml error:', e); }
    }

    function _showToast(msg, type) {
        try { if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast(msg, type); }
        catch(e) { console.error('Toast error:', e); }
    }

    function _showLoader(msg) {
        try { if (typeof showLoader === 'function') showLoader(msg || 'جاري التحميل...'); }
        catch(e) { console.error('Loader error:', e); }
    }

    function _hideLoader() {
        try { if (typeof hideLoader === 'function') hideLoader(); }
        catch(e) { console.error('HideLoader error:', e); }
    }

    function _fmtNum(n) {
        var num = parseFloat(n) || 0;
        return num.toFixed(2).replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ',');
    }

    function _esc(s) {
        return String(s == null ? '' : s)
            .replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;')
            .replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
    }

    function _escAttr(s) {
        return String(s == null ? '' : s).replace(/'/g, "\\'").replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
    }

    // ==================== تخزين البيانات المؤقت ====================
    var _cache = {
        loaded: false,
        accountsTree: [],
        accountsFlat: [],
        treasury: [],
        searchAccounts: [],
        receipts: [],
        payments: [],
        transfers: []
    };

    function _loadData(callback) {
        if (_cache.loaded) { if (callback) callback(); return; }
        
        if (RW_STATE.data._loadedAll) {
            _cache.accountsTree = RW_STATE.data._accountsTree || [];
            _cache.accountsFlat = RW_STATE.data._accountsFlat || [];
            _cache.treasury = RW_STATE.data._treasury || [];
            _cache.loaded = true;
            if (callback) callback();
            return;
        }
        
        _showLoader('جاري تحميل البيانات المالية...');
        var pending = 3;
        var done = function() { pending--; if (pending <= 0) { _cache.loaded = true; _hideLoader(); if (callback) callback(); } };
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { _cache.accountsTree = r || []; done(); })
            .withFailureHandler(function() { done(); }).getChartOfAccountsTree();
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { _cache.accountsFlat = r || []; done(); })
            .withFailureHandler(function() { done(); }).getChartOfAccountsFull();
        google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r) { _cache.treasury = r || []; done(); })
            .withFailureHandler(function() { done(); }).getTreasuryAccounts();
    }

    function _refreshCache() { _cache.loaded = false; }

    // ==================== العرض الرئيسي ====================
    function renderSubTab(subTab) {
        try {
            _loadData(function() {
                var container = _getEl('rw-page-container');
                if (!container) {
                    console.error('rw-page-container غير موجود');
                    return;
                }
                var tab = subTab || 'treasury';
                var tabs = [
                    { id: 'treasury', label: 'الخزائن والبنوك', icon: 'fa-vault' },
                    { id: 'accounts', label: 'دليل الحسابات', icon: 'fa-sitemap' },
                    { id: 'journal', label: 'قيود يومية', icon: 'fa-book' },
                    { id: 'receipts', label: 'سندات القبض', icon: 'fa-arrow-down' },
                    { id: 'payments', label: 'سندات الصرف', icon: 'fa-arrow-up' },
                    { id: 'transfers', label: 'التحويلات', icon: 'fa-right-left' },
                    { id: 'reports', label: 'التقارير المالية', icon: 'fa-chart-pie' }
                ];
                var html = '<div class="p-4" id="finance-root">';
                html += '<div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 border-b pb-3 mb-4">';
                for (var i = 0; i < tabs.length; i++) {
                    var activeClass = (tab === tabs[i].id) ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-200';
                    html += '<button onclick="RW_Finance.renderSubTab(\'' + tabs[i].id + '\')" class="px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold text-sm transition ' + activeClass + '">';
                    html += '<i class="fa-solid ' + tabs[i].icon + ' ml-1"></i>' + tabs[i].label;
                    html += '</button>';
                }
                html += '</div><div id="finance-content"></div></div>';
                _safeHtml(container, html);
                _renderCurrentTab(tab);
            });
        } catch(e) { console.error('renderSubTab error:', e); _showToast('خطأ في فتح التبويب', 'error'); }
    }

    function _renderCurrentTab(tab) {
        try {
            if (tab === 'treasury') _renderTreasury();
            else if (tab === 'accounts') _renderAccounts();
            else if (tab === 'journal') _renderJournal();
            else if (tab === 'receipts') _renderReceipts();
            else if (tab === 'payments') _renderPayments();
            else if (tab === 'transfers') _renderTransfers();
            else if (tab === 'reports') _renderReports();
        } catch(e) { console.error('_renderCurrentTab error:', e); }
    }

    // ==================== الخزائن والبنوك ====================
    function _renderTreasury() {
        var content = _getEl('finance-content');
        if (!content) return;
        var data = _cache.treasury || [];
        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4">';
        html += '<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">';
        html += '<h2 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-vault ml-2 text-blue-600"></i>الخزائن والبنوك</h2>';
        html += '<button onclick="RW_Finance._openTreasuryDialog()" class="bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl font-bold">إضافة خزينة / بنك</button>';
        html += '</div>';
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><input type="text" id="tr-search" placeholder="بحث..." class="w-full md:w-80 border rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm" oninput="RW_Finance._filterTreasury()"></div>';
        html += '<div id="tr-list" class="overflow-x-auto">' + _buildTreasuryTable(data) + '</div></div>';
        _safeHtml(content, html);
    }

    function _buildTreasuryTable(data) {
        if (!data.length) return '<div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد خزائن</div>';
        var html = '<table class="w-full text-sm border-collapse"><thead><tr class="bg-gray-50">';
        html += '<th class="p-2 border">الكود</th><th class="p-2 border">الاسم</th><th class="p-2 border">النوع</th><th class="p-2 border">الرصيد الافتتاحي</th>';
        html += '<th class="p-2 border">الرصيد الحالي</th><th class="p-2 border">الحالة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var t = data[i];
            var typeLabel = (t.type === 'Cash' || t.type === 'cash') ? 'خزينة' : 'بنك';
            var statusClass = t.is_active ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700' : 'bg-red-100 text-red-700';
            var statusText = t.is_active ? 'نشط' : 'غير نشط';
            html += '<tr class="border-t hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer" onclick="RW_Finance._editTreasury(\'' + _escAttr(t.account_code) + '\')">';
            html += '<td class="p-2">' + _esc(t.account_code) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 font-bold">' + _esc(t.account_name) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2">' + typeLabel + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2">' + _fmtNum(t.opening_balance) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 font-bold text-blue-600">' + _fmtNum(t.current_balance) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2"><span class="px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs ' + statusClass + '">' + statusText + '</span></td>';
            html += '</tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table>';
        return html;
    }

    function _filterTreasury() {
        var input = _getEl('tr-search');
        if (!input) return;
        var query = input.value.toLowerCase();
        var filtered = _cache.treasury.filter(function(t) {
            return (t.account_name && t.account_name.toLowerCase().indexOf(query) !== -1) ||
                   (t.account_code && t.account_code.toLowerCase().indexOf(query) !== -1);
        });
        var listDiv = _getEl('tr-list');
        if (listDiv) listDiv.innerHTML = _buildTreasuryTable(filtered);
    }

    function _openTreasuryDialog() {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'إضافة خزينة / بنك جديد',
            html: '<div class="text-right"><div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">الاسم *</label><input id="tr-name" class="swal2-input w-full"></div>' +
                  '<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">النوع</label><select id="tr-type" class="swal2-input"><option value="Cash">خزينة</option><option value="Bank">بنك</option></select></div>' +
                  '<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">الرصيد الافتتاحي</label><input id="tr-balance" type="number" step="0.01" value="0" class="swal2-input"></div></div>',
            showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'حفظ', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            preConfirm: function() {
                var name = document.getElementById('tr-name').value.trim();
                if (!name) { Swal.showValidationMessage('الاسم مطلوب'); return false; }
                return {
                    accountName: name,
                    type: document.getElementById('tr-type').value,
                    openingBalance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('tr-balance').value) || 0,
                    isActive: true
                };
            }
        }).then(function(res) {
            if (res.isConfirmed) {
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'saveTreasury',
                    payload: res.value,
                    onSuccess: function() { _showToast('تمت الإضافة', 'success'); _refreshCache(); renderSubTab('treasury'); },
                    onFailure: function(e) { _showToast('فشل: ' + (e.msg || e.message), 'error'); }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function _editTreasury(code) {
        var item = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < _cache.treasury.length; i++) {
            if (_cache.treasury[i].account_code === code) { item = _cache.treasury[i]; break; }
        }
        if (!item) { _showToast('الخزينة غير موجودة', 'error'); return; }
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تفاصيل الخزينة / البنك',
            html: '<div class="text-right">' +
                '<div class="bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded-lg mb-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-sm">' +
                '<div><span class="font-bold">الكود:</span> ' + _esc(item.account_code) + '</div>' +
                '<div><span class="font-bold">النوع:</span> ' + (item.type === 'Cash' ? 'خزينة' : 'بنك') + '</div>' +
                '<div><span class="font-bold">الرصيد الافتتاحي:</span> ' + _fmtNum(item.opening_balance) + ' EGP</div>' +
                '<div><span class="font-bold">الرصيد الحالي:</span> ' + _fmtNum(item.current_balance) + ' EGP</div>' +
                '<div><span class="font-bold">الحالة:</span> ' + (item.is_active ? 'نشط' : 'غير نشط') + '</div>' +
                '<div><span class="font-bold">ملاحظات:</span> ' + _esc(item.notes || '-') + '</div>' +
                '</div>' +
                '<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">الاسم *</label><input id="tr-name" class="swal2-input" value="' + _escAttr(item.account_name) + '"></div>' +
                '<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">النوع</label><select id="tr-type" class="swal2-input"><option value="Cash"' + (item.type === 'Cash' ? ' selected' : '') + '>خزينة</option><option value="Bank"' + (item.type === 'Bank' ? ' selected' : '') + '>بنك</option></select></div>' +
                '<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-sm font-bold mb-1">الرصيد الافتتاحي</label><input id="tr-balance" type="number" step="0.01" value="' + item.opening_balance + '" class="swal2-input"></div>' +
                '<div class="mb-4"><label class="flex items-center"><input id="tr-active" type="checkbox" ' + (item.is_active ? 'checked' : '') + '> نشط</label></div>' +
                '</div>',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'حفظ التعديلات',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            showDenyButton: true,
            denyButtonText: 'حذف الخزينة',
            denyButtonColor: '#ef4444',
            preConfirm: function() {
                var name = document.getElementById('tr-name').value.trim();
                if (!name) { Swal.showValidationMessage('الاسم مطلوب'); return false; }
                return {
                    accountId: code,
                    accountName: name,
                    type: document.getElementById('tr-type').value,
                    openingBalance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('tr-balance').value) || 0,
                    currentBalance: parseFloat(document.getElementById('tr-balance').value) || 0,
                    isActive: document.getElementById('tr-active').checked
                };
            }
        }).then(function(res) {
            if (res.isConfirmed) {
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'saveTreasury',
                    payload: res.value,
                    onSuccess: function() { _showToast('تم التعديل', 'success'); _refreshCache(); renderSubTab('treasury'); },
                    onFailure: function(e) { _showToast('فشل: ' + (e.msg || e.message), 'error'); }
                });
            } else if (res.isDenied) {
                Swal.fire({
                    title: 'تأكيد الحذف', text: 'حذف "' + item.account_name + '"؟', icon: 'warning',
                    showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#ef4444', confirmButtonText: 'حذف', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
                }).then(function(delRes) {
                    if (delRes.isConfirmed) {
                        enqueueSync({
                            type: 'deleteTreasury',
                            payload: code,
                            onSuccess: function() { _showToast('تم الحذف', 'success'); _refreshCache(); renderSubTab('treasury'); },
                            onFailure: function(e) { _showToast('فشل: ' + (e.msg || e.message), 'error'); }
                        });
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function _deleteTreasury(code, name) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف', text: 'حذف "' + name + '"؟', icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'حذف', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(res) {
            if (res.isConfirmed) {
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'deleteTreasury',
                    payload: code,
                    onSuccess: function() { _showToast('تم الحذف', 'success'); _refreshCache(); renderSubTab('treasury'); },
                    onFailure: function(e) { _showToast('فشل: ' + (e.msg || e.message), 'error'); }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    // ==================== دليل الحسابات ====================
    function _renderAccounts() {
        var content = _getEl('finance-content');
        if (!content) return;
        var tree = _cache.accountsTree || [];
        var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4">';
        html += '<div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">';
        html += '<h2 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-sitemap ml-2 text-indigo-600"></i>دليل الحسابات</h2>';
        html += '<div><button onclick="RW_Finance._seedAccounts()" class="bg-amber-500 text-white px-3 py-2 rounded-lg ml-2">تهيئة افتراضية</button>';
        html += '<button onclick="RW_Finance._openAccountDialog()" class="bg-indigo-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg">حساب جديد</button></div></div>';
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><input type="text" id="acc-search" placeholder="بحث..." class="w-full md:w-80 border rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm" oninput="RW_Finance._filterAccounts()"></div>';
        html += '<div id="acc-tree" class="overflow-auto">' + _buildAccountTree(tree, 0) + '</div></div>';
        _safeHtml(content, html);
    }

    function _buildAccountTree(nodes, level) {
        if (!nodes || !nodes.length) return '<div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد حسابات</div>';
        var html = '';
        for (var i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
            var node = nodes[i];
            var margin = level * 20;
            var hasChildren = node.children && node.children.length > 0;
            var chevron = hasChildren ? '<i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-down text-gray-400 cursor-pointer text-xs ml-1" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); RW_Finance._toggleTreeNode(this)"></i>' : '<span class="inline-block w-4"></span>';
            html += '<div class="border-b border-gray-100 py-2" style="margin-right:' + margin + 'px">';
            html += '<div class="flex items-center justify-between hover:bg-gray-50 cursor-pointer rounded px-2 py-1" onclick="RW_Finance._openAccountDialog(\'' + _escAttr(node.id) + '\')">';
            html += '<div class="flex items-center"><span class="ml-2">' + chevron + '</span>';
            html += '<span class="font-bold text-gray-800">' + _esc(node.name) + '</span>';
            html += '<span class="text-xs text-gray-400 mr-2">(' + _esc(node.id) + ')</span>';
            html += '<span class="text-xs bg-gray-100 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full mr-1">' + _esc(node.type || '') + '</span></div>';
            html += '</div>';
            if (hasChildren) {
                html += '<div class="children-container" data-parent="' + node.id + '">' + _buildAccountTree(node.children, level + 1) + '</div>';
            }
            html += '</div>';
        }
        return html;
    }

    function _toggleTreeNode(btn) {
        var parentDiv = btn.parentNode.parentNode;
        var childrenDiv = parentDiv.querySelector('.children-container');
        if (childrenDiv) {
            var isHidden = childrenDiv.style.display === 'none';
            childrenDiv.style.display = isHidden ? 'block' : 'none';
            btn.classList.toggle('fa-chevron-down', !isHidden);
            btn.classList.toggle('fa-chevron-left', isHidden);
        }
    }

    function _filterAccounts() {
        var input = _getEl('acc-search');
        if (!input) return;
        var query = input.value.toLowerCase();
        var filtered = _filterTree(_cache.accountsTree, query);
        var treeDiv = _getEl('acc-tree');
        if (treeDiv) treeDiv.innerHTML = _buildAccountTree(filtered, 0);
    }

    function _filterTree(nodes, query) {
        var result = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
            var node = nodes[i];
            var match = (node.name && node.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(query) !== -1) ||
                        (node.id && node.id.toLowerCase().indexOf(query) !== -1);
            var childFiltered = node.children ? _filterTree(node.children, query) : [];
            if (match || childFiltered.length > 0) {
                var newNode = { id: node.id, name: node.name, type: node.type, parent: node.parent, balance: node.balance, children: childFiltered };
                result.push(newNode);
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

    function _openAccountDialog(editId, parentId) {
        var isEdit = !!editId;
        var item = null;
        if (isEdit) {
            for (var i = 0; i < _cache.accountsFlat.length; i++) {
                if (_cache.accountsFlat[i].account_code === editId) { item = _cache.accountsFlat[i]; break; }
            }
        }
        var title = isEdit ? 'تفاصيل الحساب: ' + _esc(item.account_name) : (parentId ? 'إضافة حساب فرعي' : 'إضافة حساب جديد');
        var html = '<div class="text-right">';
        if (isEdit) {
            html += '<div class="bg-gray-50 p-3 rounded-lg mb-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-sm">';
            html += '<div><span class="font-bold">الكود:</span> ' + _esc(item.account_code) + '</div>';
            html += '<div><span class="font-bold">النوع:</span> ' + _esc(item.account_type) + '</div>';
            html += '<div><span class="font-bold">الأب:</span> ' + _esc(item.parent_account_id || 'لا يوجد') + '</div>';
            html += '<div><span class="font-bold">الرصيد الطبيعي:</span> ' + _esc(item.normal_balance || '') + '</div>';
            html += '<div><span class="font-bold">الحالة:</span> ' + (item.is_active !== false ? 'نشط' : 'غير نشط') + '</div>';
            html += '<div><span class="font-bold">ملاحظات:</span> ' + _esc(item.notes || '-') + '</div>';
            html += '</div>';
        }
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><label class="block text-sm font-bold">كود الحساب</label><input id="acc-code" class="swal2-input" value="' + (isEdit ? _escAttr(item.account_code) : '') + '" readonly></div>';
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><label class="block text-sm font-bold">اسم الحساب *</label><input id="acc-name" class="swal2-input" value="' + (isEdit ? _escAttr(item.account_name) : '') + '"></div>';
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><label class="block text-sm font-bold">النوع</label><select id="acc-type" class="swal2-input">';
        var types = [
            { val: 'asset', label: 'أصول' }, { val: 'liability', label: 'خصوم' },
            { val: 'equity', label: 'حقوق ملكية' }, { val: 'revenue', label: 'إيرادات' },
            { val: 'expense', label: 'مصروفات' }
        ];
        for (var t = 0; t < types.length; t++) {
            var sel = (isEdit && item.account_type === types[t].val) ? ' selected' : '';
            html += '<option value="' + types[t].val + '"' + sel + '>' + types[t].label + '</option>';
        }
        html += '</select></div>';
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><label class="block text-sm font-bold">الحساب الأب</label><select id="acc-parent" class="swal2-input"><option value="">لا يوجد</option>';
        for (var p = 0; p < _cache.accountsFlat.length; p++) {
            var acc = _cache.accountsFlat[p];
            if (isEdit && acc.account_code === editId) continue;
            var parSel = (isEdit && item.parent_account_id === acc.account_code) ? ' selected' : '';
            if (!isEdit && parentId === acc.account_code) parSel = ' selected';
            html += '<option value="' + _escAttr(acc.account_code) + '"' + parSel + '>' + _esc(acc.account_name) + ' (' + _esc(acc.account_code) + ')</option>';
        }
        html += '</select></div>';
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><label class="block text-sm font-bold">الرصيد الطبيعي</label><select id="acc-normal" class="swal2-input">';
        html += '<option value="debit"' + (!isEdit || item.normal_balance === 'debit' ? ' selected' : '') + '>مدين</option>';
        html += '<option value="credit"' + (isEdit && item.normal_balance === 'credit' ? ' selected' : '') + '>دائن</option>';
        html += '</select></div>';
        html += '<div class="mb-3"><label class="flex items-center"><input id="acc-active" type="checkbox" ' + (!isEdit || item.is_active !== false ? 'checked' : '') + '> نشط</label></div>';
        html += '<div><label class="block text-sm font-bold">ملاحظات</label><textarea id="acc-notes" rows="2" class="swal2-textarea">' + (isEdit ? _esc(item.notes || '') : '') + '</textarea></div></div>';

        var confirmButtonText = isEdit ? 'حفظ التعديلات' : 'إضافة الحساب';
        var showDeleteButton = isEdit;
        var showAddSubButton = isEdit;

        Swal.fire({
            title: title, html: html, width: '600px', showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: confirmButtonText, cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء',
            showDenyButton: showDeleteButton,
            denyButtonText: '<i class="fa-solid fa-trash ml-1"></i> حذف',
            denyButtonColor: '#ef4444',
            didOpen: function() {
                if (!isEdit && !parentId) {
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(code) {
                        var codeInput = document.getElementById('acc-code');
                        if (codeInput) codeInput.value = code;
                    }).getNextAccountCode('');
                }
                if (parentId) {
                    google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(code) {
                        var codeInput = document.getElementById('acc-code');
                        if (codeInput) codeInput.value = code;
                    }).getNextAccountCode(parentId);
                }
            },
            preConfirm: function() {
                var name = document.getElementById('acc-name').value.trim();
                if (!name) { Swal.showValidationMessage('اسم الحساب مطلوب'); return false; }
                return {
                    accountId: document.getElementById('acc-code').value.trim(),
                    accountName: name,
                    accountType: document.getElementById('acc-type').value,
                    parentAccount: document.getElementById('acc-parent').value || null,
                    normalBalance: document.getElementById('acc-normal').value,
                    isActive: document.getElementById('acc-active').checked,
                    notes: document.getElementById('acc-notes').value.trim()
                };
            }
        }).then(function(res) {
            if (res.isConfirmed) {
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'saveAccount',
                    payload: res.value,
                    onSuccess: function() { _showToast('تم حفظ الحساب', 'success'); _refreshCache(); renderSubTab('accounts'); },
                    onFailure: function(e) { _showToast('فشل: ' + (e.msg || e.message), 'error'); }
                });
            } else if (res.isDenied) {
                Swal.fire({
                    title: 'تأكيد الحذف', text: 'حذف "' + item.account_name + '"؟', icon: 'warning',
                    showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#ef4444', confirmButtonText: 'حذف', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
                }).then(function(delRes) {
                    if (delRes.isConfirmed) {
                        enqueueSync({
                            type: 'deleteAccount',
                            payload: editId,
                            onSuccess: function() { _showToast('تم الحذف', 'success'); _refreshCache(); renderSubTab('accounts'); },
                            onFailure: function(e) { _showToast('فشل: ' + (e.msg || e.message), 'error'); }
                        });
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function _addSubAccount(parentId) {
        _openAccountDialog(null, parentId);
    }

    function _deleteAccount(code, name) {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تأكيد الحذف', text: 'حذف "' + name + '"؟', icon: 'warning',
            showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonText: 'حذف', cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(res) {
            if (res.isConfirmed) {
                enqueueSync({
                    type: 'deleteAccount',
                    payload: code,
                    onSuccess: function() { _showToast('تم الحذف', 'success'); _refreshCache(); renderSubTab('accounts'); },
                    onFailure: function(e) { _showToast('فشل: ' + (e.msg || e.message), 'error'); }
                });
            }
        });
    }

    function _seedAccounts() {
        Swal.fire({
            title: 'تهيئة الحسابات',
            text: 'سيتم إنشاء حسابات افتراضية',
            icon: 'question',
            showCancelButton: true,
            confirmButtonText: 'تهيئة',
            cancelButtonText: 'إلغاء'
        }).then(function(res) {
            if (res.isConfirmed) {
                _showLoader('جاري التهيئة...');
                google.script.run
                    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
                        // ✅ تمت التهيئة بنجاح على الخادم.
                        // الآن نجبر إعادة تحميل البيانات من الخادم.
                        _cache.loaded = false;
                        _cache.accountsFlat = [];
                        _cache.accountsTree = [];
                        
                        // نعرض رسالة الخادم للمستخدم
                        var msg = result && result.msg ? result.msg : 'تمت التهيئة';
                        _showToast(msg, 'success');
                        
                        // نطلب تحديث الشجرة الآن
                        _showLoader('جاري تحديث الشجرة...');
                        _loadData(function() {
                            _hideLoader();
                            // الآن نعرض التبويب بالبيانات الجديدة
                            renderSubTab('accounts');
                        });
                    })
                    .withFailureHandler(function(e) {
                        _hideLoader();
                        _showToast('فشل: ' + e.message, 'error');
                    })
                    .seedChartOfAccounts();
            }
        });
    }

    // ==================== سندات القبض (مُحدَّثة مع طباعة) ====================
    function _renderReceipts() {
        var content = _getEl('finance-content');
        if (!content) return;
        content.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 text-center py-8">جاري تحميل سندات القبض...</div>';
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
                _cache.receipts = data || [];
                var html = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4"><div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-4"><h2 class="text-xl font-bold"><i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-down ml-2 text-green-600"></i>سندات القبض</h2><button onclick="RW_Finance._newReceipt()" class="bg-green-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl">سند قبض جديد</button></div>';
                html += '<div id="receipts-list">' + _buildReceiptsTable(_cache.receipts) + '</div></div>';
                _safeHtml(content, html);
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function() { _showToast('فشل تحميل سندات القبض', 'error'); })
            .getCashReceipts({});
    }

    function _buildReceiptsTable(data) {
        if (!data.length) return '<div class="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">لا توجد سندات قبض</div>';
        var html = '<table class="w-full text-sm border-collapse"><thead><tr class="bg-gray-50"><th class="p-2 border">الكود</th><th class="p-2 border">التاريخ</th><th class="p-2 border">الخزينة</th><th class="p-2 border">المبلغ</th><th class="p-2 border">المرجع</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">طباعة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var r = data[i];
            var ref = r.reference || r.voucher_code || '';
            html += '<tr class="border-t"><td class="p-2">' + _esc(r.voucher_code || '') + '</td><td class="p-2">' + _esc(r.voucher_date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2">' + _esc(r.treasury_name || r.cashId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 font-bold text-green-600">' + _fmtNum(r.amount) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2">' + _esc(ref) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 text-center"><button onclick="RW_Finance._printReceipt(\'' + _escAttr(ref) + '\')" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800" title="طباعة"><i class="fa-solid fa-print"></i></button></td></tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table>';
        return html;
    }

            })

    }

    function _buildPaymentsTable(data) {

        var html = '<table class="w-full text-sm border-collapse"><thead><tr class="bg-gray-50"><th class="p-2 border">الكود</th><th class="p-2 border">التاريخ</th><th class="p-2 border">الخزينة</th><th class="p-2 border">المبلغ</th><th class="p-2 border">المرجع</th><th class="p-2 border text-center">طباعة</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var p = data[i];
            var ref = p.reference || p.voucher_code || '';
            html += '<tr class="border-t"><td class="p-2">' + _esc(p.voucher_code || '') + '</td><td class="p-2">' + _esc(p.voucher_date || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2">' + _esc(p.treasury_name || p.cashId || '') + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 font-bold text-red-600">' + _fmtNum(p.amount) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2">' + _esc(ref) + '</td>';
            html += '<td class="p-2 text-center"><button onclick="RW_Finance._printPayment(\'' + _escAttr(ref) + '\')" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800" title="طباعة"><i class="fa-solid fa-print"></i></button></td></tr>';
        }
        html += '</tbody></table>';
        return html;
    }



    // ==================== التحويلات (مُحدَّثة مع طباعة) ====================
    function _renderTransfers() {
        var content = _getEl('finance-content');
        if (!content) return;
        content.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-sm border p-4 text-center py-8">جاري تحميل التحويلات...</div>';
        google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
